

।।
।।

nārāyaṇaṃ nikhilapūrṇaguṇaikadehaṃ nirdoṣamāpyatamamapyakhilaiḥ suvākyaiḥ ।
asyodbhavādidamaśeṣaviśeṣato api vandyaṃ sadā priyatamaṃ mama sannamāmi ।।

tameva śāstraprabhavaṃ praṇamya jagadgurūṇāṃ gurumañjasaiva ।
viśeṣato me paramākhyavidyāvyākhyāṃ karomyanvapi cāhameva ।।
prādurbhūto harirvyāso viriñcabhavapūrvakaiḥ ।
arthitaḥ paravidyākhyaṃ cakre śāstramanuttamam ।।
gururgurūṇāṃ prabhavaḥ śāstrāṇāṃ bādarāyaṇaḥ ।
yatastaduditaṃ mānamajādibhyastadarthataḥ ।।
vaktṛśrotṛprasaktīnāṃ yadāptiranukūlatā ।
āptavākyatayā tena śrutimūlatayā tathā ।।
yuktimūlatayā caiva prāmāṇyaṃ trividhaṃ mahat ।
dṛśyate brahmasūtrāṇāmekadhānyatra sarvaśaḥ ।।
ato naitādṛśaṃ kiñcit pramāṇatamamiṣyate ।
svayaṃ kṛtāpi tadvayākhyā kriyate spaṣṭatārthataḥ ।।
tatra tārāthamūlatvaṃ sarvaśaśastrasya ceṣyate ।
sarvatrānugatatvena pṛthagoṅkriyate akhilaiḥ ।।
otatvavācī hyoṅkāro vaktayasau tadguṇotatām ।
sa eva brahmaśabdārtho nārāyaṇapadoditaḥ ।।
sa eva bhargaśabdārtho vyāhṛtīnāṃ ca bhūmataḥ ।
bhāvanāccaiva sutvācca so ayaṃ puruṣa ityapi ।।
sa eva sarvavedārtho jijñāsyo ayaṃ vidhīyate ।
jñānī priyatamo ato me taṃ vidvāneva cāmṛtaḥ ।।
vṛṇute yaṃ tena labhya ityādyuktibalena hi ।
jijñāsotthajñānajāt tatprasādādeva mucyate ।।
dravyaṃ karma ca kālaśca svabhāvo jīva eva ca ।
yadanugrahataḥ santi na santi yadupekṣayā ।।
narte tvat kriyate kiñcidityāderna hariṃ vinā ।
jñānasvabhāvato api syānmuktiḥ kasyāpi hi kvacit ।।
ajñānāṃ jñānado viṣṇurjñānināṃ mokṣadaśca saḥ ।
ānandadaśca muktānāṃ sa evaiko janārdanaḥ ।।
ityukterbandhamithyātvaṃ naiva muktirapekṣate ।
mithyātvamapi bandhasya na pratyakṣavirodhataḥ ।।
mithyātvaṃ yadi duḥkhādestadvākyāgrato bhavet ।
mithyāyāḥ sādhakatvaṃ ca na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ ।।
tacca mithyāpramāṇena satā vā sādhyate tvayā ।
satā ced dvaitasiddhiḥ syānna siddhaṃ cānyasādhanam ।।
sādhakatvaṃ satastena sākṣiṇā siddhimicchatā ।
svīkṛtaṃ hyaviśeṣasya sādhyā sādhakatā punaḥ ।।
taccāviśeṣamānena sādhyamityanavasthitiḥ ।
anaṅgīkurvatāṃ viśvasatyatāṃ tanna vāditā ।।
tasmād vyavahṛtiḥ sarvā satyetyeva vyavasthitā ।
vyāvahārikametasmāt satyamityeva cāgatam ।।
vyavahārasataścāpi sādhakatvaṃ tu pūrvavat ।
sattraividhyaṃ ca mānena siddhayet keneti pṛcchyate ।।
tasyāpyuktaprakāreṇa naiva siddhiḥ kathañcana ।
vailakṣaṇyaṃ sadasatorapyetena niṣidhyate ।।
vailakṣaṇyaṃ sataścāpi svayaṃ sadbhedavādinaḥ ।
asataścāpi viśvasya tenāniṣyaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ।।
yadyucyate api sarvasmāditi sadbhedasaṃsthitiḥ ।
sanmātratvaṃ brahmaṇo api tasmāt tadapi no bhavet ।।
jñānabādhyatvamapi tu na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ ।
vijñātasyānyathā samyag vijñānaṃ hyeva tanmatam ।।
asadvilakṣaṇajñaptyai jñātavyamasadeva hi ।
tasmādasatpratītiśca kathaṃ tena nivāryate ।।
anyathātvamasat tasmād bhrāntāveva pratīyate ।
sattvasyāsata evaṃ hi svīkāryaiva pratītatā ।।
tasyānirvacanīyatve syādeva hyanavasthitiḥ ।
nirviśeṣe svayaṃ bhāte kimajñānāvṛtaṃ bhavetaḥ ।।
mithyāviśeṣo apyajñānasiddhimeva hyapekṣate ।
nacāavaraṇamajñānamasatye tena ceṣyate ।।
aprakāśasvarūpatvājjaḍe ajñānaṃ na manyate ।
ajñānābhāvataḥ śāstraṃ sarvaṃ vyarthībhaviṣyati ।।
ajñānasya ca mithyātvamajñānāditi kalpane ।
anavasthitistathāca syādanyonyāśrayatāthavā ।।
svabhāvājñānavādasya nirdoṣatvānna tad bhavet ।
avidyādurghaṭatvaṃ cet syādātmāpi hi tādṛśaḥ ।।
ato adhikāriviṣayaphalayogādivarjitam ।
anantadoṣaduṣṭaṃ ca heyaṃ māyāmataṃ śubhaiḥ ।।
satyatvāt tena duḥkhādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ ।
na brahmatāṃ vaded vedo jīvasya hi kathañcana ।।
yajamānaprastaratvaṃ yathā nārthaḥ śruterbhavet ।
brahmatvamapi jīvasya pratyakṣasyāviśeṣataḥ ।।
sārvajñyādiguṇaṃ jīvād bhinnaṃ jñāpayati śrutiḥ ।
īśaṃ tāmupajīvyaiva vartate hyaikyavādinī ।।
upajīvyavirodhena nāsyāstanmānatā bhavet ।
svātantrye ca viśiṣṭatve sthānamattyaikyayorapi ।।
sādṛśye caikyavāk samyak sāvakāśā yatheṣyataḥ ।
avakāśojkhitā bhedaśrutirnātibalā katham ।।
ajñānāsambhavādeva mithyābhedo nirākṛtaḥ ।
ato yathārthabandhasya vinā viṣṇuprasādataḥ ।।
anivṛttestadarthaṃ hi jijñāsātra vidhīyate ।
yathā dṛṣṭayā prasannaḥ san rājā bandhāpanodakṛt ।।
evaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān kuryād bandhavibhedanam ।
kāryatā ca na kācit syādiṣṭasādhanatāṃ vinā ।।
kāryaṃ na hi kriyāvyāpyaṃ niṣiddhasya samatvataḥ ।
na bhaviṣyatkriyā kāryaṃ srakṣyatīśa iti hyapi ।।
kāryaṃ syānnaiva cākartumaśakyaṃ kāryamiṣyate ।
sāmyādeva niṣiddhasya tadiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ tathā ।।
kāryaṃ sādhanamiṣṭasya bhagavāniṣṭadevatā ।
mukhyeṣyaṃ vā sumanasāṃ preyastaditi ca śrutiḥ ।।
prāṇabuddhimanaḥkhātmadehāpatyadhanādayaḥ ।
yatsamparkāt priyā āsaṃstataḥ ko nvaparaḥ priyaḥ ।।
ityādivākyairākāṅkṣāsannidhiryogyatā yataḥ ।
asminneva samastasyetīṣye vyutpattiriṣyate ।।
attyapūpāṃstava bhrātetyādāvāvāpato api ca ।
udvāpād vartamānatvādākāṅkṣādibalādapi ।।
bālo vyutpattimapyeti nānayetyādivākyataḥ ।
ānīyamānadṛṣṭayaiva vyutpatteḥ sambhave sati ।।
eṣyadānayanāyāyaṃ kuta eva pratīkṣate ।
vyutpanno vartamāne tu kriyāśabde bhaviṣyati ।।
punardṛṣṭyaiva śabdaśrut paścāt vyutpattimeṣyati ।
vartamānamatītaṃ ca bhaviṣyaditi ca kramāt ।।
ākāṅkṣādiyutaṃ yasmād vidhervyutpādanaṃ kutaḥ ।
dṛṣṭyā jñātapadārthasya padākāṅkṣā bhaviṣyati ।।
vyutpattiḥ prathamā tasmād vatarmāne gate tataḥ ।
iṣṭamākāṅkṣate sarvo na pravṛttimapekṣate ।।
aparokṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā jñānamiṣṭasya sādhanam ।
kvāpi ceṣyā tadarthā syādattirhi rasavittaye ।।
vākyārthajñānamātreṇa kvacidiṣṭaṃ bhavedapi ।
na ca srukasruvavahnayādāvatātparyaṃ śruterbhavet ।।
yatkiñcitkaraṇarasyāpi yajñataivānyathā bhavet ।
tasmādupāsanārthaṃ ca svārthe tātparyavad bhavet ।।
iti śabdonnaye agnāvityunnīte smṛtirbhavet ।
itiśabdavyapetāni hyapi santi vacāṃsyalam ।।
ātmānamevetyādīni yoge agnāvapi tat samam ।
ekavākyatvayoge tu vedasyāpi hyaśeṣataḥ ।।
vākyabhedo na yuktaḥ syād yogaśca syānmahāphale ।
iti brūyāditi vaco gatamagnau samīpagam ।।
kalpanāgauravaṃ cet syāt pṛthak tātparyasambhave ।
kalpanāgauravādeva padārthā na syureva hi ।।
pramāṇāvagatatvaṃ cet tātparyāṇaśaṃ tathaiva hi ।
tasmāt padārthe vākyārthe tātparyamubhayatra ca ।।
pṛthageva ca vākyatvaṃ pṛthaganvayato bhavet ।
avāntaratvād vākyānāṃ vākyabhedo na dūṣaṇam ।।
aṅgīkṛtatvādapi taiḥ padārthānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।
kriyāpadenānvayasya vākyabhedāddhi dūṣaṇam ।।
pratyakṣādivirodhe ato gauṇārthasyāpi sambhavāt ।
atātparyaṃ padārthe api na kalpyamavirodhataḥ ।।
ato jñānaphalānyeva karmāṇi jñānameva hi ।
mukhyaprasādadaṃ viṣṇorjijñāsāyāśca tad bhavet ।।
kartavyā tena jijñāsā śrutiprāmāṇyayogataḥ ।
pratyakṣavacca prāmāṇyaṃ svata evāgamasya hi ।।
anavasthānyathā hi syādaprāmāṇyaṃ tathānyataḥ ।
mithyājñaptipralambhādestena vedavirodhi yat ।।
na mānamapi vedānāmaṅgīkāryā hi nityatā ।
na hi dharmādisiddhiḥ syānnityavākyaṃ vinā kvacit ।।
avipralambhastajjñānaṃ tatkṛtatvādayo api ca ।
kalpyā gauravadoṣeṇa puṃvākyaṃ jñāpakaṃ na tat ।।
pratyakṣaḥ kasyacid dharmo vastutvāditi codite ।
na buddho dharmadarśī syāt puṃstvādityanumāhatiḥ ।।
adharmavādino vākyamaprayojanameva hi ।
dharmābhāvo api no tena pratyakṣāvagato bhavet ।।
ataḥ saṃśayasampattau vākyaṃ pratyakṣavat pramā ।
śaktiścaivānvite svārthe śabdānāmanubhūyate ।।
ato anvitābhidhāyitvaṃ gauravaṃ kalpane anyathā ।
nacāśakyābhidhāyitvaṃ pravṛttiśca dvidhānyathā ।।
etat sarvaṃ tarkaśāstre brahmatarke hi vistarāt ।
uktaṃ vidyāpṛthaktavāttu saṅkṣepeṇātra sūcitam ।।
pramāṇanyāyasacchikṣā kriyate tarkaśāstrataḥ ।
mānanyāyaistu tatsiddhaimīmāṃsā meyaśodhanam ।।
brahmatarkaṃ ca bhagavān sa eva kṛtavān prabhuḥ ।
pañcāśatkoṭivistārānnārāyaṇatanau kṛtāt ।।
uddhṛtya pañcasāhasraṃ kṛtavān bādarāyaṇaḥ ।
atastadarthaṃ saṅkṣepādata ityabhyasūcayat ।।
yato anubhavataḥ sarvaṃ siddhametadato api ca ।
devaiśca durgamārtheṣu vyāpṛto nātivistṛtim ।।
cakāraitā hyavajñeyā yuktayaḥ pratipakṣagāḥ ।
pratyakṣekṣākṣamaḥ pakṣaṃ kamevātrābhivīkṣate ।।
tasmādakṣamapakṣatvānmokṣaśāstre abhyupekṣitaḥ ।
svayaṃ bhagavatā viṣṇurbrahmetyetat puroditam ।।
sa viṣṇurāha hīyante devaśāstrasya tena hi ।
ādyantaṃ devaśāstrasya svayaṃ bhagavatā kṛtam ।।
madhyaṃ tadājñayā pailaśeṣābhyāṃ kṛtamañjasā ।
atastatraiva viṣṇutvasiddherbrahmetyasūcayat ।।
doṣāracchidraśabdānāṃ paryāyatvaṃ yatastataḥ ।
guṇā nārā iti jñeyastadvān nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
brahmaśabdo api hi guṇapūrtimeva vadatyayam ।
ato nārāyaṇasyaiva jijñāsātra vidhīyate ।।
siddhatvād brahmaśabdasya viṣṇau spaṣṭatayā śrutau ।
ambhasyapāra ityukto nārāyaṇapaderitaḥ ।।
āpo nārā iti hyāha sa evāpsvantarīritaḥ ।
kāmato vidhirudrādipadadātṛyā svayaṃ śriyā ।।
yonitvenātmano viṣṇostiṣṭhantītyuditasya ca ।
yasmin devā adhītyuktavā samudraṃ sthānameva ca ।।
nāma cākṣaramityeva ṛca ityuditaṃ tu yat ।
yataḥ prasūtetyuktavā ca tadeva brahma cābravīt ।।
antaḥsamudragaṃ viśvaprasūteḥ kāraṇaṭha tu yat ।
sūktopaniṣadādyuktaṃ janmādyasyeti lakṣyate ।।
sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhāro niyatirjñānamāvṛtiḥ ।
bandhamokṣāvapi hyāsu śrutiṣūktā hareḥ sadā ।।
yaṃ nāmāni viśantyaddhā yo devānāmiti hyapi ।
śruternāmāni sarvāṇi viṣṇoreva yatastataḥ ।।
ato na mukhyato nāma tadanyasya hi kasyacit ।
guṇāḥ śrutā iti hyasmānna doṣo arthaḥ śruterbhavet ।।
prītyā mokṣaparatvācca tātparyaṃ naiva dūṣaṇe ।
sarveṣāmapi vākyānāṃ mahātātparyamatra hi ।।
tadvirodhe na mānatvaṃ phalaṃ muktirhi vākyataḥ ।
na purāṇādimānatvaṃ viruddhārthe śruterbhavet ।।
darśanāntaramūlatvānmohārthaṃ cājñayā hareḥ ।
na sarvanāmatānyeṣāṃ śrutāvuktā hi kutracit ।।
adoṣavacanāccaiva niyamena hareḥ śrutau ।
ajñānaṃ pāratantryaṃ ca praḷaye abhāva eva ca ।।
aśaktiścoditānyeṣāṃ sarveṣāmapi ca śrutau ।
janmādyasyeti tenaitad viṣṇoreva svalakṣaṇam ।।
asyodbhavādihetutvaṃ sākṣādeva svalakṣaṇam ।
kṛṣṇaddhayānacchalenaiva svayaṃ bhāgavate abravīt ।।
ato jīvaikyamapi sa nirācakre jagadguruḥ ।
na hi janmādihetutvaṃ jīvasya jagato bhavet ।।
hitākriyādidoṣaṃ ca vakṣyatyeva svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।
nirguṇatvaṃ ca tenaiva niṣiddhaṃ prabhuṇā svayam ।।
bhedenaiva tu mukhyārthasambhave lakṣaṇā kutaḥ ।
kathaṃ nityaguṇasyāsya syādaikyaṃ guṇahānataḥ ।।
sadaiva guṇavattve asya bhinnaṃ syānnirguṇaṃ sadā ।
na ca mithyāguṇatvaṃ syādanirvācyasya dūṣaṇāt ।।
nirguṇatvaṃ tadā ca syādāsuratvaṃ nacānyathā ।
lakṣyalakṣaṇayorbhedo abhedo vā yadi vobhayam ।।
iti pṛṣṭe tadaikyasya gatireva na vidyate ।
aikyābhede na śāstreṇa jñeyaṃ tat svaprakāśataḥ ।।
bhede mithyātvato bhedasatyatvaṃ syād balādapi ।
bhedābhedau yadi tadā syādeva hyanavasthitiḥ ।।
svanirvāhakatā cet syād bāhyaṃ bāhakamityapi ।
paryāyo bhedavān vā syādanavasthobhayatra ca ।।
satyajñānādike apyeva na vyāvṛttyā prayojanam ।
vyāvṛttasyāviśeṣatve tadakhaṇḍaṃ ca khaṇḍitam ।
nirviśeṣatvametena mūko ahamitivad bhavet ।।
abhinne api viśeṣo ayaṃ balādāpatati hyataḥ ।
viśeṣatadvatoścaiva svanirvāhakatā bhavet ।।
bhedahīne tvaparyāyaśabdāntaraniyāmakaḥ ।
viśeṣo nāma kathitaḥ so asti vastuṣvaśeṣataḥ ।।
viśeṣāste apyanantāśca parasparaviśeṣiṇaḥ ।
svanirvāhakatāyuktāḥ santi vastuṣvaśeṣataḥ ।।
ato anantaguṇaṃ brahma nirbhedamapi bhaṇyate ।
evaṃ dharmāniti śrutyā tadabhedo apyudīryate ।।
śaivādyāgamasamprāptadṛṣṭagena phalena tu ।
tadvākyopamayānyacca pramāṇatve anumīyate ।।
īśavākyatvata iti cet tadgavyabhicāriṇā ।
aprāmāṇyānumā ca syānna pṛthak cānumeśvare ।।
puṃstvahetubalādeva pūrvoktenaiva vartmanā ।
śāstrayonitvametena kāraṇasya balād bhavet ।।
nāvedavinna tarkeṇa matirityādivākyataḥ ।
tarko jñāpayituṃ śakto neśitāraṃ kathañcana ।।
vanakṛttvādirūpeṇa pakṣabhūtasya ceśituḥ ।
kiñcijjñānaṃ hi puṃstvena śakyaṃ sādhayituṃ sukham ।।
vṛkṣakṛnnākhilaṃ vṛkṣaṃ vetti puṃstvāddhi caitravat ।
ityādyanumayā spardhi nānumānaṃ pareśituḥ ।
śaktaṃ vijñāpane cātiprasaṅgo anumayedṛśā ।।
vastutvāt turagaḥ śṛṅgī puṣpavat khaṃ sutairyutā ।
citriṇī ca rasaḥ ṣaṣṭho rasatvāt sottaro bhavet ।
upakramādiliṅgebhyo nānyāsyādanumā tataḥ ।।
ta evānvayanāmānastaiḥ samyak pravicārite ।
mukhyārtho bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvaśāstrasya nāparaḥ ।।
īkṣaṇīyatvato viṣṇurvācya eva nacānyathā ।
lakṣyatvaṃ kvāpi dṛṣṭaṃ hi kiṃ tadityanavasthitiḥ ।।
mādhuryādiviśeṣāśca tacchabdairuditāḥ sadā ।
vākyārtho api hi vākyārthaśabdenaivodito bhavet ।।
nāvācyaṃ tena kiñcit syād yata ityādikairvadan ।
avācyatvaṃ kathaṃ brūyānmūko ahamitivat sudhīḥ ।।
yena lakṣyamiti proktaṃ lakṣyaśabdena so avadat ।
ekasyāpi hi śabdasya gauṇārthasvīkṛtau satām ।।
mahatī jāyate lajjā yatra tatrākhilā ravāḥ ।
amukhyārthā iti vadan yastanmārgānuvartinām ।
kathaṃ na jāyate lajjā vaktuṃ śābdatvamātmanaḥ ।।
ātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāḥ sākṣāt pūrṇābhidhāyinaḥ ।
janmādikāraṇaṃ brahma lakṣitaṃ ca yadā tadā ।।
vandhyāputropamaṃ māyāśabalaṃ vācyamityapi ।
kalpayitvā vinā mānaṃ lakṣyaṃ śuddhaṃ vadan padaiḥ ।।
ātmaśabdoditasyaiva jñānaṃ muktāvasādhanam ।
āha śrutaparityāgaḥ syāccāsyāśrutakalpanam ।।
syāt sarvatra ca yatraikamapi loko jugupsate ।
niyamenobhayaṃ syāddhi yasya svaparayormate ।।
alaṅkṛtaḥ sadaivāyaṃ durghaṭaireva bhūṣaṇaiḥ ।
andhantamo nityuduḥkhaṃ tasya syād vasanadvayam ।।
anandā nāma te lokā andhena tamasā'vṛtāḥ ।
tāṃste pretyābhigacchantyavidvāṃso budho janāḥ ।।
asuryā nāma te lokā andhena tamasā'vṛtāḥ ।
tāṃste pretyābhigacchanti ye kecātmahano janāḥ ।।
ityādiśrutayo mānaṃ śataśo atra samantataḥ ।
heyatvāvacanāccaiva nātmā gauṇaḥ śrutau śrutaḥ ।।
tamevaikaṃ jānathānyā vāco muñcatha ceti ha ।
ukta ātmā kathaṃ gauṇo heyapakṣe hyasau śrutaḥ ।।
parivāratayā grāhyā api heyāḥ pradhānataḥ ।
pūrṇasya pūrṇamādāya pūrṇamevāvaśiṣyate ।।
iti svasyaiva pūrṇasya pūrṇe apyaya udāhṛtaḥ ।
kathaṃ māyāvyavacchinnaḥ pūrṇo mukhyatayā bhavet ।।
padaṃ ca nirguṇa iti kathaṃ gauṇaṃ vadiṣyati ।
guṇābhāvopalakṣyaṃ cet padaṃ tadapi vācakam ।।
ato anavasthitimukhasarvadoṣamahāspadam ।
kathametanmataṃ sadbhirādriyeta vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।।
na ca sāṅkhayanirākṛtyai sūtrāṇyetānyacīkḷpat ।
bhagavān nahyaśabdatvaṃ pradhāne aṅgīkarotyasau ।।
samanvaye pratijñāte śabdagocarataiva hi ।
prathamapratipādyā syāt tadabhāve kuto anvayaḥ ।।
kathaṃ ca lakṣaṇāvādī brūyād brahmasamanvayam ।
yo asau śabdasya mukhyārthastatraiva syāt samanvayaḥ ।।
janmādikāraṇe sākṣādāha devaḥ samanvayam ।
uktaṃ tadeva jijñāsyaṃ kvāvakāśo atra nirguṇe ।।
kathañcāsambhavastasya mukhyārthasya nirākṛtau ।
mānena kena vijñeyamavācyājñeyanirguṇam ।।
ameyaṃ cenna śāstrasya tatra vṛttiḥ kathañcana ।
tasmācchāstreṇa jijñāsyamasmadīyaṃ guṇārṇavam ।।
vāsudevākhyamadvandvaṃ paraṃ brahmākhilottamam ।
vijñeyavācyalakṣyatvapūrvāśeṣaviśeṣataḥ ।।
nirgataṃ manaso vāco yadi tat syādagocaram ।
astu tanmā vaded vādī nacāsmacchāstragaṃ tu tat ।।
avācyaṃ vācyamityuktavā kimityunmattavanmṛṣā ।
asmacchāstrasya cauryāya yatate svoktidūṣakaḥ ।।
janmādikāraṇaṃ yattat sākṣānnārāyaṇābhidham ।
vadantu śrutayo brahma śāstraṃ caitat tadarthataḥ ।।
svaprakāśatvamapi tu yairjñānasya nivāritam ।
kathaṃ sarvajñatā tasya svajñānādhigamaṃ vinā ।।
pravṛttamastvavācyaṃ te maiva brūyāḥ kathañcana ।
sarvaśabdairavācyaṃ taduktavā tadviṣayaṃ punaḥ ।।
vayaṃ tvāṃ śrutiyuktibhyāṃ baddhvāsmacchāstramañjasā ।
vicārayāmaḥ śrutibhiryuktibhiścaiva sādaram ।।
adbhutatvādavācyaṃ tadatarkyājñeyameva ca ।
anantaguṇapūrṇatvādityūde paiṅgināṃ śrutiḥ ।
avācyamiti loke api vaktayāścāryatamaṃ bhuvi ।।
evaṃ śāstrāvagamyatve vibhāgena samanvayam ।
ānandamaya ityādinādhyāyena vadatyajaḥ ।।
tatrānyatra prasiddhānāṃ viṣṇāveva samanvayam ।
śabdānāṃ prathame pāde guṇisāmānyavācinām ।।
guṇavācināṃ ca prathamamāha devaḥ samanvayam ।
samudraśāyinaṃ sarvaprasūtiprasavaṃ śrutiḥ ।।
tadeva brahma paramamiti sāvadhṛtirjagau ।
yato ato brahmaśabdasya tatraiva niyatatvataḥ ।।
yo annaṃ brahmetyādirūpādabhyāsāt taittirīyake ।
anyāsu caitadrūpāsu śākhāsvapi sahasraśaḥ ।।
ānandamaya ityādyaiḥ śabdairvācyo hariḥ svayam ।
upalakṣaṇatvaṃ śabdānāmānandamayapūrviṇām ।।
sūtrasyālpākṣaratvena sarvaśākhāvinirṇaye ।
punaśca prāpakāddhetostatrādhikaraṇāntaram ।।
sarve vedā āmananti yat padaṃ tviti hi śrutiḥ ।
ānandamayarūpe tu brahmaṇaḥ pucchatoktitaḥ ।।
samastābrahmatāprāpterānandamayanāma hi ।
brahmaśabdasya cābhyāsāt pañcarūpādiṣu sphuṭam ।।
brahmatāvayave api syāt tathāvayavini svataḥ ।
yathaiva kṛṣṇakeśasya kṛṣṇasya brahmatākhilā ।।
darśitā caiva pārthāya niḥsīmāḥ śaktayo asya hi ।
ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahma puruṣaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam ।।
viṣṇvākhyamuktamanyatra hyūrdhvaretaṃ ca tat prati ।
virūpākṣākhyamavaraṃ brahmoktaṃ tadvrate sthitam ।।
samānādhikṛtatvaṃ ceduttaraṃ nīlalohitam ।
kṛṣṇapiṅgalarūpeṇa punaruktaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
brahmādhipatirityatra tāpanīyaśrutau puraḥ ।
svaritabrahmaśabdāntaṃ bahuvrīhitvameṣyati ।।
svāhendraśatruvardhasva yad bahuvrīhitāmagāt ।
mahāvyākaraṇe sūtramiti svaravinirṇaye ।।
pūrvāntasvarite puṃsorbahuvrīhitvameṣyati ।
mahāvyākaraṇe sūtramiti svaravinirṇaye ।।
ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahmetyādyuddeśyadvitīyakā ।
vibhaktirūrdhvaretādiḥ prathamā rudragocarā ।।
tasmād viṣṇuṃ paraṃ brahma prati rudro vrate sthitaḥ ।
ūrdhvaretā iti hyeva śrutyartho avasito bhavet ।।
ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahma prati viṣṇuṃ sadāśivaḥ ।
ūrdhvaretā dhyāyati ha śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ ।।
ityarthametamevāha nīlagrīvaśrutiḥ parā ।
ārtharvaṇī paraṃ brahma tasmādeko hariḥ śrutau ।।
tadevartamiti prāha kathamevānyathā śrutiḥ ।
avadhārayantī tasyaiva hyṛtatvādikamañjasā ।।
eko nārāyaṇa āsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ ।
vāsudevo agra evāsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ ।।
nendrasūryau na ca guho na somo na vināyakaḥ ।
ityādivākyato viṣṇorutpattiravatāragā ।।
mukhyaṃ brahma haristasmāt prastāvaḥ paramityapi ।
mukhyabrahmagrahe yukte nāmukhyaṃ yujyate kvacit ।।
asambhave hi mukhyasya gauṇārthāṅgīkṛtirbhavet ।
prācuryārthāśca mayaṭaḥ sarve atra pratipāditāḥ ।।
bhogyatvamatra cādyatvamupajīvyatayā hareḥ ।
mahābhoktā mahābhogya ityartho annamaye bhavet ।।
mahāprāṇo mahābodho mahāvijñānavānapi ।
viśeṣasāmānyatayā vijñānaṃ mana ityapi ।।
ekasya jñānarūpasya hareruktirvibhāgataḥ ।
abhede api viśeṣeṇaivānya ityudito hariḥ ।।
bhedaśabdā viśeṣaṃ tu harāvanyatra bhinnatvāt ।
brūyurharerjīvajaḍairapi bhedaṃ hi mukhyataḥ ।।
brahmatarkavaco apyevamata ekaḥ sa pañcadhā ।
ukto annamaya ityādi bhṛgoścaitad vadiṣyati ।।
prāpyatvena mayaṭprokterna tatrāpyanyaducyate ।
pracurānnādirevāto hyannamannamayetyapi ।।
ucyate hyaviśeṣeṇa nānyat kiñcidihocyate ।
mahānandatva evāsya hetuḥ ko anyāditi sphuṭam ।।
uktaḥ śrutyantare yasmāt sukhaṃ labdhvā karotyayam ।
karoti nāsukhī bhūmā sukhaṃ nālpe sukhaṃ bhavet ।।
ityuktaṃ yat pravṛttiśca nṛttagānādikā sukhāt ।
duḥkhād rodādikā caiva sarvakartṛtvato asya ca ।।
sarvaśakter na duḥkhaṃ syādataḥ kevalalīlayā ।
pravartako na cedeṣa prāṇyādanyācca kaḥ pumān ।।
brahmavit paramāpnotīti yat prathamasūcitam ।
tadeva mantravarṇena satyaṃ jñānamanantavat ।।
lakṣitaṃ tatra satyatvaṃ sṛṣṭayānnaprāṇayorapi ।
uktaṃ jñānaṃ tu manasā vijñānenāpyudīritam ।।
anantatvaṃ tathā'nandamayavācāpyudāhṛtam ।
sadbhāvaṃ yāpayed yasmāt satyaṃ tat tena kathyate ।।
iti sṛṣṭiriha proktā jagatsadbhāvayāpakam ।
brahmeti sthāpanāyaiva sattvaṃ jīvanameva ca ।।
viśīrṇatā ca sattvaṃ syāt sannamityāhureva yat ।
ato adyatāttṛtānnatvaṃ satyaśabdārtha eva hi ।।
prāṇaṃ devā anuprāṇanti manuṣyāḥ paśavaśca ye ।
āyuḥ prāṇo hi bhūtānāmiti yad gatijīvane ।।
ukte saditidhātvartho gatiścāto hi satyatā ।
prāṇatvamavabodhārtho manudhātuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
nālpe sukhamiti proktayaivānandamayatoktitaḥ ।
anantatvaṃ sunirṇītaṃ pūrṇānando hi nālpake ।।
ato hi mantravarṇoktavistṛtistu samastayā ।
kriyate parayā yasmāditaro atra na kathyate ।।
puruṣaṃ vetti yo mucyennānyaḥ panthā hi vidyate ।
iti śruteranyavedī kathaṃ muktiṃ prayāsyati ।।
puruṣaḥ para ātmājo brahma nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।
mahānānanda ud viṣṇurbharga oma itīryate ।।
svayaṃ nārāyaṇo devo nānyasyaitāni kasyacit ।
tasmādomityudāhṛtya yajñadānādi kurvate ।।
sūktena pauruṣeṇainaṃ yajantyadhyātmakovidāḥ ।
iti paiṅgiśrutistena nānyajñānād vimucyate ।।
brahmaśabdodite tasminnātmaśabdaṃ prayujya ca ।
tasmādākāśasṛṣṭiṃ ca provācātra catuvirdhām ।।
bhūtaṃ bhūtābhimānī ca taddeho antarniyāmakaḥ ।
hariścākāśaśabdokto mukhyato harireva ca ।।
ā samantāt kāśate yadākāśo mukhyato hariḥ ।
balajñānasvarūpatvād vāyuragniragaṃ nayan ।।
āpa āpālanāccaiva pṛthivī prathito yataḥ ।
uṣyānāmāśrayatvena sa evoṣadhināmakaḥ ।।
oṣadhīṣu sthito viṣṇuḥ kṣudhitairāśrito bhavet ।
puri śete yataḥ so atha puruṣaśceti gīyate ।।
kriyāpravartakatvena prādurbhāvo harerjaniḥ ।
ākāśādiṣu nānyāsti hyabhimāno abhimāninaḥ ।।
abhimāniśarīrasya sākṣād bhūtasya codbhavaḥ ।
evaṃ dehādiparyantamāgataṃ harimeva tu ।।
parāmṛśati tasyaiva pañcarūpatvavittaye ।
tyaktavā bhūtādikaṃ sarvaṃ sa vā eṣa iti śrutiḥ ।।
sa ityātmapadoddiṣṭa eṣa jīvaśarīragaḥ ।
sārānnamaya evāyaṃ na lokānnamayaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
iti taṃ rasaśabdena viśinaṣṭi śarīragam ।
idamityeva nirdeśo vastraprāvṛtavad vibhoḥ ।।
śira āderbhavejjīvaśira ādau vyavasthiteḥ ।
taṃ viditvāsya muktiḥ syānnānyajñānāt kathañcana ।।
āditye puruṣe cāyamiti bhedopadeśataḥ ।
nāsyābhedo asti jīvena nānumā kāmacāriṇī ।।
vimatāni śarīrāṇi madbhogāyatanāni yat ।
śarīrāṇītyādikā tu tattvajñāne hyapekṣyate ।।
pratyakṣādiviruddhatvādakṣāgamabhayojkhitā ।
anumā kāmavṛttā hi kutra nāvasaraṃ vrajet ।।
jaḍa ātmaiva vastutvāt prameyatvājjaḍaṃ citiḥ ।
ghana ākāśa ityādyā vāryante kena hetunā ।।
na jīvabhedasūtrāṇāṃ śaṅkayātra punaruktatā ।
vākyāntaradyotakatvāt pṛthagityatra pūrṇatā ।
yogamannamayādyairyat phalatvenāsya śaṃsati ।
sthānadvaye apyataḥ kośā eta ityatisāhasam ।।
upasaṅkramaṇaṃ caiva dvitīyoddeśitaṃ prati ।
atikramaṃ vadantaṃ tamupaśabdo nivārayet ।।
aśrutasyātiśabdasya sthānaṃ dadyāt kathaṃ punaḥ ।
śrutāśrutaparityāgakalpane vigatahriyām ।।
mṛtāveva parityāgaḥ kṛto hyannamayasya ca ।
ye annaṃ brahmetyādyupāsāṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyataḥ ।।
uktavā pañcasvarūpāṇāṃ punastatprāptivādinī ।
sthānadvayagatā vedavāṇī tadapalāpinām ।।
tamaso anyatra saṃsthānaṃ kathameva saheta sā ।
adhīhi bhagavo brahmetyukto annaprāṇapūrvakam ।।
āha brahma kathaṃ tanna dvāraṃ taditi vādinaḥ ।
upasattiṃ kathaṃ vidyurupasannāya hi triśaḥ ।।
vaktavyaṃ brahma guruṇā caturvāramathāpi vā ।
sakṛd vetyāgamā brūyuḥ sampradāyavido api ca ।।
tad yatkiñcit kathaṃ brūyādupasannāya dikpatiḥ ।
na vaded brahma ca kathaṃ māyāvī na hi vārirāṭ ।।
caṣṭa ityeva taccakṣuḥ śravaṇācchrotramucyate ।
vacanādeva vāg brahma sṛṣṭisthityādikāraṇam ।।
tacca vāghūlaśākhāyāmaṣṭarūpamudāhṛtam ।
vijñānānandasahitaṃ pṛthak sṛṣṭayādilakṣaṇaiḥ ।।
āvāpodvāpataṣa śākhā yata āhuḥ paraṃ padam ।
yato bhūtāni jāyanta ityādyairlakṣaṇaiḥ svayam ।।
lakṣitaṃ guruṇā paścāt tapasaivāparokṣataḥ ।
dṛṣṭvaikaikaṃ svarūpaṃ tu samastoktānudarśanam ।।
icchatā'jñāṃ guroḥ prāpya tapasaivārokṣitam ।
abrahmetyeva vadatāṃ śrutahānyaśrutagrahau ।।
sākṣāllakṣaṇatāṃ prāptāviti lajjā taduktiṣu ।
samīpe sahabhogasya muktitvenoktito asakṛt ।।
bhedo jīveśayormithyetyeva mithyā svayaṃ bhavet ।
etena mayaṭaścaiva dvaividhyenārthakalpanāt ।
tadanyeṣāṃ matamapi satsaṃsatsu na bhāsate ।।
ato nārāyaṇo devo niḥśeṣaguṇavācakaiḥ ।
guṇisāmānyavacanairapi mukhyatayoditaḥ ।।
adhyātmagaiśca prāṇādyaistathaiva hyadhibhūtagaiḥ ।
annādiśabdairbhagavāneko mukhyatayoditaḥ ।।
janmādyasyeti sūtreṇa guṇasarvasvasiddhaye ।
brahmaṇo lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ śāstramūlaṃ yatastataḥ ।।
anvayaḥ sarvaśabdānāṃ guṇasarvasvavedakaḥ ।
śabdapravṛttihetūnāṃ tasmin mukhyasamanvayāt ।।
anyārtheṣvalpatāhetostannimittatvatastathā ।
tadvācakatvaṃ śabdānāṃ bahulātiprayogataḥ ।।
rūḍhamityeva sādhyaṃ syād rūḍhirhi dvividhā matā ।
avidvadvidvadāptyaiva mukhyā hi viduṣāṃ tu sā ।।
vidvadrūḍhirvaidikā syāt sā yogādeva labhyate ।
tasmānmukhyārthatā viṣṇoriti kṛtvā hṛdi prabhuḥ ।।
samanvayaṃ sādhayati devānāṃ tatra śaktatām ।
āśaṅkaya tatra rūḍhiṃ ca tacchabdānāmapi svayam ।।
samudrāntasthitatvādyaistaddharmairviṣṇurūḍhatām ।
sādhayitvābhidāṃ taiśca punareva nyavārayat ।।
ceṣṭā hi cetanānāṃ yā sā bhavet tatprasādataḥ ।
acetanasvabhāvastu vivarādiḥ kathaṃ tataḥ ।।
iti śaṅkānivṛttyarthamākāśa iti nāma ca ।
parato apivarīyastvapūrvālliṅgāddharerbhavet ।।
iti śaṅkānivṛttyarthamākāśa iti nāma ca ।
parato api varīyastva pūrvālliṅgāddharerbhavet ।।
prāṇādihetutādṛṣṭeratideśo hi tādṛśaḥ ।
liṅgaṃ balavadeva syāt prerako asyāpi yaddhariḥ ।।
nityatvādeva śabdasya tatsvabhāvaḥ kathaṃ hareḥ ।
kathaṃ prasiddhabahulaśabdānāmayathārthatā ।।
iti cet taddharereva bāhulyācchrutiliṅgayoḥ ।
tādṛśatvācca tacchakterbāhulye śrutiliṅgayoḥ ।।
anyasya mukhyavācyatvamiti tannātragasya hi ।
viṣṇoreva tu liṅgāni prāṇasthāni tu sarvaśaḥ ।।
prāṇasaṃvādapūrvāṇi mukhyato jīvagāni ca ।
abhyārcacchatavarṣāṇi prāṇavaṃśatvamityapi ।।
tasmādanyatragaiḥ śabdairuktanyāyaiḥ samantataḥ ।
eko nārāyaṇo devo bhaṇyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
vāsudevādirūpeṇa caturmūrtiśca sarvaśaḥ ।
athavā pañcamūrtiḥ sa prokto adhikaraṇaṃ prati ।।
pratisūtraṃ pratipadaṃ pratyakṣaramathāpi vā ।
taistairyuktiśrutinyāyaviśeṣairyogyatā yathā ।।
bṛhattantrapramāṇena bahvarthamapi saṅgrahāt ।
ucyate narabuddhīnāmapi kiñcidgrahārthataḥ ।।
grantho ayamapi bahvartho bhāṣyaṃ cātyarthavistaram ।
bahujñā eva jānanti viśeṣaṇārthametayoḥ ।
tasmānmahāguṇo viṣṇurnāmnāyapunaruktitaḥ ।।

।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāyarviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।

liṅgātmakānāṃ śabdānāṃ vṛttirnārāyaṇe pare ।
cintyate sarvagatvaṃ tu prathamaṃ pravicāryate ।।
tatra tatra sthito viṣṇustattacchaktiprabodhakaḥ ।
dūrato apyatiriktaḥ sa līlayā kevalaṃ prabhuḥ ।।
iti jñāpayituṃ karmakartrorutsargato bhidā ।
abhedo api viśeṣe syād balī so apyanapoditaḥ ।।
etad bhāvābhidhaṃ liṅgaṃ kriyāliṅge tataḥ param ।
antaryāmyantaraśceti kriyābhāvākhyamucyate ।।
adṛśyatvādyabhāvākhyaṃ śrutirliṅgādhikā parā ।
anityatvāt kriyāṇāṃ tu kathameva svarūpatā ।।
iti cet sa viśeṣo api kriyāśaktayātmanā sthiraḥ ।
śaktitā vyaktatā ceti viśeṣo api viśeṣavān ।।
abhinno api kriyādiśca svabhāva iti hi śrutiḥ ।
jñānaṃ nityaṃ kriyā nityā balaṃ śaktiḥ parātmanaḥ ।।
iti paiṅgiśrutiścāha śaktisadbhāva eva tu ।
kriyādinityatā jñeyā tadanyatra tvanityatā ।।
iti sattattvavacanaṃ dvitvaṃ caikasya yujyate ।
yaḥ seturiti caikatvavacanena viśeṣaṇāt ।।
antaḥ sthitvā ramaṇakṛdantaraḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।
ramaṇaṃ cātmaśabdenādeyaṃ mātīti cocyate ।।
viśiṣṭasukhavattvācca brahmatvaṃ ca viśiṣṭatā ।
anyonyaniyatiśceśaniyame nānyathā bhavet ।।
cetanānāṃ viśeṣo yaḥ svabhāvo apīśvarāpirtaḥ ।
anyonyaniyame tasmādanavasthityasambhavau ।।
īśvaraścenniyantā ca sa eva prathamāgataḥ ।
kimityapodyate kasmād vṛthāvasthitikalpanā ।
doṣavatyeva tasmāt sā naiva kāryā kathañcana ।।
ramaṇaṃ nātiyatnasya vikṣepādeva yujyate ।
iti cet sarvaniyamo yasya kasmānna śakyate ।।
ātmanāniyataṃ vastu pratīpaṃ hyātmano bhavet ।
svādhīnasattāśaktayādi kathamātmapratīpakam ।।
guṇakriyādayo bhāvā yadivā syurabhedinaḥ ।
abhedo abhāvadharmāṇāṃ brahmaṇā yujyate katham ।।
nābhāvo bhāva iti ca viśeṣaḥ prāyaśo bhavet ।
atadbhāvo anyatā ceti na viśeṣo asti kaścana ।।
doṣābhāvo guṇa iti prasiddho laukikeṣvapi ।
adṛśyatvādikāṃstasmād guṇānāha svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।।
bhāvābhāvavirodho api na tu sarvatra vidyate ।
tadabhāvo hi tadbhāvavirodhī na tato aparaḥ ।।
pṛthaktavābhāvatadrūpān bhedāṃstrīn kalpayanti cet ।
kalpanāgauravādyāstu doṣāstatra virodhinaḥ ।।
pṛthaktavānyatvabhedāstu paryāyeṇaiva laukikaiḥ ।
vyavahriyante satataṃ vaidikairapi sarvaśaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭahāniradṛṣṭasya kalpanetyeva dūṣaṇam ।
yadā tadadhiko doṣo vidyate ko nu vādinām ।।
bhāvābhāvasvarūpāstu viśeṣā eva vastunaḥ ।
abhinnā eva saṅgrāhyā vyavahāraprasiddhaye ।।
yathaikaḥ samavāyo api bhedābhedau ca vastuni ।
aṅgīkāryā viśeṣeṇa sthāneṣu vyavahartṛbhiḥ ।।
akhaṇḍavādino' pi syādviśeṣo anicchato apyasau ।
vyāvṛtte nirviśeṣe tu kiṃ vyāvartyabahutvataḥ ।।
bahuliṅgasamāyuktairbahubhī rūḍhanāmabhiḥ ।
prasiddhairanyagatvena vācyaḥ sākṣājjanārdanaḥ ।।
vaiśvānarādayaḥ śabdā api tadvācinastataḥ ।
tāni liṅgāni te śabdā api tadgā hi sarvaśaḥ ।
bahulāpyajñarūḍhistatprajñārūḍhiṃ na bādhate ।।

।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

tatrānyatra ca siddhānāṃ liṅganāmnāṃ punarhariḥ ।
viśeṣānmukhyato vṛttiṃ svasminnevātra vaktayajaḥ ।।
viṣṇāvevātmaśabdasya rūḍhatvānna śivādikān ।
śrutirvaktyakhileśatvād bhūmā viṣṇuḥ sukhādhikaḥ ।।
ato viruddhavad bhātamapi vyākhyāya tattvataḥ ।
yojanīyaṃ harau vākyaṃ viruddhairlakṣaṇairyutam ।।
brahmaiva tāni liṅgāni tadanyatra tvasantyapi ।
avirodhena govinde santyasthūlādikāni ca ।।
anyavastusvabhāvānāṃ sthaulyādīnāmapākṛtim ।
nārāyaṇe śrutirvakti natu tasyāsvabhāvatām ।।
sarvadharmā sarvanāmā sarvakarmā guṇāḥ śrutāḥ ।
doṣāḥ śrutāśca netyādyā pramāṇaṃ śrutiratra ca ।।
liṅgaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ śabdau sthānaṃ liṅgamanugrahaḥ ।
punaḥ śabdā liṅgaśabdau vicāryā dvisthitā iha ।।
bāhulyaṃ liṅgaśabdānāmanuktiśca viruddhatā ।
adṛṣṭiranvayābhāvo viparītaśrutibhramaḥ ।।
liṅgāvakāśarāhityabhramastādṛg dvayaṃ tathā ।
bahutādṛktavamuktasya virodho arthāt tathā gatiḥ ।
samastametadityatra pūrvapakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ ।।
tā eva balavantastu gatyantaravivarjitāḥ ।
siddhāntayuktayo jñeyā dṛśyante tāśca sarvaśaḥ ।।
muktopasṛpyatā prāṇādādhikyaṃ sarvatastathā ।
vailakṣaṇyaṃ svabhāvasya prekṣāpūrvakriyā tathā ।।
arasya ṇyasya ceśatvaṃ sūryādyanukṛtistathā ।
vāmanākhyā sarvakampastacchabdānanyasiddhatā ।।
anāmarūpatā bhedasyopajīvyapramāṇatā ।
sarvaiśvaryādikādyāstā vedeśena pradarśitāḥ ।।
adhikāraśca taddhāniḥ prasaṅgādeva cintitau ।
tatphalāya vidhiḥ siddhe copāsāyā nirākṛtaḥ ।।
yato jaimininānyārthamasiddhe arthe vidhistathā ।
vidyādhirājasya matamavirodhastayostataḥ ।।
mokṣe phalaviśeṣo asti na ca sarvaṃ prakāśate ।
sarvadā tena devānāmapi yuktā hyupāsanā ।।
nityaṃ vṛddhikṣayāpetaṃ viṣṇoḥ pūrṇaṃ tu vedanam ।
spaṣṭātispaṣṭaviśadaṃ brahmaṇo aśeṣavastugam ।।
anyeṣāṃ kramaśo jñānaṃ mitavastugataṃ sadā ।
ityādayo viśeṣāstu sadā vidyāpaterhṛdi ।।
jaiminyādyāstu sāmānyavettṛtvāt tat tathāvadan ।
vidyeśamatametasmānnaiva sadbhirviruddhayate ।।

।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrībrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

duḥkhibaddhāvarādyāstu tadadhīnatvahetutaḥ ।
śabdā brahmaṇi vartante rājñi yadvat parājayaḥ ।।
svātantryaṃ tadgatatvaṃ ca śabdavṛtterhi kāraṇam ।
svātantryaṃ tatra mukhyaṃ syāt kuto rājñi jayo anyathā ।।
na hi bhṛtyasya vijayiśabdastāvat prayujyate ।
yāvad rājñyanyagatve api svātantryābhāsamātrataḥ ।।
bhṛtyabandhādikaṃ rājñi rājño bandhādiyogyataḥ ।
kāraṇaṃ saṃśayasya syāditi naiva prayujyate ।।
amaṅgalatvācchabdānāṃ rājñā yogādamaṅgale ।
apriyatvāttu śabdasya syāt prayoganivartanam ।।
guṇāstu tādṛśā yatra prayujyante akhilā api ।
pūjyeṣveva viśeṣeṇa svātantryaṃ mukhyakāraṇam ।।
tato doṣātidūratvāt saṃśayasyāpyasambhavāt ।
doṣāṇāṃ viṣṇugatvasya prājñabuddhivyapekṣayā ।।
svātantryārthamabhipretya doṣaśabdāśca viṣṇavi ।
vāsudevaśrutiścāha naiva viṣṇāvamaṅgalam ।।
maṅgalāmaṅgale anyatra tato nāmaṅgalaṃ vadet ।
svātantryāpekṣayā viṣṇau doṣo nāmaṅgaloktitaḥ ।।
bahubhuktavaṃ yathā doṣo nṛṣu naiva harau kvacit ।
evaṃ duḥkhyādiśabdāśca svātantryāpekṣayoditāḥ ।।
naiva doṣā harau tadgabuddhayoktā doṣakāriṇaḥ ।
tasmāt te doṣaśabdāśca tatraiva guṇavācakāḥ ।।
jātamotaṃ harau yasmājjyotiḥ ṣaḥ prāṇarūpataḥ ।
āyajñetaścāyajeto vasantiśca vasantataḥ ।।
vigatacchādanatvāt tu gaccha bhūtakṣayaṅkaraḥ ।
bhuṅkṣetyukto harir huṃ ca hutamasmin jagad yataḥ ।।
sphuṭatvāt phaḍiti proktaḥ kavarakṣaṇa ityataḥ ।
kavacaṃ vatarte yasmāt ṣaḍguṇatvena sarvadā ।
vaṣaṭ tadgatvatasteṣāṃ vauṣaḍityeva kathyate ।।
svīyaṃ svīkurute yasmāt svāhetyukto janārdanaḥ ।
namantyasmin guṇā yasyānnama ityeva kathyate ।।
ityaśeṣakriyānāmaśabdaireko janārdanaḥ ।
ucyate mukhyato yasmāt padavarṇasvarādibhiḥ ।।
tasmādanantaguṇatā śrutitātparyato asya hi ।
vijñānārthatvataḥ sarvaśabdānāṃ nāsti dūṣaṇam ।।
aṅgīkṛte api naivāsti doṣo vākyasamanvaye ।
tadarthatvena karmādeḥ sambhavādalpabuddhaye ।।
kaśchandasāṃ yogamiti śruteryogārthatattvavit ।
brahmaiko naiva cānyo asti ka ityasyarobhayārthataḥ ।।
tasyāpi pūrvasiddhasya jñānameveti niścayāt ।
nityayogo api śabdānāmarthairnaiva niṣiddhayate ।
strīśabdāśca niṣedhārthāḥ sarve api brahmavācakāḥ ।।
virodhisarvabāhulyakāraṇastrīniṣedhinām ।
pṛthak samanvayārthāni sthānānyetāni sarvaśaḥ ।।
sarvamānairvirodhaśca vyutpatterapyaśakyatā ।
parasparavirodhaśca virodhaḥ kāryatadvatoḥ ।
strīliṅgatvaṃ niṣedhaśca pūrvapakṣeṣu hetavaḥ ।।
doṣātyaspṛṣṭiniyamaḥ śabdārthānekatā tathā ।
bahurūpatvamīśasya vyaktayavyaktiviśeṣitā ।।
utpādanaṃ svadehācca durjanāvyaktatā tathā ।
itayādyā yuktayaḥ sākṣāt siddhāntasthāpakā iha ।।
anvayaḥ sarvaśabdānāmaśakyo jñātumañjasā ।
iti yallokavaimukhyaṃ jaiminyādimataṃ vadan ।।
vidyādhinātho bhagavānapācakre svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।
svaśiṣyāṇāṃ prasiddhayarthaṃ matamātmīyamaṃśataḥ ।।
vijñātaṃ tairjagādātra tāratamyaṃ nṛṇāṃ vadan ।
teṣu teṣu padārtheṣu rūḍhiraṅgīkṛtā yataḥ ।।
prayojanabahutvena tasya tasyāvirodhataḥ ।
upadeśādisāmarthyād viṣṇau śaktiśca gṛhyate ।।
tathāpyetadvirodhe tu tadvācitvamapodyate ।
avirodhe tu bahvarthā etanmūlatayā matāḥ ।।
ito hi rūḍhatānyeṣāmupajīvyatvamatra hi ।
tatsiddhistadapekṣā ca sāpekṣā ca harīcchayā ।।
tasmāt paramamukhyatvaṃ viṣṇāvanyatra mukhyatā ।
upalakṣaṇā ca gauṇī ca tisraḥ śabdasya vṛttayaḥ ।।
pravṛttihetorbāhulyaṃ jñeyaṃ paramamukhyatā ।
tatra prayogabāhulyaṃ yadi tatparatā kimu ।।
ubhayaṃ dṛśyate viṣṇau śabdānāmapi sarvaśaḥ ।
prayogamātrabāhulyaṃ rūḍhirityabhidhīyate ।।
prayogayuktasādṛśyaṃ sambandho vāpyamukhyataḥ ।
vṛttiheturiti jñeyaḥ pūrvāyoge paragrahaḥ ।।
etameva tathā santaṃ śatarcītyādināmabhiḥ ।
ācakṣata iti hyatra santamityavadhāraṇā ।।
yogasya rūḍheḥ prābalyaṃ vidvadrūḍhiṃ ca tatragām ।
bahuśo darśayatyañjastātparyāt saniruktikam ।।
a iti brahma kathitaṃ tadvayākhyānānmatā tathā ।
śabdānāmapi sarveṣāṃ nāmavitkṛtakṛtyatā ।।
viṣṇunāmārtharūpatvaṃ saṃhitāderathābravīt ।
ṇakāraṃ ca ṣakāraṃ ca balaceṣṭātmakaṃ vadan ।।
tajjñānapūrvakatvena saṃhitādhyayanaṃ tathā ।
upasargatvato vestu tācchīlyārthādunastathā ।।
ṇakāraśca ṣakāraśca nāmarūpatayā matau ।
tasmāt samanvayo viṣṇau svaravarṇapadātmanaḥ ।।
api vedasya kimuta vākyarūpeṇa saṅgatiḥ ।
ghoṣāḥ sarve api vedāśca sarve vedāśca yat padam ।।
indraṃ mitraṃ yamindraṃ ca prathamaḥ saṅkṛtistathā ।
nāmadhāḥ sarvadevānāmeka ityādikā śrutiḥ ।।
pramāṇamuktaviṣaye tadevoktamupakramāt ।
iti svayaṃ bhagavatā bruvatāśeṣamanvayam ।।
na śabdavācyataivātra pradhanasya niṣiddhayate ।
sarvavedetihāseṣu purāṇeṣu ca saṅgrahāt ।।
sattvaṃ rajastama iti guṇāḥ prakṛtisambhavāḥ ।
nibadhnanti mahābāho dehe dehinamavyayam ।।
ityādivākyarūpeṇa yatrārtho nānya iṣyate ।
tejo abannātmakaṃ vāpi yadyupādānamiṣyate ।।
anādyevāparādhaḥ kaḥ pradhānamiti codite ।
ajāmekāmiti prāha śrutiretāṃ yadā tadā ।
ko doṣaḥ sarvathaivāsti pariṇāmi jaḍaṃ yadi ।।
asmākaṃ paramamukhyārtho bhagavāneka eva tu ।
mukhyamātratayā rūḍhaṃ sarvamabhyupagamyate ।।
sarveṣāmapi śabdānāṃ gauṇyādyaṃ tadayogataḥ ।
arthadvayamabhipretya pravṛtte hariruktavān ।।
kāryāṇāṃ kāraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ vacasāṃ vācyamuttamam ।
yogānāṃ paramāṃ siddhiṃ paramaṃ te padaṃ viduḥ ।।
iti buddhau samārohādubhayoryogarūḍhayoḥ ।
tyāge ca kāraṇābhāvādubhayārthatvamiṣyate ।।
viparītapramābhāve pūrvārohastu kāraṇam ।
sā bhaved yatra sa vyarthaḥ pūrvāroho bhramo yathā ।
ato jagadupādānaṃ pradhānaṃ vakti sā śrutiḥ ।।
yattat triguṇamavyaktaṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmakam ।
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ prāhuraviśeṣaṃ viśeṣavat ।।
pañcabhiḥ pañcabhirbrahma caturbhirdaśabhistathā ।
etaccaturviṃśatikaṃ gaṇaṃ prādhānikaṃ viduḥ ।।
iti bhāgavate prāha vidyādhīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।
na ca prakṛtiśabdena brahmopādānamucyate ।।
avikāraḥ sadā śuddho nitya ātmā sadā hariḥ ।
sadaikarūpavijñānabala ānandarūpakaḥ ।।
nirvikāro akṣaraḥ śuddho nirātaṅko ajaro amaraḥ ।
aviśvo viśvakartājo yaḥ paraḥ so abhidhīyate ।।
nirvikāramanaupamyaṃ sadaikarasamakṣayam ।
brahmeti paramātmeti yaṃ vidurvaidikā janāḥ ।।
iti śrutipurāṇoktayā na vikārī janārdanaḥ ।
parādhīnaviśeṣāptiranivartyānyathābhavaḥ ।।
kṣīrādivad vikāraḥ syānnaiva sa syāddhareḥ kvacit ।
apādānatvamevāsya yadyupādānateṣyate ।।
aṅgīkṛtaṃ tat pitṛvannatu viśvātmanā bhavaḥ ।
na corṇanābhijanitṛmātṛṇāṃ ca vikāritā ।।
cetanatvāt tadannaṃ hi kāryarūpatayā bhavet ।
apādānatayā viśvakartṛtvaṃ buddhipūrvakam ।।
uktaṃ bhāllaviśākhāyāṃ brahmatarke ca sādaram ।
icchāmātrāt prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiravikārasya sarvadā ।।
svabhāvo ayamanantasya rajo yenābhavajjagat ।
svadehādicchayā viśvaṃ bhuktapūrvaṃ janārdanaḥ ।।
sasarja mātāpitṛvadūrṇanābhivadeva vā ।
pradhānaṃ pariṇāmyeśo nirvikāraḥ svayaṃ sadā ।।
na cetanavikāraḥ syād yatra kvāpi hyacetanam ।
nācetanavikāro api cetanaḥ syāt kadācana ।।
nacānyasyānyarūpatvaṃ vikṛtatve api dṛśyate ।
na kṣīrādanyatā dadhnaḥ kenacid dṛśyate kvacit ।।
sarvajñād brahmaṇo anyatvaṃ jagato hyanubhūyate ।
abhedaḥ sattvamātreṇa syād kharvasvaṇayorapi ।।
bhāgena pariṇāmaśced bhāgayorbheda eva hi ।
yo bhāgo na vikārī syāt sa evāsmākamīśvaraḥ ।।
bhinnānāṃ samudāyasya nāma brahmeti ced bhavet ।
brahmopādānatā na syāt tadā viśvasya hi kvacit ।।
śṛṅgāccharo avilomabhyo dūrvā gomayatastathā ।
vṛścikaścetyevamādyeṣvapādānatvamiṣyate ।।
upādānaikadeśatvaṃ yadyapyatra pradṛśyate ।
apyapādānataivātra dṛṣṭānto brahmaṇo bhavet ।।
na hy upādānataivātra bāhyāvayavagauravāt ।
na cācetanatas tatra cetanasya samudbhavaḥ ।।
upādānatayā kintarhyapādānaṃ hyacetanam ।
kāryadehagatasyāsya cetanasya pradṛśyate ।।
sacca tyaccābhavaditi nāsya viśvatvamucyate ।
tat sṛṣṭveti giraivāsya pūrvaṃ viśvasya siddhitaḥ ।।
sattvāt tatervaidikatvāt samyag vaktumaśakyataḥ ।
āśrayatvāt svāśrayatvājjñānatvād durvidatvataḥ ।।
sattateryātanāccaiva hyaprāptatvācca durjanaiḥ ।
nityāsādhuguṇavyāptiyantṛrūpatvataḥ sadā ।
jagadgatena rūpeṇa brahmaiva hi tathocyate ।।
vyaktiruktaguṇānāṃ hi puruṣāpekṣayā nṛṇām ।
bhavedabhavadityādyaḥ prayogaścātra yujyate ।।
tasmādaśeṣakartaiko nirvikāro ramāpatiḥ ।
śabdaiḥ prakṛtirityādyaiḥ strīliṅgairabhidhīyate ।।
bahu syāmiti tasyaiva hyuktamārgeṇa yujyate ।
tattadgatena rūpeṇa tadarthaṃ hyasṛjajjagat ।।
yaccāvikṛtamevaitad brahma viśvātmanā mṛṣā ।
dṛśyate mandadṛṣṭayaiva sa sarga iti kathyate ।।
sā mandadṛṣṭistasyaiva brahmaṇaḥ kiṃ tato anyagā ।
brahmaṇaścet kva sārvajñyamanyagā cet svato anyatā ।।
nādehayogino dṛṣṭiriti tat kāraṇaṃ svataḥ ।
dehinaḥ kāraṇayutā dehāśca yadi na bhramāt ।।
kiṃ bhrāntikalpitaṃ tatra bhedo api bhramajo yadi ।
bhrānterajñānamūlatvāt tasya bhedavyapekṣayā ।।
nājñānakalpakaṃ kiñcidanyonyāśrayatā yataḥ ।
bhramatve tviyamuktiśca tadantaḥpatanānnahi ।।
vyāvahārikatā cāsya syādabādhyatva eva hi ।
bādhyaṃ nārthakriyākāri na ca svapno api no mṛṣā ।।
vāsanājanitatvena tasyāpyaṅgīkṛtatvataḥ ।
sa hi karteti vākyācca jāgrattvamiti hi bhramaḥ ।।
sarpabhramādāvapi hi jñānamastyeva tādṛśam ।
tadevārthakriyākāri tat sadevārthakārakam ।।
brahma tvarthakriyākāri parataḥ svata eva vā ।
aṅgīkṛtaṃ hi tenaiva paratastve na ca pramā ।।
amukhyasatyamānasya sādhakatve sadā'vayoḥ ।
na hi sampratipattiḥ syādatastiṣṭhatu sā pramā ।।
na hi vipratipannena śakyaṃ sādhayituṃ kvacit ।
sādhakatvaṃ tu satyasya sākṣiṇo hyāvayordvayoḥ ।
samyak sampratipannaṃ tanna vivatarmamataṃ bhavet ।।
yadi nāṅgīkṛtaṃ kiñcidanaṅgīkṛtatāpi hi ।
nāṅgīkṛteti mūkaḥ syāditi nāsmadvivāditā ।।
viśvaṃ satyaṃ yacciketa praghānvasya yathārthataḥ ।
ityādiśrutayaḥ sarvā viśvasatyatvavācakāḥ ।।
satyatvaṃ gaganādeśca sākṣipratyakṣasādhitam ।
sākṣisiddhasya na kvāpi bādhyatvaṃ tadadoṣataḥ ।।
savarkāleṣvabādhyatvaṃ sākṣiṇaiva pratīyate ।
kālo hi sākṣipratyakṣaḥ suṣuptau ca pratītitaḥ ।।
atītānāgatau kālāvapi nāsākṣigocarau ।
pakṣīkartumaśakyatvānnānumā tatra vartate ।।
tadetaditi sarvaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ vā smṛtigocaram ।
sākṣisiddhena kālena khacitaṃ hyeva vartate ।।
tasmānna taṃ vinā kiñcit smartuṃ draṣṭumathāpi vā ।
śakyaṃ tannityasiddherhi nānumāvasaro bhavet ।।
ato adoṣapratītasya satyatvaṃ sākṣiṇā matam ।
parīkṣādeśca satyatvaṃ tena hyeva mataṃ bhavet ।।
anyathā śrutiyuktayādipramāṇaiśca sahaiva tu ।
akasmād vinivṛttiśca kiṃ viśvasya na śaṅkayate ।।
itaḥ pūrvaṃ tathābhāvād yadi no saṃsṛtergatiḥ ।
vākyānumāditaścet syāt tatprāmāṇyaṃ ca sākṣitaḥ ।।
tatprāmāṇyaṃ yathā sākṣī sthāpayatyevameva hi ।
sarvakāleṣvapi sthairyād vyabhicāramapohya ca ।।
evamakṣajamānatvasiddhāṃ viśvasya satyatām ।
kimiti sthāpayennāyaṃ nirdoṣajñānaśaktitaḥ ।।
ekajñānakṛtaṃ viśvamiti yaccoṣyate mṛṣā ।
bahujñānakṛtaṃ viśvamiti tasyottaraṃ bhavet ।।
parasya satyatāṃ jānannapi yaḥ svātmataskaraḥ ।
paro nāstīti vadati kimityunmattavad vadet ।।
parābhāve hi vāg vyarthā yadi naivocyate tadā ।
kaśāvetrādikaṃ tasya taskarasyottaraṃ vadet ।।
prapañco yadi vidyeta nivarteta na saṃśayaḥ ।
māyāmātramidaṃ dvaitamadvaitaṃ paramārthataḥ ।।
vikalpo vinivarteta kalpito yadi kenacit ।
upadeśādayaṃ vādo ajñāte dvaitaṃ na vidyate ।।
ityatra yadiśabdau ca nivarteteti ca dvayam ।
viśvasya satyatāmāhurvidyetotpattimeva ca ।।
vidotpattāviti hyasmād dhātorutpattireva hi ।
nivṛttivyāptiyuk prāyaḥ prapañco bhedapañcakaḥ ।।
jīveśvarabhidā caiva jaḍeśvarabhidā tathā ।
jīvabhedo mithaścaiva jaḍajīvabhidā tathā ।
mithaśca jaḍabhedo yaḥ prapañco bhedapañcakaḥ ।।
so ayaṃ satyo hyanādiśca sādiścennāśamāpnuyāt ।
dvaitaṃ na vidyata iti tasmādajñānināṃ matam ।।
iti śrutermitaṃ trātaṃ māyākhyaharividyayā ।
uttamo artho haristvekastadanyanmadhyamādhyamam ।।
vācārabdhaṃ tu sāṅketyaṃ nāma syād vikṛtaṃ bahu ।
nityaṃ tu nāmadheyaṃ yanmṛttiketyādi vaidikam ।।
prādhānyāt tatparijñānāt prākṛtājño api pūruṣaḥ ।
vidvānityucyate sadbhirevaṃ nityaparātmavit ।।
sadātanaṃ satyamiti nityamevocyate budhaiḥ ।
prayogaścottaratrāsti jarā yadyenamāpnuyāt ।।
dehaḥ pradhvaṃsate vāyaṃ kiṃ tato asyātiśiṣyate ।
hanyate na vadhenāyaṃ jarayā ca na jīryati ।।
etat satyaṃ brahmapuramiti nityatva eva hi ।
vācārambhaṇamityukte mithyetyaśrutakalpanam ।।
punaruktirnāmadheyamitītyasya nirarthatā ।
ekaḥ piṇḍo maṇiśceti padavaiyathyarmeva ca ।।
vikāratvavivakṣāyāṃ nacaikanakhakṛntanam ।
sarvakārṣṇāyasaṃ ca syādataḥ sādṛśya eva ca ।।
vivakṣātra tu nityatve prādhānye coktavartmanā ।
prādhānyapratipattyarthaṃ sṛṣṭayādeścaiva vistaraḥ ।।
tasmāt kenāpi mārgeṇa na vivartamataṃ bhavet ।
tadasaṅkhayātadoṣetaṃ heyameva śubhārthibhiḥ ।।
asaṅkhayatvena doṣāṇāṃ granthādhikyabhayādapi ।
uparamyate tato viṣṇuricchāpūrvakamaśramaḥ ।
karoti pitṛvad viśvaṃ pūrṇaśeṣaguṇātmakaḥ ।।

।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne prathamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

uktaḥ samanvayaḥ sākṣādavirodho atra sādhyate ।
caturvidhasya tasyādau yauktastatrāpi ca smṛteḥ ।।
tasyāścatuḥsvarūpatvāt pratyekaṃ caturātmakāḥ ।
pādāḥ sarve tadaṃśāśca mūrtīnāṃ varṇamā'gamāt ।।
āptatā samatādṛṣṭiśrutisāmyabalādbhavāḥ ।
sarvānusāro laghutā viśeṣādarśanāphale ।।
iṣṭasiddhiśca niyamaḥ pūrvapakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ ।
etā eva tvatibalā siddhāntasya niyāmakāḥ ।।
āptaiḥ pratyakṣato dṛṣṭvā proktamarthaṃ kathaṃ śratiḥ ।
pipīlikālipinibhā vārayeta sarvagā hi te ।।
iti ced yadyaśeṣajñā rudrādyā haripūrvakāḥ ।
kiṃ nāśeṣavido mānaṃ hy ubhayatra samaṃ bhavet ।।
nacāptiniścayastatra śakyate vyabhicārataḥ ।
nacāsyā vyabhicāre api hīyate mānatā kvacit ।।
vedoktasyādhikārasya durnirūpatvataḥ sadā ।
niyamo vyabhicāro vā naiva jñātuṃ hi śakyate ।।
adhikāro hi sulabhaḥ kathito anyāgameṣvalam ।
vedokto hy adhikārastu durlabhaḥ sarvamānuṣaiḥ ।।
anyāgameṣu vipratvamapi caṇḍālajanmanām ।
maṇḍalāntaḥpraveśena kramaśaḥ pratipādyate ।।
adhikāraṃ durāpādyamuktavātisulabhaṃ punaḥ ।
aśakyaṃ sādhanaṃ coktavā suśakaṃ tatphalāptaye ।
ucyate atastaduktaṃ hi vyabhicāri phale api tu ।।
kathaṃ pramāṇatāṃ gacchennityatvāt puruṣodbhavaiḥ ।
ujkhitaṃ sarvadoṣaiśca kathaṃ no mānatāṃ vrajet ।।
virūpa nityayā vācā nityayānityayā sadā ।
ityādiśrutibhirvedo nitya ityavagamyate ।।
pipīlikālipiścāpi pramāṇamavirodhataḥ ।
yathā drauṇerulūkena kṛtamapyāsa bodhakam ।।
aviruddhaṃ viruddhaṃ tu virodhādeva bādhitam ।
virodhādarśanāt tasmād vedaprāmāṇyamiṣyate ।।
tanmūlatvāt smṛtīnāṃ ca virodho yatra na kvacit ।
virodho api sa evoktaḥ pratyakṣeṇāgamena vā ।।
āgamenāgamasyaiva virodhe yuktiriṣyate ।
upajīvyavirodhe tu vedasyānyārthakalpanā ।।
pratyakṣamupajīvyaṃ syāt prāyo yuktirapi kvacit ।
āgamaikapramāṇeṣu tasyaiva hyupajīvyatā ।।
yukto ayuktaśca yadyartha āgamasya pratīyate ।
syāt tatra yukta evārtho yuktiśca trividhā matā ।।
vyāptiḥ pratyakṣatā yasyā yuktigā'gamagā tathā ।
pratyakṣāgamamūlā tu yuktistatra balīyasī ।।
yāthārthyameva mānatvaṃ tanmukhyaṃ jñānaśabdayoḥ ।
arthatvamaryataiva syānna kriyārtheṣu sā matā ।।
jñānārthe jñeyatā mukhyā śabdārthe tadanantaram ।
yathārthajñānajanakā yathārthā yuktayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
anupramāṇametāni hyakṣayuktivacāṃsyataḥ ।
prāmāṇyaṃ nānuvādasya smṛterapi vihīyate ।।
yāthārthyameva prāmāṇyaśabdārtho yad vivakṣitaḥ ।
aṅgīkṛtaṃ cet prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtyādeḥ kā virodhatā ।।
nacāphalatvaṃ vaktavyaṃ sarvasmṛtyanuvādayoḥ ।
phalavattvaṃ nacāsmābhiḥ prāmāṇyaṃ hi vivakṣitam ।।
tṛṇādidarśane kiṃ ca phalavattvaṃ nigadyate ।
sukhaduḥkhādikaṃ kiñcit smṛtāvapi hi dṛśyate ।।
na paricchedakāryeva pramāṇamiti ca pramā ।
nirdoṣākṣodbhavaṃ hyatra pratyakṣamiti gīyate ।।
prākṛtaṃ śuddhacaitanyamakṣaṃ tu dvividhaṃ matam ।
śuddhamīśaramāmukteṣvanyatra prākṛtairyutam ।।
nirdoṣameva caitanyamanyatrobhayamiṣyate ।
sukhaduḥkhādiviṣayaṃ śuddhaṃ saṃsārageṣvapi ।।
nirdoṣatvātiniyamāt tad baliṣṭhatamaṃ matam ।
pañcendriyamanobhedāt prākṛtaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ smṛtam ।।
anumā yuktirevoktā vyāptireva tu sā smṛtā ।
pratijñātārthasiddhayarthaṃ vyāptireva yadoditā ।।
avaśiṣṭaṃ kimatrāsti liṅgaṃ tatra vijānataḥ ।
yadi liṅgamasiddhaṃ syāt kuta evāsya mānatā ।।
yadi smārakamātraṃ syāt smarturnātra prayojanam ।
na pañcāvayoktau ca vivādāvasitirbhavet ।।
dṛṣṭāntādiṣu caivaṃ syāt sādhanaṃ punareva hi ।
liṅgoktāvapi caivaṃ syādanumāvasitirdhruvā ।।
virodho asaṅgatiścaiva sākṣād yuktestu dūṣaṇam ।
pratijñāyāmasambandho yukteruktā hyasaṅgatiḥ ।।
virodho api tridhaiva syāt pratijñārthaviruddhatā ।
liṅgarāhityamavyāptirnyūnādhikye tu vācike ।।
sādhyavyāpakavailomyamavyāptiḥ sādhanasya ca ।
durbalena virodhe api na pramāṇamasādhakam ।।
svavākyena virodhe api naiva sādhakatāṃ vrajet ।
saṃvādānuktisaṃyuktā eta eva ca nigrahāḥ ।।
vādo jalpo vitaṇḍeti kathāstisro vijānatām ।
svārthaṃ parārthamapi vā tattvanirṇayasādhanī ।।
kevalaṃ tu kathā vādo jalpo arthādivyapekṣayā ।
satāmeva kathā jñeyā vitaṇḍā tvasatāṃ satām ।।
aprakāśya svasiddhāntamasatāṃ pakṣadūṣaṇam ।
ukte taiḥ prathamaṃ māne vaktavyaṃ tasya dūṣaṇam ।।
vidyāparīkṣāpūrvaiva vitaṇḍā jalpa eva ca ।
uccanīcatvanirṇītiryato jayaparājayau ।।
vinaiva tattvanirṇītiṃ na hi jalpādinā kvacit ।
uccanīcatvavijñānamiti vidyāparīkṣaṇam ।।
vādena coccanīcatvavijñānaṃ bhavati sphuṭam ।
iti vādasya pūrvatvaṃ tatsiddhau vyarthatānyayoḥ ।।
bahuvidyatvasiddhau tu naiva vādo api kāraṇam ।
sabhāsabhāpaprāśnīkapūrvastu spardhināmapi ।।
vāda evobhayārthaḥ syānnirṇītijayakārakaḥ ।
tattvāprakāśa evaiko vitaṇḍājalpayoḥ phalam ।।
vinā vādena vidyāyā yadi śakyaṃ parīkṣaṇam ।
syājjalpādirapi kvāpi vāda evānyathā bhavet ।।
jalpa ityapi nāma syād vādasyaitādṛśasya tu ।
pratijñāmātrasādhyatvamapi syād yājñavalkyavat ।।
sabhā sabhāpatiścaiva prāśnikāścaiva vaiṣṇavāḥ ।
rāgadveṣavihīnāśca syuḥ sabhyāḥ sarvavedinaḥ ।।
prāśnikāścaitadajñāne sabhyāścaiṣāṃ ca dūragāḥ ।
pramāṇaṃ nirṇayāya syuḥ pakṣapātavivarjitāḥ ।।
ubhābhyāṃ sādhanaṃ caiva dūṣaṇaṃ vādajalpayoḥ ।
sadbhirāgama evaikaḥ prayojyo abhīṣyasādhakaḥ ।।
svasiddhāntānusāreṇa hyasadbhiranumocyate ।
pratyakṣāgamavairūpyamāśrityānyārthataiva tu ।।
āgame daśarnīyātra doṣo liṅgavilomatā ।
liṅgānukūlyaṃ svārthasya śrutyādīnāmanugrahaḥ ।।
tripañcāvayavāmeva yugmāvayavinīmapi ।
niyamād yo anumāṃ brūyād taṃ brūyād yadi tādṛśī ।
nānumeti tadā kena sādhyāvayavakalpanā ।।
[NOTE jump in verse numbering, no lacuna in text!]
niyatāvayavāsiddhau vyāptimātreṇa sādhanam ।
kartavyameva tena syāt tasmāt saivānumā matā ।।
anubhūtiḥ pramāṇaṃ cet kena smṛtirapodyate ।
pūrvānubhūte kiṃ mānamityukte syāt kimuttaram ।।
mānasaṃ taddhi vijñānaṃ tacca sākṣipramāṇakam ।
atītānāgataṃ yadvad yogibhirdṛśyate añjasā ।
evaṃ pūrvānubhūtaṃ ca manasaivāvagamyate ।।
vijñātaṃ manasā pūrvaṃ mayaitat kṛtamityapi ।
sākṣādanubhavāt siddhaṃ kathameva hyapodyate ।।
evaṃ lakṣaṇake mānatraye brahmādivastuṣu ।
pramāṇaṃ veda evaikas tatprāmāṇyaṃ ca sādhitam ।।
tathāpi mṛjjalādīnāṃ buddhivāgādivācakaḥ ।
dṛṣṭavyāptiviruddhatvāt tatra mānaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ।।
tatastannāmakaḥ kaścit pumānanyo bhavediti ।
yuktayāgamāvirodhena prāptamatrābhidhīyate ।।
bālarūḍhiṃ vinaivāpi vidvadrūḍhisamāśrayāt ।
tattannāmāna evaite tattadvastvabhimāninaḥ ।।
santi teṣāṃ viśeṣeṇa śaktiranyebhya ucyate ।
vyāptiścoktānusāreṇa dṛśyante cādhikāribhiḥ ।।
śāstroktavastunaścaiva vyutpattiḥ śāstraliṅgataḥ ।
vyutpattiḥ sā balavatī mūrkhavyutpattitā hi yat ।।
dṛḍhayuktivirodhe tu sarvatra nyāya īdṛśaḥ ।
alpavākyayutā yuktirbahulaiva virodhinī ।।
yatra tatra kathaṃ vastunirṇayaḥ syāditīrite ।
virodhiyuktibāhulyāditi nyāyo viniścitaḥ ।।
yuktestu yuktibāhulyamāgamādāgamasya ca ।
kathaṃ na nirṇayaṃ kuryādityasat kāraṇaṃ na hi ।।
śrutyartho bhavati kvāpi śrutiprāyopapattibhiḥ ।
avirodhaścaturthe tu pāte samyak samarthyate ।।
asat kāryaṃ yathā dṛṣṭaṃ vastutvāt kāraṇaṃ tathā ।
iti cenna niṣedhaikasvarūpasya na kartṛtā ।।
buddhipūrvapravṛttirhi kartṛtvamiha niścitam ।
pratiṣedhātmakatvaṃ tu bhāvasyābhāvadharmataḥ ।
dharmadharmaikyataścaiva natu tanmātratā bhavet ।।
abhāvasya ca bhāvo api dharmo athāpi hi dharmiṇaḥ ।
tādṛktavaṃ mātratehoktā buddhirāhityameva tat ।।
viśeṣyataiva dharmitvaṃ prathamapratipattiṣu ।
niṣedhavidhirūpatvaṃ bhāvābhāvatvamatra hi ।।
sarvanāśeṣvapi sadā śiṣṭatvād yasya kasya nuḥ ।
nāśo ayaṃ vimato api syānnāśatvāt kartṛśeṣavān ।।
nacāśeṣanṛnāśastu dṛṣṭo dṛśyo asti vā kvacit ।
dharmādharmāśrayatvena svīkāryo api naro laye ।।
anāditvaṃ vinādṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ syāt kāraṇaṃ kvacit ।
pūrvādṛṣṭāt parādṛṣṭaṃ yadi naivottaraṃ kutaḥ ।।
adṛṣṭaṃ kāraṇaṃ no cellaye mānaṃ ca kiṃ bhavet ।
utpattināśakārī hi buddhimān dṛśyate kvacit ।।
taddṛṣṭāntena sarvatra kartā kiṃ nānumīyate ।
āgamānugṛhītā tu mānameṣānumāpitu ।।
āgamānugrahābhāve na tarkaḥ syāt pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।
akṣajāgamamūlasya syādevāsya pratiṣṭhitiḥ ।
anyathāsyāpratiṣṭhā ca svavācā vyāhataiva hi ।।
na ca śiṣyāgṛhītatvaṃ nirīśādīśavādinaḥ ।
ato avaśiṣṭajīvādikartṛtātra niṣiddhayate ।।
tanmano akurutetyāderasato manaso janiḥ ।
nivāritā tu pūrvatra hyakasmāditi tadvinā ।।
asato viśvajananamāśaṅkayātra niṣiddhayate ।
prāpakaṃ vākyamātraṃ tu parihāro viśeṣitaḥ ।।
kvacijjīvākṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā cetanādeva cākṛtam ।
tadvadevānumānyatra vastutvāt kriyate śruteḥ ।।
nānyadanyatvamāpannaṃ kvacid dṛṣṭaṃ kathañcana ।
ato jīvasya na brahmabhāvaḥ syāddhi kadācana ।।
kvacid bhinnatayā dṛṣṭaṃ tadabhinnatayā katham ।
dṛśyenno dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ hi tādṛśaṃ na ca dṛśyate ।।
bhoktṛtvāpattita iti yanmataṃ tat kuto hariḥ ।
bhoktrāpatteriti prāha kathaṃ ca tadananyatā ।।
jagatastvavikāratva uktanyāyena sādhite ।
svatantrakāraṇānyatvaṃ tena hyatra niṣiddhayate ।।
dravyaṃ karma ca kālaśca svabhāvaścetanā dhṛtiḥ ।
yatprasādādime santi na santi yadupekṣayā ।
iti śrutestadvaśasya bhāvo na para ityataḥ ।।
śakto api hyanyathākartuṃ svecchāniyamato hariḥ ।
kāraṇairniyataireva karotīdaṃ jagat sadā ।।
nityabhedo nimittena hyupādānena tu dvayam ।
asad yat kāryarūpeṇa kāraṇātmatayāsti hi ।।
anavasthānyathā hi syāt sarvatrotpattināśayoḥ ।
śakto api bhagavān viṣṇurakartuṃ kartumanyathā ।।
svabhinnaṃ kāraṇābhinnabhinnaṃ viśvaṃ karotyajaḥ ।
iti śruteravasita uktārtho ayamaśeṣataḥ ।।
anaṃśasyāpi jīvasya kiñcit sāmarthyayojanām ।
kāryeṣu yaḥ karotyaddhā namastasmai svayambhuve ।।
yadi bhāgena kāryeṣu jīvaśaktiṃ na yojayet ।
haristadā hi sarvatra kṛtsnayatnoṃ'śitāpi vā ।।
aṃśino hi paṭādyā ye bhinnaireva parasparam ।
aṃśairaṃśina ucyante naivameva hi cetanāḥ ।।
ato anaṃśina ityeva śrutireteṣu vartate ।
apyanekasvarūpeṣu viśeṣādeva kevalam ।।
bahusvarūpatākhyā tu teṣvastyeva hi sāṃśatā ।
bahutvenāvinābhāvād bhinnatā niyamād bhavet ।।
yadi naivaṃ niyamakṛd bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ ।
tasya tvaśeṣaśaktitvād yujyate savarmeva ca ।।
virodhaḥ sarvavaiśiṣṭaye yo dvitīye nirasyate ।
nārāyaṇasya tvadhyāye tadanye tatratatragāḥ ।।
sṛṣṭisaṃhāravākyānāṃ jīvarūpābhidhāyinām ।
apyanyonyāvirodhastu dvitīyādhyāyagocaraḥ ।।
mānameyaviśeṣeṇa punaruktirna jāyate ।
sadā pravṛttirīśasya svabhāvādeva kevalam ।।
aṅgaceṣyā yathā puṃsaḥ kāściduddeśavarjitāḥ ।
devasyaiṣa svabhāvo ayamityāha śrutirañjasā ।।
krīḍāṃ prayojanaṃ kṛtvā sṛṣṭiḥ śrutivirodhinī ।
iti kevalalīlaiva nirṇītā prabhuṇā svayam ।।
ātmaprayojanārthāya spṛhāṃ śrutiravārayat ।
na prayojanavattvenetyata āha jagadguruḥ ।।
icchāmātraṃ prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiriti sṛṣṭau viniścitāḥ ।
iti praśaṃsayā kāmaśrutibhyaścaiva yuktitaḥ ।
mahātātparyayukteśca necchāmātraṃ niṣiddhayate ।।
mokṣārthāḥ śrutayo yasmāt sa ca tasya prasādataḥ ।
unninīṣativākyācca lokadṛṣṭānusārataḥ ।।
icchāṃnimittako yasmāt tadabhāve kutaḥ śrutiḥ ।
mahātātparyarahitā pramāṇatvaṃ gamiṣyati ।।
yāthārthyameva mānatvamapi vākyaṃ prayojakam ।
mānatvameti tatrāpi yat sampūrṇaprayojanam ।।
vaiṣamyaṃ caiva nairghṛṇyaṃ vedāprāmāṇyakāraṇam ।
nāṅgīkāryamato anyattu na vaiṣamyādināmakam ।।
yadadhīnā guṇāścaiva doṣā api hi sarvaśaḥ ।
guṇāstasya kathaṃ na syuḥ syurdeṣāśca kathaṃ punaḥ ।।
sarvadharmāpapattestad vākyairapi hi tādṛśaiḥ ।
nirdoṣāśeṣaguṇako nirṇīto bhagavān hariḥ ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrībrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।

smṛtiyuktiśrutiguṇayuktayo bahuyuktayaḥ ।
evaṃ caturvidhā naiva viruddhayante anvayaṃ prati ।।
iti prathamapādena nirṇīte apyabhiyogataḥ ।
darśanānāṃ pravṛttatvānmanda āśaṅkate punaḥ ।।
anādikālato vṛttāḥ samayā hi pravāhataḥ ।
nacocchedo asti kasyāpi samayasyetyato vibhuḥ ।।
bhrāntimūlatvameteṣāṃ pṛthag darśayati sphuṭam ।
tarkairdṛḍhatamaireva vākyaiścāgamavādinām ।।
daurlabhyācchuddhabuddhīnāṃ bāhulyādalpavedinām ।
tāmasatvācca lokasya mithyājñānaprasaktitaḥ ।
vidveṣāt parame tattve tattvavediṣu cāniśam ।।
anādivāsanāyogādasurāṇāṃ bahutvataḥ ।
durāgrahagṛhītatvād vartante samayāḥ sadā ।।
tathāpi śuddhabuddhīnāmīśānugrahayoginām ।
yuyuktayastamo hanyurāgamānugatāḥ sadā ।।
iti vidyāpatiḥ samyak samayānāṃ nirākṛtim ।
cakāra nijabhaktānāṃ buddhiśāṇatvasiddhaye ।।
cetanācetanaṃ tattvadvayameva nirīśvarāḥ ।
āhustat pañcapañcatvavibhāgasthamacetanam ।
cetanaṃ tadasaṅkhayātaṃ bhinnamanyad layaṃ bhavet ।।
acetanasya kartṛtvaṃ svātantryeṇa nigadyate ।
parasparavibhedaśca kāryāṇāmālayaṃ bhavet ।।
bhoktṛṇāṃ cetanasyāhuḥ kecit tāmapi nāpare ।
svarūpacaitanyabalāt svaprakāśācca bhogitām ।।
prakṛteśca svarūpasya vivekāgrahameva tu ।
abhogavādino bhogamāhurbhedagrahāt tayoḥ ।।
bhogināṃ muktiruddiṣṭā sa evābhogavādinām ।
īśasyāsaṅgrahādeva na yuktau tāvubhāvapi ।।
cetanecchānusāreṇa yadā dṛṣṭaḥ paṭodbhavaḥ ।
etādṛśatvamanyasya vastutvāt kena vāryate ।।
na ca kācit pramoktārthe śrutireva pramā hi naḥ ।
āptatvamuktamārgeṇa vakturnaivopapadyate ।।
aprāmāṇyasvatastvasya svīkārādapi māyivat ।
svoktākhilaniṣedhī syānna ca kiñcit prasiddhayati ।।
idaṃ nācetanavaśaṃ vastutvāt pratipannavat ।
ityeva pratiṣiddhasya kena mūlānumā bhavet ।।
svatantravṛttī racanā sā caivācetane kutaḥ ।
acetanatvaṃ svātantryamiti cātmapramāhatam ।।
svecchānusāritāmeva svātantryaṃ hi vido viduḥ ।
kuta icchācetanasya secchaṃ cet kimacetanam ।।
icchāmyahamiti hyeva nijānubhavarodhataḥ ।
acetanecchāpagatā yadi bhedāgraho atra ca ।।
kathaṃ na sa ghaṭasya syānmano ma iti bhedataḥ ।
manaso api gṛhītatvādubhayātmakatā yataḥ ।।
kāmasya tu manaḥ kāmaḥ priyāpriyavibhedataḥ ।
dvaividhyaṃ dṛśyate cāsya tasmād bhedāgrahaḥ kutaḥ ।।
racanānupapattestanna sarvajñānumāgatam ।
acetanaṃ jagatkartṛ payo ambvādi ca nopamā ।।
etatpraśāstivacanāccetanācetanasya ca ।
dvaividhye apitu kāmādeḥ kutaḥ svāmitvamātmanaḥ ।।
sākṣādanubhavārūḍhaṃ śakyate apodituṃ kvacit ।
icchāsvāmitvamevoktamicchāvattvaṃ nacāparam ।।
kiñcit tadvaśagatve api svāmitvaṃ lokavad bhavet ।
sarvātmatantrakāmādeḥ kimutaiva pareśituḥ ।।
na cānubhavagaṃ kāmasvāmitvaṃ vedavāgapi ।
śaktāpavadituṃ tasmāt sā tadanyābhidhāyinī ।।
mokṣakāmo bhavedanyo yadi muktād bhaviṣyataḥ ।
mokṣakāmasya kiṃ tena svanāśārthaṃ ca ko yatet ।।
kartṛtvaṃ yasya tasyaiva bhoktṛtvamupalabhyate ।
vibhāge ca tayormānaṃ naiva kiñcit kvacid bhavet ।।
sarvamānavirodhaikadurdīkṣādīkṣitastvayam ।
māyāvādyupamāṃ yāyāt taccaśabdānnirākṛtaḥ ।।
sāṅkhayastu seśvaro brūte kṣetrānugrahaśaktimān ।
astīśvaraḥ svayambhātaḥ kleśakarmādivarjitaḥ ।।
kṣetraśaktimatī saiva prakṛtirbījaśaktimān ।
jīvaḥ parjanyavad daivaśaktimānīśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
pṛthivīvat pradhānaṃ tajjīvaḥ sannidhimātrataḥ ।
bījāvapanakartevetyatra prāha prabhuḥ svayam ।।
anyatra kāpi śaktirna svātantryeṇeśa eva hi ।
śaktīstāḥ prerayatyañjastadadhīnāśca sarvadā ।।
sattāpradhānapuruṣaśaktīnāṃ ca pratītayaḥ ।
pravṛttayaśca tāḥ sarvā nityaṃ nityātmanā yataḥ ।।
yathā nityatayā nityaṃ nityaśaktayā svayeśvaraḥ ।
niyāmayati nityaṃ ca na ṛte tvaditi śruteḥ ।।
svabhāvajīvakarmāṇi dravyaṃ kālaḥ śrutiḥ kriyāḥ ।
yatprasādādime santi na santi yadupekṣayā ।।
iti śruterna sattādyā api nārāyaṇaṃ vinā ।
tatpatañjalivindhyādimataṃ na puruṣārthadam ।।
cārvākairucyate mānamakṣajaṃ nāparaṃ kvacit ।
deha ātmā pumarthaśca kāmārthābhyāṃ vinā na hi ।।
yadevaṃ darśanenāsya ko arthaḥ pratyakṣagocaraḥ ।
labdhastenaiva hi naraiḥ śāstrāt kiṃ mohanaṃ vinā ।।
svaparārthavihīnatvāt svamatenaiva niṣphalam ।
kimityunmattavacchāstraṃ vṛthā pralapati svayam ।।
dehādanyo anubhavata ātmā bhāti śarīriṇām ।
mama deha iti vyaktaṃ mamārtha itivat sadā ।।
pratyakṣasyaiva mānatvamiti kenāvasīyate ।
yadi tatsādhakaṃ vedaprāmāṇye na kathaṃ bhavet ।।
na cānyāmānatā kvāpi pramāṇenāvasīyate ।
svamatenārtharahita upekṣyaḥ pakṣa īdṛśaḥ ।।
sannidhānāccetanasya vartate yadyacetanam ।
tathāpyabuddhipūrvatvāduktadoṣaḥ samo bhavet ।।
aṅgitvaṃ puruṣasyaiva sarvairapyanubhūyate ।
tadaṅgatvoktitaścaiva syāt sarvasyāpalāpakaḥ ।
kimu sarveśvarasyāsya hyapalāṣād yato akhilam ।।
aṅgitvaṃ yadi tasyaiva svātantryaṃ cennacākhilam ।
tatpreraṇe apyaśaktatvāt svatantro anyo hyapekṣitaḥ ।।
na ca svātantryamasyaiva pratyakṣādivirodhataḥ ।
hitākṛtyādidoṣācca bhadraṃ nānīśvaraṃ matam ।।
saṃsāriṇo anyaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvaśaktimanaupamam ।
cetanācetanasyāsya sattvādestadadhīnatām ।
nāṅgīkurvanti ye teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca samā ime ।।
tasmācchrutipramāṇena yuktibhiśca paro hariḥ ।
aṅgīkāyartamo nityaḥ sarvairapi suniścitam ।।
nityajñānaprayatnecchaṃ saṅkhayadyairapi pañcabhiḥ ।
yuktamīśaṃ vadantyanye tadicchādṛṣṭacoditāḥ ।
paramāṇavaścaturvargāḥ saṃyujyante dviśo akhilāḥ ।।
paramāṇudvayenaiva dvayaṇukaṃ nāma jāyate ।
dvayaṇukatrayeṇa tṛyaṇukaṃ taiścaturbhistadātmakam ।।
tatastvaniyamenaiva khaṇḍāvayavināṃ bhavaḥ ।
tataścāniyamenaiva sarvāvayavisambhavaḥ ।।
kāraṇaṃ samavāyyākhyaṃ paramāṇvādi tatra hi ।
īśecchādṛṣṭakālāstu nimittaṃ kāraṇaṃ matam ।।
sāmānyāntyaviśeṣau ca samavāyaśca tattrayam ।
nityaṃ kriyā anityāstu guṇadravye dvirūpake ।।
kārye guṇakriyāṇāṃ tu samavāyyanyakāraṇam ।
kāraṇasthā guṇādyāstu saṃyogo dravyakāraṇam ।।
evaṃ sthite api siddhānte viśeṣastatra kalpitaḥ ।
dvayaṇuke paramāṇau ca hrasvatvaṃ parimaṇḍalam ।।
na kāraṇaṃ kāryaguṇe vairūpyaṃ tatra kāraṇam ।
ityāhustānathovāca vidyādhīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।।
mahattvaṃ caiva dīrghatvaṃ tṛyaṇukādyeṣu kalpitam ।
tasmācca sadṛśaṃ kāryaṃ tatkāryeṣūpajāyate ।।
yathā tathaiva hrasvatvāt pārimāṇḍalyato api hi ।
jāyeta sadṛśaṃ kārye parimāṇaṃ samatvataḥ ।।
na cenmahattvataścaiva dīghartvādapi no bhavet ।
sadṛśasya hi kāryasya naiva yogaḥ kathañcana ।।
apratyakṣatvamevaṃ syād yataḥ kāryeṣvaṇutvataḥ ।
iti cenna mahattvaṃ ca paramāṇāvaṇāvapi ।
kathaṃ tṛyaṇukapūrveṣu nāṇutvamapi kathyate ।।
pratyakṣatvatadanyatve puruṣāpekṣayākhile ।
aṇutvaṃ ca mahattvaṃ ca yato vastuvyapekṣayā ।।
tāratamyasthitā yasmāt padārthāḥ sarva eva ca ।
yathā mahattvaviśrāntistathāṇutvasya ceṣyate ।।
parimāṇatvataścenna mahattvasyāpi viśramaḥ ।
dṛśyate ananta ityeva tathānantyamaṇāvapi ।।
na mahattatvaguṇata etāvāniti hīśvaraḥ ।
paricchinnastathāṇośca naitāvadbhāgatā kvacit ।।
viśrānto yadyanantāṃśaḥ kaścidastīti gamyate ।
nāvasāyayituṃ śakyo virodhādeva kevalam ।।
kevalaṃ sākṣimānena kālo deśo api nāntavān ।
aparyavasitiścāṇordṛśyate sakṣiṇā dvayoḥ ।।
yadi no sākṣigamyaṃ tanmahattvaṃ kena gamyate ।
viśrāntistāratamyena dṛśyate hyanumānataḥ ।।
yadyāgamādanantaṃ tanmahattvamavagamyate ।
anantameva cāṇutvaṃ kuto naivāvasīyate ।।
mahattvāṇutvayornaiva viśrāntirupalabhyate ।
anyadeva hyanantatvaṃ mahattvāṇutvayoḥ samam ।।
bahutvālpatvayoryadvat sāṅkhayāyāmupalabhyate ।
ānantyamekabhāgānāṃ tāvattvaṃ hyeva gaṇyate ।।
aṇīyāṃśca mahīyāṃśca bhagavānāgamoditaḥ ।
ānantyavācakaḥ śabdo dvidhānantye api mānatām ।।
yāti naiva guṇālpatvaṃ kālātpatvaṃ ca mānagam ।
sarvakālagatasyālpakāle api syādavasthitiḥ ।।
mahāguṇasya cālpo api guṇaḥ syāditi ced bhavet ।
tāvattvameva naiva syād deśe apyetanna no matam ।।
mahato alpatvamapi hi vyomavat prāha vedavit ।
yadyalpadeśasaṃsthānaṃ na sarvatrāpi no bhavet ।।
sthitasya hyalpadeśeṣu sarvagatvaṃ bhaved dhruvam ।
ekatrāpyanavasthasya kuta evākhilasthatā ।।
śūnyatvameva tasya syād yasyaikatrāpi na sthitiḥ ।
ato nāṇutvaviśrāntirna mahattvasya ca kvacit ।।
ubhayānantyayuk tasmād yadi mukhyamahad bhavet ।
tacca brahma paraṃ sākṣāt sarvānantyayutaṃ sadā ।।
yadi sākṣī svayambhāto na mānaṃ kena gamyate ।
akṣajādeśca mānatvamanavasthāthavā bhavet ।।
ataḥ sarvapadārthānāṃ bhāgāḥ santyeva sarvadā ।
sarvadikṣvapi sambandhādavibhāgaḥ parāṇutā ।।
tatsaṃyogādaniyatāt padārthānāṃ janirbhavet ।
dvayoreva tu saṃyoga iti kenāvasīyate ।।
kāraṇasya guṇāstena bhaveyuḥ kāryagā api ।
tāratamyena sarve api mahāntaścāṇavo yataḥ ।।
na ca tatproktasṛṣṭau tu mānaṃ kevalakalpanā ।
kathaṃ sākṣimitasyāsya śaknuyād vāraṇe kvacit ।।
yadi sākṣimitaṃ naitannānumā tatra vartate ।
pakṣīkartumaśakyatvāt kuta evānumā bhavet ।।
yatra nāsti padanyāsaḥ kastaṃ viṣayamāpnuyāt ।
deśāntarādiśabdaśca śaśaśṛṅgādiśabdavat ।।
sadṛśaṃ ca sajātīyaṃ nāsmatpakṣe kim eva hi ।
yenaiva ca prakāreṇātyasiddhamanumīyate ।
tenaiva śaśṛṅgādeḥ śakyamastitvakalpanam ।।
pratyakṣamāgamo vāpi bhaved yatra niyāmakaḥ ।
saiva vyāptirbhavenmānaṃ nānyā sandigdhamūlataḥ ।।
sahadarśanamātreṇa na vyāptiravasīyate ।
yadaivāvyatirekasya hyakṣajaṃ vāgamo bhavet ।
tannirdhāritayuktirvā vyāptiḥ saivāparā na hi ।।
anyathā saptamarasabhavo apyanumayā'patet ।
aniṣṭāni ca sarvāṇi hyanumā kāmacāriṇī ।।
kāryakāraṇayoścaiva guṇādeḥ pañcakasya ca ।
bhinnasyaiva tu sambandhaḥ samavāyo anya īryate ।।
bhinnatvasāmyatastasya tābhyāṃ yogo bhaved dhruvam ।
sa svanirvāhakaścet syād dravyameva tathā na kim ।।
viśeṣastadgatatvādiryadyabhinne avasīyate ।
guṇakriyādirūpasya niṣedhaḥ kena hetunā ।।
dravyameva tato anantaviśeṣātmatayā sadā ।
nānāvyavahṛterheturanantatvaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
viśeṣaśca viśeṣī saḥ svenaiva samavāyavat ।
kalpanāgurutādoṣāt padārthāntaratā na hi ।।
kalpayitvā ṣaṭ padārthān sābhāvānapi kevalam ।
ekasmin sa viśeṣaścet kiṃ pūrvaṃ tasya vismṛtiḥ ।।
yena pratyakṣasiddhena vyavahāro akhilo bhavet ।
bhāvābhāvavibhāgena yaṃ vinā na kathañcana ।।
abhedena pratītiśca kāryakāraṇapūrvake ।
abhāvānte padārthe asmin saviśeṣāvasīyate ।।
sāmānyādipadārtheṣu tanniṣṭhatvādayo akhilāḥ ।
kathaṃ dharmā nivāryante vastvaikye api hi vādibhiḥ ।।
kāryasya tattanniṣṭhatvaṃ guṇādervyāpitādikaḥ ।
kathaṃ viśeṣo naivāsti sa ca dharmo aparo yadi ।।
ṣaṭpadārthātirekaḥ syāt padārthāniyame api hi ।
dharmasya dharmasantānādanavasthākaro bhavet ।।
sāmānyasyāpi sāmānyaṃ guṇasyāpi guṇo hyataḥ ।
nāṅgīkṛtaḥ sa ca yadi nānavasthā kvacid bhavet ।।
asmatpakṣe guṇādyāśca tadvanto hi viśeṣataḥ ।
ananyatvānnānavasthā bhedo nāśe bhavet tathā ।।
viśeṣameva saṃśritya viśeṣo balavān yataḥ ।
dṛṣṭipramāṇataścaiva virodho darśane katham ।।
virodho hyavirodhaśca yato darśanamānagau ।
tato dṛṣṭe virodhastu sadbhirāpādyate katham ।।
abhinno bhagavān svena tadanyena vibhedavān ।
nityā dharmāstadīyāstu sarve asmānnaiva bhedinaḥ ।।
sāmastyocchedino anyatra dharmā ubhayarūpakāḥ ।
bhāve ta eva cocchedāt tadanye ca samastaśaḥ ।।
aṃśāṃśinorabhedena tvaṃśasaṃyoga eva hi ।
aṃśino nānavasthāto yadyapyaṃśeṣvaviśramaḥ ।।
ekasmin jāta evānyaḥ saṃyogo jāyate yadi ।
anavasthā tadaiva syāt saṃyogaikye bhavet kva sā ।।
aṃśe saṃyogadṛṣṭeśca dṛṣṭe kā sānavasthitiḥ ।
yadyaṃśago na saṃyogaḥ kāryeṣu prathimā katham ।।
paramāṇoraṇornāsti mahattetyadbhutaṃ vacaḥ ।
aṇūnāṃ prathimāpekṣāṃ vinaiva tṛyaṇuke api saḥ ।
paramāṇormahattvaṃ ca vinetyetad vacaḥ katham ।।
aṃśino aṃśairabhedo ayamaṃśena tu bhidābhidā ।
sarvapratyakṣaviṣayaḥ kathameva hyapohyate ।।
saṃyogaśca vibhāgaśca bhedaścaiva pṛthak pṛthak ।
anyonyapratiyogena hyubhayorapi dṛśyate ।।
bhinnā iti tu bhedānāṃ samudāyo hi dṛśyate ।
yathaiva ca padārthānāmanayorbheda ityapi ।।
ito amuṣyāmuto apyasya bhedo dṛṣṭo dvidharmikaḥ ।
tatraikavacanaṃ yattad viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ yathā ।।
naratvādikamapyevaṃ tattaddharmatayeyate ।
na sarvadharma eko asti samudāyastu bhinnagaḥ ।।
etādṛśaṃ ca sādṛśyaṃ padārtheṣu pṛthak pṛthak ।
ekasmin sa vinaṣṭe api yato anyatraiva dṛśyate ।।
kuto bhasmatvamāptasya naratvaṃ punariṣyate ।
ekatve nāsti mānaṃ ca śrutirapyāha sādaram ।।
bhinnāśca bhinnadharmāśca padārthā akhilā api ।
svaiḥ svairdharmairabhinnāśca svarūpairapi sarvaśaḥ ।।
anivṛttavināśāstu dharmā ubhayarūpakāḥ ।
na kenacidabhinno ato bhagavān svaguṇairvinā ।।
iti vyutpattirapi hi sādṛśyenaiva gamyate ।
sarveṣu yugapacchabdaḥ sadṛśeṣu pravartate ।।
tathāpi prāptitastvekavacanācca viśeṣataḥ ।
abhīṣyāvagatiśca syācchaktiḥ sādṛśyagā yataḥ ।।
tādṛśo ayaṃ ca tacchabda iti jñāpayati sphuṭam ।
jātitaścet kathaṃ tāsu tatra cedanavasthitiḥ ।।
tathaiva vyaktivijñānaṃ vyaktitvābhāvadūṣitam ।
yadi taccāsti tasyāpi viśeṣeṣvanavasthitiḥ ।।
kathaṃ svarūpatvamapi jñāyate anugataṃ yadi ।
ekavyutpattiparyantamanavasthādidūṣitam ।
kalpanāgauravāt tena yuktā nānugakalpanā ।।
aupādhikaviśiṣṭādyamapi tadvastu kiṃ tataḥ ।
anyat tadeva cedagnimattvaṃ kiṃ tatra bhaṇyate ।।
agnisaṃyogamātraṃ ced bhavet tat siddhasādhanam ।
bhūdharasyāgnisaṃyogo yadi ṣaṣṭhayartha eva kaḥ ।।
samavāyo yadi hy asya caikatvāt siddhasādhanam ।
yadyasyaupādhiko bhedaḥ kuta ekatvamiṣyate ।।
nānirvācyaṃ hi teneṣyamata aupādhikānyayoḥ ।
satyatvāt ko viśeṣaḥ syānmāyāvādyanyathā bhavet ।।
upādhijanyaṃ tadgamyamiti vaupādhikaṃ bhavet ।
ubhayatrāpyanantāḥ syuḥ samavāyā itastataḥ ।
bhinnatvaṃ caiva teṣvasti ko viśeṣa upādhige ।।
avidyamāna evānyaḥ samavāyo adhigamyate ।
upādhinā tadgamakamanumānaṃ na mā bhavet ।।
evamevāsataḥ sattasamavāyo janirmatā ।
tatrāpi hyuktadoṣāṇāṃ naiva kiñcinnivārakam ।।
asmatpakṣe viśeṣasya sarvatrāṅgīkṛtatvataḥ ।
nāsti doṣaḥ kvacid bhāvo hyabhāvaśca sa eva hi ।।
abhāvasya ca dharmāḥ syurbhāvāsteṣāṃ ca te akhilāḥ ।
pratyakṣamānataḥ sarvametanno vāraṇakṣamam ।
sarve bhāvā abhāvāśca padārthāstena sarvadā ।।
tathāpi prathamaṃ buddheryo niṣedhasya gocaraḥ ।
so abhāvo vidhibuddhestu gocaraḥ prathamaṃ paraḥ ।।
tasmāt pradhvastabhedādi sadityevāvagamyate ।
astyabhāvo asti ca dhvaṃso dehābhāvaśca bhasmatā ।।
ityādi yujyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣādipramāṇataḥ ।
anyonyābhāvabhedau ca pṛthaktavaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak ।।
yat kalpayanti taccaiva kalpanāgauravād gatam ।
paryāyatvena te śabdā jñāyante sarva eva hi ।।
bhedasya tu svarūpatve ye vadanti ca śūnyatām ।
adbhutatāste yato anyasya pratiyogitvamiṣyate ।।
pratiyogino hi bhedo ayaṃ natu svasmāt kathañcana ।
vibhāgenālpataiva syāt kuta eva ca śūnyatā ।।
na śūnyānāṃ hi saṃyogād bhāvo vastuna iṣyate ।
vidāraṇārtho dhātuśca vibhāgaguṇavācakaḥ ।।
avidāraṇe api hyāsyasya bhinnāvoṣṭhau tu tasya ca ।
ata unmattavākyatvānmāyāvādo abhyupekṣitaḥ ।।
na cāmandasadānandasyandyanantaguṇārṇavaḥ ।
īśvaro aṣṭaguṇatvena prameyo apramitatvataḥ ।।
mayyanantaguṇe anante guṇato anantavigrahe ।
anantaguṇamāhātmyaśaktijñānamahārṇavaḥ ।।
nārāyaṇaḥ paro aśeṣacetanebhyaḥ paraṃ padam ।
ityādivedatadvākyairanantaiścāvasīyate ।।
anantaguṇatā viṣṇoḥ kathameva hyapodyate ।
yadyanantaviśeṣāśca tajjñānādernivāritāḥ ।।
kathaṃ tattadviṣayatā sārvajñyārthaṃ vidhīyate ।
aupādhikaviśeṣastu pūrvameva nirākṛtaḥ ।।
svaprakāśatvamapi tu yairjñānasya nivāritam ।
kathaṃ sarvajñatā tasya svajñānādhigamaṃ vinā ।।
jñānaṃ viśvādhigaṃ tvekaṃ tajjñānaviṣayaṃ param ।
iti jñānadvayenaiva sarvavit parameśvaraḥ ।।
iti cedeṣa evārthastajjñānāvasito yadi ।
svaprakāśatvameva syājjñānaṃ hyetad viśeṣaṇam ।।
jñānāntareṇa cedatra bhavedevānavasthitiḥ ।
svaprakāśatvametasmād durnivāryaṃ samāpatet ।।
sukhavān duḥkhavāṃśca syāditi vyāptiśca no bhavet ।
nirduḥkhatvaṃ mahānandaḥ śrutyaiveśasya bhaṇyate ।।
yo aśanāyāpipāse ca śokādīṃścātivartate ।
ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvān vipāpmetyādikā ca sā ।।
īśvarasya tatheṣṭatvaṃ duḥkhitvopādhirityapi ।
ukte kimuttaraṃ brūyācchrutyanādaratatparaḥ ।।
nacātmaduḥkhitecchā syādata etannivāryate ।
sahadarśanamātreṇa śrutīnāmapalāpakaḥ ।।
yajñāder api pāpasya hetutvaṃ hiṃsayā yuteḥ ।
nānumāti kathaṃ tatra yadyupādhirniṣiddhatā ।।
aduḥkhitvena cānuktiḥ kathaṃ nopādhitāṃ vrajet ।
aduḥkhamitarat sarvaṃ jīvā eva tu duḥkhinaḥ ।
teṣāṃ duḥkhaprahāṇāya śrutireṣā pravartate ।।
iti śrutirhi paramā śrutyuktir yadi kāraṇam ।
kiṃ kāryamanumānena gaḷastanasamena hi ।।
anumānena yadyarthaḥ śrutidṛṣṭo vyapodyate ।
pūrvoktena prakāreṇa neśvaro dharma eva ca ।
syāt tatphalaṃ ca tenātra śrutireva pramā bhavet ।।
īśasyānumayā siddheḥ śrutirdhamirpramā bhavet ।
tayā sarvaguṇaiḥ pūrṇa ukta īśo yatastataḥ ।।
anānandānumā tasya dharmigrāhivirodhataḥ ।
na pramāṇaṃ bhavet tasmānnānumātropayoginī ।।
nityecchatvāt pareśasya paramāṇusadātvataḥ ।
adṛṣṭakālayoścaiva bhāvāt kāryaṃ sadā bhavet ।।
na hi kālavibhedo asti tatpakṣe asmanmate hareḥ ।
viśeṣakāla evaitatsṛṣṭayādīcchā sadātanā ।।
viśeṣāścaiva kālasya harericchāvaśāḥ sadā ।
sarve nimeṣā iti hi śrutirevāha sādaram ।।
udīrayati kālākhyaśaktimityasya vāgapi ।
kālasya kālagatvena na virodho api kaścana ।।
asaṅkhayātaviśeṣatvādicchāyā api sarvadā ।
īśo deśaś ca kālaś ca svagatā eva sarvadā ।।
īśādhīnau ca tau nityaṃ tadādhārau ca tadgatau ।
iti śrutirapi prāha kāle svoddiṣṭa eva tu ।।
tatkālasṛṣṭimevāto vāñchatīśaḥ sadaiva hi ।
syāt kālaḥ sa tadaiveti kālasya svagatatvataḥ ।।
svabhāvādeva hīcchaiṣā devasyaiva iti śruteḥ ।
svabhāvo api pareśecchāvaśa ityuditaḥ purā ।।
nityā anityāśca tatastadadhīnā iti śrutiḥ ।
rūpasparśādihetubhyaḥ paramāṇoranityatā ।।
anumeyā śrutīnāṃ ca viruddhatvānna tanmatam ।
upādeyamataścāyamaviruddhaḥ samanvayaḥ ।।
vaibhāṣikāśca sautrāntāḥ svarasakṣaṇikaṃ jagat ।
aṇūnāṃ samudāyaṃ ca kālakarmanimittataḥ ।।
utpattikāle yuktānāmātmānaṃ ca kṣaṇasthitim ।
nityaṃ santānameteṣāṃ pañcaskandhātmanā sthitam ।।
saṃskārarūpavijñānasañjñāduḥkhātmanā sthitiḥ ।
duḥkhābhāvaṃ sukhaṃ cāhurarūpajñānasantatim ।।
mokṣaṃ sa samudāyo hi naikasmādeva yujyate ।
nobhayoścobhayatvaṃ yat samudāyavyapekṣayā ।।
ato anyonyāśrayatvena samudāyo na yujyate ।
anyonyāpekṣayā puṃsaḥ samudāyatvavedanam ।।
syāt tatsadātanatve api tacca sāmīpyahetukam ।
iti cet kāryasambhūtimātravyāpṛtikāraṇam ।।
natu kāryaviśeṣeṣu vyāpṛtaṃ kāraṇaṃ bhavet ।
ato arthendriyasaṃyogirūpakāraṇatātmanaḥ ।
saṃyogirūparāhityānnaiva tajjñānatāpi hi ।।
viśaṣaṣakāryajanakaṃ yadi kāraṇamiṣyate ।
kutaḥ samānarūpatvaṃ kāryāṇāmapi sarvaśaḥ ।।
ato aniyatyā yatkiñcid yasya kasyāpi kāraṇam ।
adṛṣṭasyāpi tasyaiva viśeṣāpādakaṃ kutaḥ ।।
yasya kasyāpi yatkiñcid viśeṣamupapādayet ।
kāryaṃ ca kāraṇaṃ caiva yatkiñcid yasya kasyacit ।।
bhavenniyāmakābhāvādidamasyaiva kāraṇam ।
iti nityavināśitve kena mānena gamyate ।।
idaṃ na jāyate amuṣmādityatrāpi na kāraṇam ।
vināśotpattayaścaiva na dṛśyante sadātanāḥ ।।
dṛśyate pratyabhijñātaḥ sthiratvaṃ sarvavastuṣu ।
phalādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa sarvatrāpyanumīyate ।।
[NOTE jump in verse numbering, no lacuna in text!]
sattvena kṣaṇikatvaṃ cedākāśasyāviśeṣataḥ ।
aviśeṣo akhilasyāpi sattvāt kiṃ nānumīyate ।।
yadyākāśasya sattvaṃ na kuta eva narādiṣu ।
sadharmipratiyogitvamākāśasyāvagamyate ।।
tau vinā na hy abhāvaś ca kvaciddṛṣṭaḥ kadācana ।
adharmipratiyogitvamākāśasyāvagamyate ।।
svīkāratyāgato adṛṣṭadṛṣṭayoḥ sarvavastuṣu ।
guṇānunmatta evāsau vidadhātyadhikaṃ punaḥ ।।
uttarotpattimātreṇa vināśāt pūvarvastunaḥ ।
na saṃskārārpakatvaṃ ca yujyate kasyacit kvacit ।।
ato jñātaṃ mayetyādi na jñeyamanumā kutaḥ ।
ekatvamanubhūtisthaṃ tyaktavā nirmānakā bhidā ।
kuta ātmādikeṣu syād balyevānubhavo yataḥ ।।
kāryakāraṇayoścaikakālīnatvaṃ vinā katham ।
pūrvasaṃskārayogī syāduttaro niyamena ca ।।
sambaddha eva saṃskāramanyatrādattate akhilāḥ ।
asambaddhaḥ kathaṃ pūrva uttare vāsanākaraḥ ।।
ekakālatayā yogaṃ vinā saṃskārataḥ katham ।
kṣaṇamātramavasthānaṃ svīkṛtaṃ sarvavastuṣu ।।
pūrvamadhyāparakalārahitaḥ kṣaṇa iṣyate ।
pūrvabhāvabhavaṃ kāryamuta tannāśasambhavam ।।
yaugapadyaṃ sati bhavedutpādyānāmaśeṣataḥ ।
vināśe cenna tatkāryaṃ kāryotpattau ca kā pramā ।।
abhedena viśeṣeṇa dehadīpaphalādiṣu ।
viśeṣadarśanaṃ yuktamasmākamanubhūtitaḥ ।।
viśeṣadarśanaṃ mānaṃ yadi na sthairyadṛk kutaḥ ।
diksukhe ca khadṛṣṭāntād bhāvau saccet kvacid bhaved ।।
viśvaṃ pratyakṣagaṃ tyaktavā tayoryo anumitaṃ vadet ।
māyāvādivadevāsāvupekṣyo bhūtimicchatā ।।
sarvapramāṇasiddhaṃ yad buddherbhedena sarvadā ।
kathaṃ nu tasya buddhitvaṃ viśvamanyacca kimpramam ।।
sarvaloko bibhetyañjo yasmādanubhavāt sadā ।
tasyāpalāpinaḥ kiṃ na niṣpramāṇakavādinaḥ ।।
so ahaṃ tadidamevāhaṃ sukhī sad gaganaṃ diśaḥ ।
satyā ityādyanubhavāḥ sadā tatpratipakṣagāḥ ।।
ato nirmānamakhilapramāṇapratipakṣagam ।
durmataṃ ko nu gṛhṇīyād vināsuratatiṃ kvacit ।।
aparaḥ śūnyamakhilaṃ manovācāmagocaram ।
nirviśeṣaṃ svayambhātaṃ nirlepamajarāmaram ।।
aśeṣadoṣarahitamanantaṃ deśakālataḥ ।
vastutaśca tadasmīti nityopāsāparokṣitam ।
rāgādidoṣarahitaṃ tadbhāvaṃ yoginaṃ nayet ।।
tasyaivānādisaṃvṛttyā nānābhedātmakaṃ jagat ।
sadivābhāti satyatvaṃ sāṃvṛtaṃ tasya ceṣyate ।।
pāramārthikasattvaṃ tu śūnyādanyasya na kvacit ।
sāṃvṛtenaiva satyena vyavahāro akhilo bhavet ।।
śūnyāt saṃvṛtiyogena viśvametat pravartate ।
sṛṣṭikāle punaścānte stimitaṃ śūnyatāṃ vrajet ।
iti brūte tamuddiśya jagāda jagatāṃ guruḥ ।।
nāsato jagato bhāvo na hi dṛṣṭāsato janiḥ ।
sataḥ kvacit pramāṇaṃ ca dṛṣṭirevākhilād varam ।।
yadyevaṃ saptamarasānmadhurādiva pīnatā ।
bhavejjanasya mārjārṛṅgaṃ goriva ghātakam ।।
kāryārthī kāraṇaṃ sacca nopādadyāt kathañcana ।
na pravarteta ceṣyāya śūnyādeveṣyasambhavāt ।।
deśakālādiniyamo niṃha śūnyāt sato bhavet ।
puruṣecchānusāreṇa yadi kiñcit prajāyate ।।
kiṃ nānumīyate tadvad vastutvāt puruṣād bhavaḥ ।
sarvasyāpi nacābhāvo viśvaṃ saditi gamyate ।।
yato anubhavarodhe tu vacanaṃ vādinaḥ kutaḥ ।
svapnabhrāntivadevedaṃ saṃvṛttyaivopalabhyate ।।
yadi sattvena kiñcātra bhramo naiva nivartate ।
anāderasya viśvasya nivṛttiryadi ceṣyate ।
nivṛttiśca nivarteta tasyā bhrāntitvasambhavāt ।।
dṛṣṭasya bhrāntitā cet syādadṛṣṭe na bhramaḥ kutaḥ ।
gavāmaśṛṅgibhāvena na hi syācchaśaśṛṅgitā ।।
asmākaṃ tu pramāṇena prasādādīśvarasya ca ।
uktabhaṅgayā'gamānāṃ ca prāmāṇyād yujyate akhilam ।।
dṛśyatvād vimaṃta mithyā svapnavaccediyaṃ ca mā ।
mithyā cet sādhyasiddhirna vyabhicāro na ced bhavet ।।
sādhakatvamasatyasya sādhyaṃ vipratipattitaḥ ।
tasya cetyanavasthā syāt sattvaṃ cāsyānubhūtitaḥ ।।
anubhūtivirodhena mithyātve mā na kācana ।
atītānāgatau kālāvapi naḥ sākṣigocarau ।
tatsambandhitayā sattvamapi dṛṣṭasya sākṣigam ।।
dṛḍhadṛṣṭaṃ tu yad dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭābhāsastato aparam ।
bhrānteḥ saṃvṛtisatyasya viśeṣo avyabhicāravān ।
tenāpyaṅgīkṛtaḥ samyak sa naḥ satyatvameva hi ।।
vijñānād vyabhicāro asya kadācit syāditi pramā ।
naiva dṛṣṭā pramā sā ca na bhavet svavirodhataḥ ।।
bhedo viśeṣyadharmyādigrahaṇāpekṣayā yadi ।
anyonyāśrayatāhetordurgāhya iti yanna tat ।।
svarūpaṃ vastuno bhedo yanna tasya grahe grahaḥ ।
anyathāsyāmunā bheda iti vaktuṃ na yujyate ।।
agṛhīto yadā bhedastadā svasmāditi grahaḥ ।
syāt pratītivirodhācca na hi kaścit tathā vadet ।।
dharmitvapratiyogitvatadbhedā yugapad yadi ।
viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ ca tadbhāvaścaiva gṛhyate ।।
ko virodhaḥ svarūpeṇa gṛhīto bheda eva tu ।
asyāmuṣmāditi punarviśeṣeṇaiva gṛhyate ।।
kiñca bhedaḥ kathaṃ grāhya iti yaḥ paripṛcchati ।
dharmyādibhedagrahaṇāt tenokto anyonyasaṃśrayaḥ ।।
anyatvāgrahaṇe proktaḥ kathamanyonyasaṃśrayaḥ ।
anyatvaṃ yadi siddhaṃ syāt kathamanyonyasaṃśrayaḥ ।।
etādṛśasya vaktārāvubhau jātyuttarākarau ।
māyī mādhyamikaścaiva tadupekṣyau bubhūṣubhiḥ ।।
yacchūnyavādinaḥ śūnyaṃ tadeva brahma māyinaḥ ।
na hi lakṣaṇabhedo asti nirviśeṣatvatastayoḥ ।।
anṛtādivirodhitvamubhayośca svalakṣaṇam ।
svavākyābhāvasaṃvādānna kṛtyaṃ prativādinaḥ ।।
tatpakṣa iti vaidharmyānna svapnādivadityajaḥ ।
aprayatnānnirācakre ceti dṛṣṭiviruddhatām ।
niṣpramāṇatvamapyasya sūcayāmāsa viśvakṛt ।।
jñānamevaikamakhilajñeyākāraṃ prabhāsate ।
tatra santatibhedaśca svabhedo bheda eva ca ।
kalpitāḥ pratibhāsante nānāsaṃvṛtibhūmiṣu ।।
ityetadapi no yuktaṃ na hi jñānatayā jagat ।
bhāsate anubhavasyaiva viruddhatvādapeśalam ।।
tanmataṃ kṣaṇikatvācca jñānasya sthirarūpataḥ ।
jñeyasyoktaprakāreṇa sarvaśrutivirodhataḥ ।
anubhūtiviruddhatvādapi pakṣā ime aśivāḥ ।।
āha kṣapaṇako viśvaṃ sadasad dvayamadvayam ।
dvayādvayamatatsarvaṃ saptabhaṅgisadātanam ।।
naitat padārtha ekasmin yuktaṃ dṛṣṭivirodhataḥ ।
bhāvābhāvatayā viśvaṃ yena rūpeṇa mīyate ।
tadrūpameva taditi niyamaḥ kena vāryate ।।
tattaddoṣanivṛttyarthaṃ svīkṛtā tattadātmanā ।
yadi tairakhilairdeṣairlipyate caladarśanaḥ ।।
atihāya pramāṇāptaṃ niyamaṃ sadasattayā ।
aśeṣamāviruddhaṃ ca nirmānaṃ vyāhataṃ sadā ।।
sarvaprakāraṃ vadato dṛṣṭahāniramagrahaḥ ।
svavyāhatatvamityādyā doṣāḥ sarve bhavanti hi ।।
vakti svaprabhamātmānaṃ dehamānaṃ tadapyalam ।
duṣyaṃ nānāśarīreṣu praveśādanyathābhavāt ।।
anyathābhāvi yad vastu tadanityamiti sthitiḥ ।
tanmate tadanityatvaṃ pudgalasyānivāritam ।।
nānityatāsmatpakṣe tu caitanyāderviśeṣiṇaḥ ।
lakṣaṇasya nivṛttau tu syānna taccetane kvacit ।।
otaprotātmakatvaṃ tu paṭe dehe aṅgasaṃsthitiḥ ।
ityādilakṣaṇasyaiva nivṛttau syādanityatā ।।
bhautikaṃ tveva rūpādi vyāptaṃ nāśena no mate ।
naivaṃ tasyānyathābhāvo yasyānityatvamīritam ।।
rūpādiyuktasya tathā jagannāśitvasiddhaye ।
vyāptyā tayānyathābhāvādātmano anityatā bhavet ।।
nityordhvagatirapyeṣā yā muktiriti kathyate ।
alokākāśamāptasya kathaṃ na vikṛtiśca sā ।।
kīdṛśaścānyathābhāvo nāśahetutayeṣyate ।
saṃsthānāpagamaścet sa na hi bhūsāgarādiṣu ।।
yaḥ kaścidanyathābhāvo yadi muktiśca tādṛśī ।
dehamāne vikāraḥ syāditi sthāsnūnanātmanaḥ ।।
āha hastyādideheṣu hyapi syādanyathābhāvaḥ ।
aṇudehasya jīvasya gajatve vikṛtirhi yā ।
dehavyāptyai viśeṣaḥ kastasyāḥ sthāsnutanau ca nuḥ ।।
gītāt puṣpaphalāvāptiḥ sparśāt kārśyaṃ rasāt sthitiḥ ।
api vṛkṣasya dṛśyanta iti nānātmatā bhavet ।
evañcātmākārtsnyamiti tata evāha vedavit ।।
sarvajñatvādikaiḥ sarvairguṇairyuktaṃ sadāśivam ।
jagadvicitraracanākartāraṃ doṣavarjitam ।।
āhuḥ pāśupatāstacca bahuśrutivirodhataḥ ।
nopādeyaṃ mataṃ hyasya devasya stuhi gartagam ।।
utpipeṣa śirastasya gṛṇīṣe satpatiṃ padam ।
yad viṣṇorupamaṃ hantuṃ rudramākṛṣṭate mayā ।।
dhanuryaṃ kāmaye taṃ tamugraṃ mā śiśnadevatāḥ ।
ghnañchiśnadevāneko asāvāsīnnārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ।।
tasmād rudraḥ samprasādaścābhūtāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ makham ।
yajñena yajñamayajantābadhnan puruṣaṃ paśum ।।
yo bhūtānāmadhipatī rudrastanticaro vṛṣā ।
ityādiśrutisāmarthyāt pāratantryaṃ janirmṛtiḥ ।।
parādhīnaparaprāptirajñatvaṃ praḷaye abhavaḥ ।
pratīyante sadoṣatvānneśaḥ paśupatistataḥ ।।
aśarīratvatastasya sambandho jagatā kvacit ।
kartṛtvena na yujyeta dehino jñānadṛṣṭitaḥ ।।
na ca dehādivad viśvamasya syād bhogasambhavāt ।
adhiṣṭhāne sthitaḥ kartā kāryaṃ kurvan pratīyate ।
nāsyādhiṣṭhānayogo asti bhūtānāṃ praḷaye tadā ।।
adehaścedasārvajñaḥ śilākāṣṭhādivat sadā ।
dehī cedantavāneva yajñadattanidarśanāt ।।
nacaitadakhilaṃ viṣṇau śrutiprāmāṇyagauravāt ।
manobuddhayaṅgitāṃ viṣṇorlakṣayāmo ya eva saḥ ।।
sa eva deho vijñānamaiśvaryaṃ śaktirūrjitā ।
deho viṣṇorna te viṣṇo vāsudevo agrato abhavat ।।
eko nārāyaṇastvāsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ ।
ajasya nābhāvadhyekamarpitaṃ mātrayā paraḥ ।।
saddehaḥ sukhagandhaśca jñānabhāḥ satparākramaḥ ।
jñānajñānaḥ sukhasukhaḥ sa viṣṇuḥ paramākṣaraḥ ।।
ānanda eka evāgra āsīnnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।
priyaṃ tasya śire modapramodau ca bhujau hareḥ ।।
ānando madhyato brahma pucchaṃ nānyadabhūt kvacit ।
manaso asyābhavad brahmā lalāṭādapi śaṅkaraḥ ।।
pakṣayorgaruḍaḥ śeṣo mukhādāsa sarasvatī ।
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।।
ityādiśrutisandarbhabalānnityaguṇātmanaḥ ।
viṣṇordehājjagat sarvamāvirāsīditīyate ।।
mānavattvād virodhaḥ ko nāmānaṃ kvacidiṣyate ।
avirodho virodhaśca mānenaiva hi gamyate ।।
ata uktaṃ samastaṃ ca vāsudevasya yujyate ।
śivādināmayuktāśca śrutayo viṣṇuvācakāḥ ।।
nāmāni sarvāṇi ca yameko yo devanāmadhāḥ ।
viṣṇunāmāni nānyasya sarvanāmā hariḥ svayam ।।
na nārāyaṇanāmāni tadanyeṣvapare harau ।
ityādiśrutayastatra mānaṃ coktaḥ samanvayaḥ ।।
purāṇāni purāṇādyairviruddhatvānna tat pramā ।
tadviruddheṣu no mānaṃ pūrvāparavirodhataḥ ।।
samabrāhmavirodhācca niyamād vaiṣṇaveṣvapi ।
mohārthamuktitaścaiva viṣṇureko guṇārṇavaḥ ।।
skandasūryagaṇeśādimatāni nyāyato amutaḥ ।
nirākṛtānyaśeṣeṇa siddhāntasyāviśeṣataḥ ।।
nirākṛtau viśeṣasya bhāvācchaktimataṃ pṛthak ।
dūṣyate mahatī devī hrīṅkarī sarvakāraṇam ।
tripurābhairavītyādināmabhiḥ sābhidhīyate ।।
tasyāḥ sadāśivādyāśca jāyante devamānuṣāḥ ।
bhūtabhautikamapyetaditi tannopapadyate ।।
dṛṣṭā pumbhyaḥ sadā sṛṣṭiḥ strīpumbhyo vā viśeṣataḥ ।
kevalābhyo na hi strībhyastata utpattyasambhavāt ।।
nārcyaṃ mahāvāmamataṃ vāmairanyadudīryate ।
śivopasarjanā śaktiḥ sasarjedaṃ samantataḥ ।।
iti taccopapannaṃ na śivasyākaraṇatvataḥ ।
adehatvādapi hyanye brūyuḥ sarvajñamīśvaram ।।
aṇuvāmā na tadyuktamīśavādapraveśanāt ।
sārvajñyādiguṇairyuktaṃ gurukalpanayā dvayam ।।
na yujyate hyatastvīśa eka eva prayojakaḥ ।
uktadoṣaśca tatpakṣa iti naivātra dūṣyate ।।
śrutismṛtītihāsānāṃ sāmastyena virodhataḥ ।
satāṃ jugupsitatvācca nāṅgīkāryaṃ hi tanmatam ।।
pañcarātraniṣedhārthametānyācakṣate yadi ।
sūtrāṇyativiruddhaṃ tad yata āha sa bhārate ।।
pañcarātrasya kṛtsnasya vaktā nārāyaṇaḥ svayam ।
jñāneṣveteṣu rājendra sarveṣvetad viśiṣṭate ।।
pañcarātravido ye tu yathākramaparā nṛpa ।
ekāntabhāvopagatā vāsudevaṃ viśanti te ।।
iti gītā ca tacchāstrasaṅkṣepa iti hīritam ।
