vedena pañcarātreṇa bhaktayā yajñena caiva hi ।।
dṛśyo ahaṃ nānyathā dṛśyo varṣakoṭiśatairapi ।
iti vārāhavacanaṃ ślokā iti vacaḥ śrutau ।।
vedaiśca pañcarātraiśca dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ।
pañcarātraṃ ca vedāśca vidyaikaiva dvidheyate ।।
ityādivedavacanaiḥ pañcarātramapodyate ।
kathamevātra doṣaḥ ka utpattirjño ata ityapi ।।
ihaivoktā nacābhūtabhāvastatrāpi kathyate ।
anādikarmaṇā baddho jīvaḥ saṃsāramaṇḍale ।।
vāsudevecchayā nityaṃ bhramatīti hi tadvacaḥ ।
na hi saṃsārasāditvaṃ pañcarātroditaṃ kvacit ।।
jīvābhimāniśeṣasya nāmnā saṅkarṣaṇasya tu ।
vāsudevājjaniḥ proktā pradyumnasya tatastathā ।।
mano abhimāninaḥ kāmasyaivaṃ sākṣāddhareḥ kvacit ।
saṅkarṣaṇādināmnaiva nityācintyoruśaktitaḥ ।
vyūha ukto anyathānūdya kathaṃ duṣṭatvamucyate ।।
yadi vidyāccaturvedānitivad vedapūraṇam ।
pañcarātrāditi kuto dveṣaḥ śāṇḍilyavartane ।।
ataḥ paramaśāstrorudveṣāduditamāsuraiḥ ।
dūṣaṇaṃ pañcarātrasya vīkṣāyāmapi na kṣamam ।।
ato aśeṣajagaddhātā nirdoṣoruguṇārṇavaḥ ।
nārāyaṇaḥ śrutigaṇatātparyādavasīyate ।।
andhaṃ tamaḥ praviśanti ye tvavidyāmupāsate ।
tato bhūya ivāpsyanti ye tasyā naiva nindakāḥ ।।
tato vidyāmavidyāṃ ca yo jānātyubhayaṃ saha ।
doṣajñānādatītyaitān vidyayāmṛtamaśnute ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

athāśeṣasamāmnāyavirodhāpākṛtiṃ prabhuḥ ।
kariṣyannadhidaivādhibhūtajīvaparātmanām ।।
svarūpanirṇayāyaiva vacanānāṃ parasparam ।
pādenānenāvirodhaṃ darśayatyamitadyutiḥ ।।
anubhūtiyuktibahuvāgvailomyaṃ ca tato adhikam ।
etat sarvaṃ sataḥ sāmyaṃ dvāravaiyarthyameva ca ।।
dṛṣṭayuktayanusāritvamuktānyārthāvirodhataḥ ।
prasiddhanāmasvīkāre bahuvākyānuvatirtā ।।
lokadṛṣṭānusāritvaṃ jīvasāmyamanāditā ।
tatra tatra parijñānaṃ guṇasāmyaśrutī tathā ।।
utpattimattvaṃ svaguṇānanubhūtyalpakalpane ।
nānāśrutiśca vaicitṛyaṃ yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣagāḥ ।।
vyavasthānupapattiśca svātantryamanusāritā ।
mukhyatā śaktimattvaṃ ca vairūpyaṃ sarvasaṅgrahaḥ ।।
gatyādirīśaśaktiśca sarvamānavirodhitā ।
abhīṣyāsiddhisuvyaktī śāstrasiddhivirparyayaḥ ।
viśeṣakāraṇaṃ ceti siddhāntasyaiva sādhakāḥ ।।
prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālo devāstadabhimāninaḥ ।
mahadādyāśca jāyante parādhīnaviśeṣitā ।
idaṃ sarvaṃ sasarjeti janimattvamihoditam ।।
avakāśamātramākāśaḥ kathamutpadyate anyathā ।
yadyanākāśatā pūrvaṃ kiṃ mūrtanibiḍaṃ jagat ।।
mūtarsampūrṇatā caiva yadyanākāśatā bhavet ।
mūrtadravyāṇi cākāśe sthitānyeva hi sarvadā ।।
ata ākāśaśabdoktastaddevo atra vināyakaḥ ।
dehotpattyā samutpanna iti śrutyābhidhīyate ।।
bhūtamapyasitaṃ divyadṛṣṭigocarameva tu ।
utpadyate avyākṛtaṃ hi gaganaṃ sākṣigocaram ।
pradeśa iti vijñeyaṃ nityaṃ notpadyate hi tat ।।
tathāpi pūrvasambandhaparatantraviśeṣayuk ।
khamevotpattimannāma śrutiśabdavivakṣitam ।।
prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kāla ityete ca samastaśaḥ ।
īśādhīnaviśeṣeṇa janyā ityeva kīrtitāḥ ।।
kālapravāha evaiko nityo natu viśeṣavān ।
puruṣāvyaktakālānāṃ ramaivaikābhimāninī ।।
sisṛkṣutvaviśeṣaṃ tat sākṣād bhagavadicchayā ।
prāptaiva sṛṣṭetyuditā pradhānaṃ vikṛterapi ।।
pumāṃso dehasambandhāt sṛṣṭimanta itīritāḥ ।
evaṃ praḷayakāle api pratibhātaparāvaraḥ ।।
mukhyāvāyurnityasamaḥ śarīrotpattikāraṇāt ।
parādhīnaviśeṣeṇa janimāneva śabditaḥ ।।
naiva kiñcit tato janmavarjitaṃ paramādṛte ।
parādhīnaviśeṣatve janmanaḥ sthūlatābhavaḥ ।।
pūrvaśabdavilopaśca yadi janmeti kīrtyate ।
ramāyā naiva janmāsti caitanyasyāpi kevalam ।।
pradhanasya ca vedasya vedasyāpīśvarecchayā ।
vyaktirnāma viśeṣo asti tasmāt tadvaśataiva hi ।।
utpattiratra kathitā svatantratvāt parātmanaḥ ।
naivotpattiḥ kathamapi na svatantraṃ tato aparam ।।
acchedyasyāpi jīvasya vibhāgaṃ bahudhā hariḥ ।
kṛtvā bhogān pradāyaiva caikyamāpādayet punaḥ ।।
ata īśavaśaṃ sarvaṃ cetanācetanaṃ jagat ।
avibhāgaṃ vibhāgāya yadā nayati keśavaḥ ।
kimaśakyaṃ pareśasya tadeti hyabhidhīyate ।।
evaṃ sthite api jīvaikyaṃ kecidāhuḥ parātmanā ।
tad yo ahamitipūrvābhiḥ śrutibhiścānumābalāt ।।
na tad yuktaṃ yato viṣṇuḥ pṛthagevābhidhīyate ।
prajñānetro aloka iti muktau bhedo abhidhīyate ।
etamānandamityanyā paramaṃ sāmyamityapi ।।
idaṃ jñānamapāśritya mama sādharmyamāgatāḥ ।
sarge api nopajāyante praḷaye na vyathanti ca ।।
upasampadya tajjyotiḥ svarūpeṇābhipadyate ।
tatra paryeti jakṣaṃśca krīḍannapi sadā sukhī ।।
ācakṣva me mokṣaṃ dhīrā yaṃ pravadanti tam ।
ityakta āha vāgdevī paraṃ mokṣaṃ prajāpateḥ ।।
śākhāṃ śākhāṃ mahānadyaḥ saṃyānti paritaḥsravāḥ ।
dhānāpūpā māṃsakāmāḥ sadā pāyasakardamāḥ ।।
yasminnagnimukhā devāḥ sendrāḥ sahamarudgaṇāḥ ।
ījire kratubhiḥ śreṣṭhaistadakṣaramupāsate ।।
praviśanti paraṃ devaṃ muktāstatraiva bhoginaḥ ।
nirgacchanti yathākāmaṃ pareśenaiva coditāḥ ।।
bhedadṛṣṭayābhimānena niḥsaṅgenāpi kamarṇā ।
kartṛtvāt saguṇaṃ brahma puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabham ।।
sa saṅgatya punaḥ kāle kāleneśvaramūrtitā ।
jāte aguṇavyatikare yathāpūrvaṃ prajāyate ।।
ṛcāṃ tvaḥ poṣamāste ca pareṇa preritāḥ sadā ।
yatkāmastat sṛjatyaddhaiṣātmanā tat sṛjatyapi ।।
sahaiva brahmaṇā kāmān bhuṅkate nistīrṇatadguṇaḥ ।
duḥkhādīṃśca parityajya jagadvayāpāravarjitaḥ ।।
bhuṅkte bhogān sahaivoccānityādyāgamamānataḥ ।
muktasya bhedāvagateḥ kathameva hyabhinnatā ।।
jīveśayornānumā ca tadabhedaṃ pramāpayet ।
mithyaiva bhedo vimato bhedatvāccandrabhedavat ।
iti cet sādhyadharmo ayaṃ sannasan vā navobhayam ।।
yadi sannapasiddhāntaḥ sa evāsannitīrite ।
nobhayaṃ cenna siddhaṃ taditi mānasya dūṣaṇam ।।
na ca mānāntareṇaitacchakyaṃ sādhayituṃ kvacit ।
anumānena cet saiva hyanavasthā bhaviṣyati ।।
nacāgamastadartho asti nāsadāsīnna tad vadet ।
pariśeṣādanirvācyaṃ yadi siddhayet parātmanaḥ ।।
anirvācyatvameva syāt pariśiṣṭo hyasau tadā ।
nacānya āgamastatra sadasatpratiyogini ।।
na ca pratyakṣamātrāsti nacārthāpattiriṣyate ।
bādhāyogāt sata iti bādhābhāvata eva hi ।।
viṣayasya kuto bādho vidyamānaṃ hi bādhyate ।
na hi vandhyāsuto vadhyo yajñadatto hi vadhyate ।।
bādhāyogaḥ sata iti vyāptireṣā kva dṛśyate ।
kaścāyaṃ bādha uddiṣṭo na hi nāśo asato bhavet ।
nivṛttiścāpravṛttasya kathamevopapadyate ।।
nāsīdasti bhaviṣyacca taditi jñānameyatā ।
yadi bādhastadāsattvaṃ tenaivāṅgīkṛtaṃ punaḥ ।।
pratītirnāsata iti vadannaṅgīkaroti tām ।
niṣedho hyapratītasya kathañcinnopapadyate ।।
na copamā bhavedatra pratyakṣāt sattvameva ca ।
śāstragamyapareśānād bhedaḥ svātmana īyate ।।
anubhūtivirodhena kathamekatvamucyate ।
kiñcitkartā ca duḥkhīti sarvairevānubhūyate ।।
sarvajño bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvaśaktiriti śrutaḥ ।
anubhūtāddhi bhedena śrutireṣā vadatyamum ।।
upajīvyaviruddhaṃ tu kathamaikyaṃ śrutirvadet ।
aprāmāṇyaṃ yadā bhedavācakasya bhaviṣyati ।।
sa eva dharmiṇo grāhī tadabhedaḥ kathaṃ bhavet ।
yat svarūpagrahe mānaṃ taddharme na kathaṃ bhavet ।।
ekavijñānavijñaptyā dvayaṃ mānaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
na cedekamamānaṃ tad dvayamapyatra no bhavet ।।
dharmigrāhivirodhastu tasmānmānasya dūṣaṇam ।
nopajīvyo hyabhedo atra kvacid bhedaśruterbalāt ।।
na ca mānāntaropeyaṃ brahma tad bhavati kvacit ।
yena mānena cāpeyaṃ bhedastenāvagamyate ।।
sarvajñānamayaiveśo yadyupeyaḥ kathañcana ।
sarvajñathvaguṇenaiva tayā bhedo avagamyate ।।
na duḥkhānubhavaḥ kvāpi mithyānubhavatāṃ vrajet ।
na hi bādhaḥ kvacid dṛṣṭo duḥkhādyanubhavasya tu ।।
yadi duḥkhānubhūtiśca bhrāntirityavasīyate ।
aduḥkhitāśrutiḥ kena na bhrāntiriti gamyate ।।
śrutisvarūpamarthaśca mānenaivāvasīyate ।
taccenmānaṃ gṛhītaṃ te kiṃ duḥkhānubhave bhramaḥ ।।
na ca bādhaviśeṣo asti yadabādhitameva tat ।
bādho yadyanubhūte arthe kathaṃ nirṇaya īyate ।।
ko api hy artho na niścetuṃ śakyate bhramavādinā ।
bhramatvamabhramatvaṃ ca yadaivānubhavopagam ।
ekasya bhramatā tatra parasyābhramatā kutaḥ ।।
bhramatvamabhramatvaṃ ca sarvaṃ vedyaṃ hi sākṣiṇā ।
sa cet sākṣī kvacid duṣyaḥ kathaṃ nirṇaya īyate ।।
viśeṣā sarva evaite sākṣipratyayagocarāḥ ।
ūrīkṛtya ca tān sarvān vyavahāraḥ pravartate ।
sākṣiṇo vyavasāyī tu vyavahāro abhidhīyate ।।
tasmāt sarvaprasiddhasya vyavahārasya siddhaye ।
sākṣī nirdoṣa evaikaḥ sadāṅgīkārya eva naḥ ।।
śuddhaḥ sākṣī yadā siddho duḥkhitvaṃ vāryate katham ।
upajīvyapramāṇaṃ tad bhedagrāhakameva hi ।
ato jīveśayorbhedaḥ śrutisāmarthyasusthiraḥ ।।
tathāpi tu cidānandapūrvāstatsadṛśā guṇāḥ ।
sārasvarūpamasyāpi muktāvapyavaśiṣyate ।।
ato abhedavadevaitāḥ śrutayaḥ pravadanti hi ।
paurāṇāni ca vākyāni sādṛśyābhedasaṃśrayāt ।।
sādṛśyācca pradhānatvāt svātantryādapicābhidām ।
āhurīśena jīvasya na svarūpābhidāṃ kvacit ।।
sthānaikyamaikamatyaṃ ca muktasya tu viśiṣṭate ।
sādṛśyaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa jaḍānāṃ dvayameva tu ।
bhavet sādṛśyamatyalpaṃ tṛtīyaṃ paramātmanā ।।
īśarūpakriyāṇāṃ ca guṇānāmapi sarvaśaḥ ।
tathaivāvayavānāṃ tatsvarūpaikyaṃ tu mukhyataḥ ।।
yathodakaṃ durge vṛṣṭaṃ parvateṣu vidhāvati ।
evaṃ dharmān pṛthak paśyaṃstānevānuvidhāvati ।
iti śruternobhayaṃ ca bhedābhedākhyamiṣyate ।।
ekamevādvitīyaṃ neha nānāsti kiñcana ।
mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpnoti ya iha nāneva paśyati ।।
iti śrutāvivetyasmād bhedābhedanirākṛtiḥ ।
ivobhaye ca sādṛśya iti vāk śabdanirṇaye ।।
bhedasya muktau vacanādapi tatpakṣanigrahaḥ ।
cetanatvādisādṛśyaṃ yadyabheda itīṣyate ।
aṅgīkṛtaṃ tadasmābhirna svarūpaikatā kvacit ।।
na kenacidabhedo asti bhedābhedo apivā kvacit ।
samudāyamṛte viṣṇoḥ svaguṇādīn vināpi vā ।।
iti śruterna tasyāsti bhedābhedo api kenacit ।
abhedaśrutayo' ṃśatvāt sādṛśyaṃ cāṃśatāsya tu ।।
aṃśastu dvividho jñeyaḥ svarūpāṃśo anya eva ca ।
vibhinnāṃśo alpaśaktiḥ syāt kiñcitsādṛśyamātrayuk ।।
aṃśino yattu sāmarthyaṃ yat svarūpaṃ yathā sthitiḥ ।
sa eva cet svarūpāṃśaḥ prādurbhāvā hareryathā ।।
sūryamaṇḍalamānyekastatprakāśābhimānavān ।
sūryo atha saptamābdheśca bāhyodasya ca vāripaḥ ।।
kaṭhinatvena mervādeḥ pṛthivyā api devatā ।
dharādevyevamevaiko bhagavān viṣṇuravyayaḥ ।
nānāvatārarūpeṇa sthitaḥ pūrṇaguṇaḥ sadā ।।
viṇmūtrākṣyādimāninyo yathāpabhraṣṭadevatāḥ ।
sūryādibhyastathaivāyaṃ saṃsārī paramāt pṛthak ।।
dehadoṣaiśca duṣṭatvādapabhraṣṭākhyadevatāḥ ।
anyāḥ sūryādidevebhyo hyanugrāhyāśca taiḥ sadā ।।
evameva parād viṣṇoḥ pṛthak saṃsāriṇo matāḥ ।
anugrāhyāśca tenaiva tatprasādācca mokṣiṇaḥ ।।
na tu matsyādirūpāṇāmanugrāhyatvamiṣyate ।
guṇairaśeṣaiḥ pūrṇatvānmukhyābhedo aparairnaca ।।
aṃśābhāsāśca sarve api parasyāṃśā na mukhyataḥ ।
yathaiṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasminnetadātatam ।।
na tu pumpādavat pādā jīvā ete parātmanaḥ ।
pūrṇāstasya guṇā eva prādurbhāvatayā sthitāḥ ।
evaṃ jagāda paramaśrutirnārāyaṇaṃ param ।।
akṣayo bhagavān viṣṇurlakṣmyāvāso laye sthitaḥ ।
muktaiḥ sadā cintyamāno brahmādyaistāratamyagaiḥ ।।
prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālo vedāśceti catuṣyayam ।
nityaṃ svarūpato viṣṇorviśeṣāvāptimātrataḥ ।
utpattimāditi proktaṃ lakṣmīstadabhimāninī ।।
tato jātaḥ pumān nāma brahmāsyāṃ vāsudevataḥ ।
sūtrātmā prāṇanāmā ca devyau prakṛtimāninī ।।
tato rūpaṃ mahān nāma brahmaṇo ahaṅkṛtiḥ śivaḥ ।
brahmaṇo buddhināmnomā tata indro mano abhidhaḥ ।
skandaśca tata evānye sarve devāḥ prajajñire ।।
tatra pūrvatanaḥ śreyān guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ samastaśaḥ ।
tebhyaśca bhagavān viṣṇustadadhīnā ime sadā ।।
janmasthitilayājñānaniyatijñānasaṃsṛtiḥ ।
mokṣaśca tadadhīnatvameteṣāṃ naiva hīyate ।।
muktāvapi sa evaikaḥ svatantraḥ pūrṇasadguṇaḥ ।
iti śrutyupapattibhyāṃ pāde asmin prabhuṇoditam ।।

।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

śrutyarthaḥ śrutiyuktibhyāṃ viruddha iva dṛśyate ।
yatra tannirṇayaṃ devaḥ suviśiṣṭopapattibhiḥ ।
karotyanena pādena tatra spaṣṭārthavacchrutiḥ ।।
viśeṣaśrutivairūpyaṃ māhātmyaṃ vyaktasadguṇāḥ ।
dṛṣṭāyuktiḥ samānatvaṃ kartṛśaktirvimiśratā ।।
yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣeṣu sunirṇītāsatu tādṛśāḥ ।
yuktayo nirṇayasyaiva svayaṃ bhagavatoditāḥ ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ ।।

svābhāvikānyathānāmasahābhāvānyathoktayaḥ ।
aviśeṣo viśeṣau ca sahabhāvo vimiśratā ।।
viruddhoktiḥ sahasthānaṃ vaiyarthyaṃ cānyathāgatiḥ ।
yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣasya guṇādhikyārthatobhavau ।।
upapattirdvirūpatvamādhikyamanurūpatā ।
yogyatā prabalatvaṃ ca vibhāgaḥ kāraṇābhavaḥ ।
kḷptiranyāgatiścaiva siddhāntasyaiva sādhakāḥ ।।
bījāpūruṣayonīnāṃ saṅgātiniyamojkhitim ।
athaśabdena bhagavānāha kāraṇataśca tām ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।

paścādadṛṣṭayavijñānakāladuḥkhapṛthagbhavāḥ ।
sthānabhedo viruddhatvaṃ nyāyasāmyaṃ svatobhavaḥ ।।
guṇasāmyamayogaśca tarkabādho vilomatā ।
nānābhāvaḥ pralobhaśca pūrvapakṣagāḥ ।।
aśakyakartṛtāśaktiḥ svato abodhastadeva ca ।
amānakḷptisanmānavyavasthātyalpatābhavāḥ ।।
viśeṣadṛṣṭivākye ca puṃśaktiḥ sunidarśanam ।
alaukikatvamādhikyaṃ svātantryaṃ nirṇayapramāḥ ।।
vāsanāḥ sarvavastūnāmanādyanubhavāgatāḥ ।
santyevāśeṣajīvānāmanādimanasi sthitāḥ ।।
triguṇātmakaṃ mano astyeva yāvanmuktiḥ sadātanam ।
tatraivāśeṣasaṃskārāḥ sañcīyante sadaiva ca ।।
sūkṣmatvena laye sacca prākṛtairupacīyate ।
sṛṣṭikāle yadā tanna kutaḥ saṃsārasaṃsthitiḥ ।।
saṃskārairbhagavāneva sṛṣṭvā nānāvidhaṃ jagat ।
svapnakāle darśayati bhrāntirjāgrattvameva hi ।।
adṛṣṭe cāśrute bhāve na bhāva upajāyate ।
adṛṣṭādaśrutād bhāvānna bhāva upajāyate ।।
iti śrutipurāṇoktiranāditvāttu yujyate ।
kadācid darśanāyogyaṃ yat tatrāpi vibhāgataḥ ।।
dṛṣṭaṃ samānādhikaraṇaṃ dṛśyate ca sa ca bhramaḥ ।
vāsanāmātramūlatvājjāgradvat spaṣṭatā na ca ।।
bhedo abhedo athavā dvandvamiti praśno na yujyate ।
draṣṭuḥ svapnasya dṛṣṭatvād bhedasyaivākhilairjanaiḥ ।।
praśnadoṣā hi catvāraḥ svavyāhatirasaṅgatiḥ ।
siddhārthatā ca vaiphalyaṃ na taiḥ syāt tattvanirṇayaḥ ।।
tattvanirṇayavailomyaṃ syād vāde api hi nigrahaḥ ।
udbhāvanīyameva syānna kathāvasitirbhavet ।।
vijigīṣukathāyāṃ tu kathāvasitikāraṇam ।
parihāre api siddhatvaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ ।
pratijñāyāṃ tadanyasya siddhataiva hi sādhakā ।।
āśrayavyāśrayāsiddhī sādhyasiddhiśca dūṣaṇam ।
keṣāñcin na ca te doṣā vyāptau satyāṃ kathañcana ।।
doṣo vyāhatirevāsti nṛśṛṅgāstitvasādhane ।
yatra vyāhatatā nāsti ko atisaṅgo asya sādhane ।।
pratyakṣāgamamūlāstu nyāyāḥ sarve bhavanti hi ।
nyāyābhāsā amūlāḥ syurnyāyasyānyasya tau punaḥ ।।
adṛṣṭe vyabhicāre tu sādhakaṃ taditi sphuṭam ।
jñāyate sākṣiṇaivādvā mānabādhe na tad bhavet ।।
yat sākṣiṇaiva mānatvaṃ mānānāmavasīyate ।
amānasya tu mānatvaṃ mānasatvāccalaṃ bhavet ।।
utsargato api yat prāptamapavādavivarjitam ।
vyabhicāryapavādena mānameva bhaviṣyati ।।
ato hi bhojanādīnāmiṣṭasādhanatānumā ।
mānaṃ vyavahṛtau nityaṃ vyabhicāro hi tatra ca ।।
vyāptatve vyāśrayatvaṃ tu kathameva hi dūṣaṇam ।
rohiṇyudaya āsannaḥ kṛttikābhyuditā yataḥ ।
ityukte sādhanaṃ no kiṃ na hyājñaivātra sādhakā ।।
anyat sadasatorviśvamiti ca vyāhateramā ।
asiddhasādhane doṣaḥ ko vyāptiryadi vidyate ।।
vyāptiśca vyatirekeṇa tatra taiścaiva gamyate ।
aprasiddhasya sādhyasya sādhakatvaṃ yadeṣyate ।
liṅgasyoktau viśeṣo ayaṃ kena mānena gamyate ।।
sādhanaṃ paramāṇvāderyadāsiddhasya ceṣyate ।
yathānubhavamevaitannāṅgīkāryaṃ kutastadā ।।
yatra nātiprasaṅgo asti mānaṃ na ca viparyate ।
kliṣṭakalpanayaivātra sādhyamityatidurvacaḥ ।।
pariśeṣo mithaḥsiddhiḥ cakrakasvāśrayādayaḥ ।
asiddhasādhakatvena pañcāvayavatāṃ vinā ।
aṅgīkāryāḥ samastaistanniyamaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ ।।
siddasādhanatāyāṃ ca na kathāvasitirbhavet ।
vyabhicāro hetvasiddhirekapakṣe api dūṣaṇam ।।
sādhyasādhanavaikalyaṃ dṛṣṭāntasya viśeṣaṇe ।
vaiyathyarmekāsiddhau ca viśiṣṭāsiddhireva hi ।।
aprayojakatā tatra prathamapraśnadūṣaṇam ।
siddhapraśnādikaṃ yat tadādhikyāntagartaṃ bhavet ।।
arthāpattyupamābhāvā anumāntargatāḥ kvacit ।
pratyakṣāntargato abhāvaḥ sukhāderniyamena ca ।।
anyatra khaḍiti prāptaḥ prārambhādyāśca yuktayaḥ ।
āgamārthāvasityarthā niyatavyāptayo akhilāḥ ।।
vākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ sthānaṃ samākhyā ca tathāvidhāḥ ।
kurupāṇḍavavat teṣāmupapatteḥ pṛthag vacaḥ ।।
svanyāyaiḥ sādhanaṃ kāryaṃ paranyāyaistu dūṣaṇam ।
svanyāyairdūṣaṇaṃ ca syāt sādhitaiḥ prativādinaḥ ।।
prasaṅgārthatayā proktā na siddhāntasya dūṣakāḥ ।
chalaṃ jātiriti dvedhā vyāhatyantaramiṣyate ।
jātiḥ svavyāhatirjñeyā chalamarthāntarottaram ।।
evaṃ saṃśodhitanyāyasadāgamavirodhataḥ ।
nānirvācyamiha proktaṃ māyāmātrapadena hi ।।
vilakṣaṇaṃ sadasatoriti hi vyāhataṃ svataḥ ।
pratiyogitvamapyasya brahmaṇo aṅgīkṛtaṃ bhavet ।।
mithyā cet pratiyogitvaṃ vailakṣaṇyaṃ tato na hi ।
avilakṣaṇatvaṃ satyaṃ syānmithyātvaṃ brahmaṇastataḥ ।।
anirvācyasya sattvaṃ vā yadi dharmā na kecana ।
brahmaṇo naiva jijñāsyaṃ jijñāsā dharmanirṇayaḥ ।।
idamitthamiti jñānaṃ jijñāsāyāḥ prayojanam ।
itthambhāvo hi dharmo asya na cenna pratiyogitā ।।
itthambhāvātmakān dharmānāhuśca śrutayo akhilāḥ ।
adṛśyatvādayo apyasya guṇā hi prabhuṇoditāḥ ।।
yadi syustādṛśā dharmāḥ sarvajñatvādayo na kim ।
anyāpekṣā yadi syuṣṭe sattaivaṃ deśakālagā ।।
deśakālānapekṣā hi na sattā kvāpi dṛśyate ।
sarvadharmojjñitasyāsya kiṃ śāstreṇādhigamyate ।।
mithyādharmavidhātuśca vedasyaivāpramāṇatā ।
aprāptāṃ bhrāntimāpādya kiṃ vedo mānatāṃ vrajet ।।
na hi vedaṃ vinā brahma vedyaṃ dharmāśca tadgatāḥ ।
vedavedyasya mithyātvaṃ yadi naikyasya tat katham ।।
dharmāropo api sāmānyadharmādīnāṃ hi daśarne ।
idantadādidharmitve dharmo anyaḥ kalpyate atra hi ।।
sarvadharmavihīnasya dharmāropaḥ kva dṛśyate ।
tadarthaṃ yadi dharmāṇāmāropaḥ sānavasthitiḥ ।।
īśatajjñānavedākṣajānumāmātṛpūrviṇaḥ ।
bhrāntirviśvasya yenaiva mānābhāsena kalpyate atra hi ।।
tanmātrasyānyathā bhāvāt kiṃ na syād viśvasatyatā ।
yenedaṃ kalpyate bhrāntaṃ bhrāntistasyaiva kiṃ na sā ।।
bhrāntatve tasya viśvāderīśādyabhrāntameva hi ।
bhaveyurbhrāntayo nṛṇāṃ naiveśādeḥ kathañcana ।।
satyatvamakṣajaprāptaṃ yadi bhrāntamitīṣyate ।
prāmāṇyamāgamasyāpi pratyakṣādanyataḥ kutaḥ ।।
sākṣipratyakṣato hyeva mānānāṃ mānateyate ।
sākṣiṇaḥ svaprakāśatvamanavasthā tato na hi ।।
tātkālikaṃ pramāṇatvamakṣajasya yadā bhavet ।
aikyāgamasya kiṃ na syāt tasyāpyetādṛśaṃ yadi ।
aikyaprāmāṇyamithyātvaṃ yadā viśvasya satyatā ।।
aikyāgamasya mānatvaṃ yadyabādhyamitīṣyate ।
akṣajasyāpi mānatvaṃ nābādhyaṃ kimitīṣyate ।।
advaitahānisāmānyānna viśeṣaśca kaścana ।
yadi svatastvaṃ prāmāṇye viśvasattā kathaṃ na te ।।
prāmāṇyasya ca maryādā kālato vyāhatā bhavet ।
kālāntare apyamānaṃ cedidānīṃ mānatā kutaḥ ।।
mithyātvamānaṃ mokṣe api mānaṃ kiṃ neti bhaṇyatām ।
mānatve advaitahāniḥ syādamānatve apyamokṣatā ।।
viśvasya punarāpattirmithyāmānaṃ yadā na mā ।
asti cenmuktayavasthā ca dvaitāpattirato anyathā ।।
amuktatvaṃ tathā kāle kālādhīnā hi muktatā ।
kāla evāgamo apyāha muktiṃ kālanivartane ।
mukterapi nivṛttiḥ syāt saṃsāritvamato bhavet ।।
kva ca pratyakṣataḥ prāptamanumāgamabādhitam ।
dehātmatvaṃ yadi na tat prāptaṃ pratyakṣataḥ kvacit ।
mama deha iti hyeva na deho ahamiti pramā ।।
upacāraśca kṛṣṇo ahamiti kardamalepane ।
vastrasya yadvadevaṃ syād yadyupādhikṛtaṃ tadā ।
svataḥ śuklatvavat kārṣṇyaṃ na mameti pratīyate ।।
kathaṃ ca bhedo dehāderātmano na pramīyate ।
jātamātrā mṛgā gāvo hastinaḥ pakṣiṇo khaṣāḥ ।
bhayābhayasvabhogādau kāraṇāni vijānate ।।
asmṛtau pūrvadehasya vijñānaṃ tat kathaṃ bhavet ।
anvayavyatirekāderanusandhānavismṛtau ।।
yadā dehāntarajñānaṃ dehaikyāvasitiḥ kutaḥ ।
vyāptatvādātmano dehe vyavahāreṣvapāṭavāt ।।
bhedajñāne api cāṅgāravahnivat svāviviktavat ।
bhavanti vyavahārāśca na hi pratyakṣagānapi ।।
arthān yathānubhavataḥ pratipādayituṃ kṣamāḥ ।
lokāstato hi pratyakṣasiddhaṃ nānyena kenacit ।।
śakyaṃ vārayituṃ kvāpi taccennottaragocaram ।
kathamevottaraḥ kālastadgo mokṣaśca gamyate ।।
āgamo api hi sāmānye siddhe pratyakṣataḥ punaḥ ।
viśeṣaṃ gamayedeva kathaṃ śaktigraho anyathā ।।
atītānāgatārtheṣu jāte śaktigrahe akhilam ।
viśeṣaṃ jñāpayed vākyaṃ na tadajñātaśaktike ।।
śaktiśced vartamāne syānnātītānāgataṃ vadet ।
yadi śaktigraho anyatra kathaṃ sa syāt tadagrahe ।।
sāmānyaṃ dṛṣṭamevāsāvanyatra gamayed yadi ।
sāmānyavarjitaṃ vastusvarūpaṃ gamayet katham ।।
na svarūpatvasāmānyaṃ kenāpyaṅgīkṛtaṃ kvacit ।
svarūpaṃ cedanugataṃ vyāvṛttaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet ।।
sarvānugatadharmāṇāmante hi svatvamiṣyate ।
kiṃ vyāvṛttamiti praśne svarūpamiti kevalam ।
syāduttaraṃ tato anyaccet tadeva svayameva naḥ ।।
evaṃ vyāvṛttarūpe api yadā śaktigraho bhavet ।
tasya sāmānyato jñānaṃ vinā sa ca bhavet kutaḥ ।।
ato viśeṣasāmānyarūpaṃ sarvamapīṣyate ।
vyāvṛttaṃ yacca sāmānyaṃ tadeva syād viśeṣataḥ ।।
nacaikadharmatā tena padārthānāṃ parasparam ।
dharmāṇāṃ bhedadṛṣṭayaiva tatsādṛśyasya darśanāt ।।
ataḥ sarvapadārthāśca sāmānyāt sākṣigocarāḥ ।
sarvamityeva vijñānaṃ sarveṣāṃ kathamanyathā ।।
kiñcitsādṛśyavijñānādakhilasyāpi vastunaḥ ।
śabdaśaktigrahaśca syāt tattatsādṛśyamānataḥ ।।
pratyakṣaṃ mānasaṃ caiva yadātītārthagocaram ।
tadā smṛtipramāṇatvamatītatvaviśeṣitam ।।
ādhikyamanubhūtāttu yadātītatvamiṣyate ।
mānatā ca kathaṃ na syāt smṛterbādhaśca nātrahi ।।
mānatvaṃ pratyabhijñāyā api sarvānubhūtigam ।
atītavartamānatvadharmiṇī sā ca dṛśyate ।।
na ca sā smṛtimātrārdhā tadidantvagrahaikataḥ ।
ato na vatarmānaikaniyamaḥ syād grahe akṣaje ।।
na ca pramāṇato anyā syāt pramitirnāma kutracit ।
mānābhāvād gauravācca kalpanāyāḥ kimetayā ।।
mayaitajjñātamiti tu sākṣigaṃ jñānagocaram ।
jñānameva tato anyā na pramitirnāma dṛśyate ।।
mānāmātṛprameyāṇāṃ taducchittirnahi kvacit ।
svapnānāmapi caiteṣāṃ na bādho dṛśyate kvacit ।।
jāgrattvamātramatraikamanyathā dṛśyate sphuṭam ।
ato mithyā na ca svapno jāgradvajjāgradeva ca ।।
ātmavat kvacidātmā ca syādeva bhramagocaraḥ ।
etāvatā na mithyāsau svapne jāgarite tathā ।।
yadyātmanyanyathā dṛśyaṃ bhrāntamatrāpi tad bhavet ।
abādhitānuvṛttestu svapnāderbhrāntatā kutaḥ ।।
na ca kācit pramā viśvabhrāntatve sarvameva ca ।
abhrāntatve pramāṇaṃ tu kathaṃ tadbhrāntitā bhavet ।।
kiñca bhrāntatvavādī sa bhrāntatvaṃ svamatasya ca ।
aṅgīkaroti niyataṃ tatra sampratipannatā ।
vādinostena cābhrāntaṃ viśvameva bhaviṣyati ।।
bhrāntitvabhrāntatā cet syāt kathaṃ nābhrāntisatyatā ।
aśeṣadoṣaduṣyaṃ tanmataṃ heyaṃ bubhūṣibhiḥ ।।
yena svamataheyatvaṃ svayamaṅgīkṛtaṃ sadā ।
bhrāntitvād durghaṭatvasya bhūṣaṇatvācca kevalam ।।
unmatto api kathaṃ tasya mataṃ svīkartumicchati ।
īśaśakteracintyatvānmahonmattaiḥ pravartitam ।।
ataḥ prajñātra māyoktā jaivyupādānameva sā ।
nimittamaiśvarī mukhyaṃ nirmitaṃ trātameva ca ।।
tābhyāṃ saha pṛthak caiva māyāmātramitīryate ।
ubhābhyāṃ mātamaiśvaryā trātaṃ saha pṛthak tataḥ ।।
prajñātmakaṃ mano yena manorūpāśca vāsanāḥ ।
dhīrbhīriti manastvevetyāha ca śrutirañjasā ।।
cidacinmiśramevaitanmano yāvacca saṃsṛtiḥ ।
tenāvasthā imāḥ sarvā jīvaḥ paśyati sarvadā ।।
manovikārā viṣayāḥ svāpnā yad bahyavanna te ।
sthūlā bhavantyatasteṣāṃ spaṣṭatā na tathā kvacit ।।
kvacit spaṣṭā api syuṣye vāsanā mānasī ca sā ।
īśecchayāntardadhāti vyajyate ca punastayā ।।
sṛṣṭvaiva vāsānabhiśca prapañcaṃ svāpnamīśvaraḥ ।
vāsanāmātratāṃ tasya nītvāntardhāpayatyajaḥ ।।
suṣuptimohabodhāṃśca svavaśastadvaśaṃ sadā ।
jīvaṃ nayati deveśo nānyaḥ kartāsya kaścana ।।
na sthānabhedato apyasya bhedaḥ kaścit pareśituḥ ।
sarvatrāśeṣadoṣojkhapūrṇakalyāṇacidguṇaḥ ।।
tadviruddhaṃ tu yat tatra mānaṃ naiva bhavet kvacit ।
mahātātparyarodhena kathaṃ tanmānamatra tu ।।
duḥkhāpyayasukhāvāptihetutvenaiva vedavāk ।
bhavenmānaṃ tadīśānāt prasannādeva nānyathā ।।
prasannatā guṇotkarṣajñānādeva hi kevalam ।
nirdoṣatāparijñānādapi nānyena kenacit ।।
yo māmaśeṣadoṣojkhaṃ guṇasarvasvabṛṃhitam ।
jānātyasmai prasanno ahaṃ dadyāṃ muktiṃ nacānyathā ।।
yo māmaśeṣābhyadhikaṃ vijānāti sa eva mām ।
vijānātyakhilāṃstasya dadyāṃ kāmān paraṃ padam ।।
yo māmevamasammūḍhaḥ kiṃ mā nindanti śatravaḥ ।
ityādivedasmṛtigavākyairevāvasīyate ।।
lokataśca prasādena muktiḥ sa guṇavedanāt ।
mahātātparyamukhyasya virodhādata eva hi ।।
doṣitvanirguṇatvālpaguṇatvādi kathañcana ।
nārthaḥ śrutipurāṇādestadviruddho akhilasya ca ।
arthaḥ svayaṃ vinirṇīto vāsudevena sādaram ।।
iti guhyatamaṃ śāstramidamuktaṃ mayānagha ।
etad buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaśca bhārata ।।
ityato akhilasacchāstraviruddhatvena nānumā ।
vartate tatra teneśo nirṇīto akhilasadguṇaḥ ।।
na ca cittvādabhinnatvaṃ jīvasyeśavadāpyate ।
yata ābhāsatāmeva śrutirasya vadatyalam ।।
yathaiṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasminnetadātatam ।
chāyā yathā puṃsadṛśā pumādhīnā ca dṛśyate ।
evamevātmakāḥ sarve brahmādyāḥ paramātmanaḥ ।।
sattāpratītikāryeṣu pumadhīno yatheyate ।
ābhāsa eva puruṣā muktāśca paramātmanaḥ ।।
chāyā viṣṇo ramā tasyāśchāyā dhātā viśeṣakau ।
tasyendrakāmau ca tayostayoranye akhilā api ।।
harerbrahmāsya gīstasyā viśeṣāvindra etayoḥ ।
māraścābhāsakāḥ sarva etayostadadhīnataḥ ।।
sarve alpaśaktayaścaiva pūrṇaśaktiḥ paro hariḥ ।
cetanatve api bhinnāste tasmādetena sarvadā ।
ityādiśrutivākyebhyo jñāyate bheda eva hi ।।
ābhāsatvaṃ hi nirṇītaṃ jīvasya paramātmanaḥ ।
tanna yuktaṃ yadābhāsa upādhyāyatta īyate ।।
upādhyāyattatābhāvādābhāsatvavirodhataḥ ।
cetanatvena cāṃśatvāt samudāyaikyamāpatet ।।
ataḥ pṛthaktavamuditaṃ samudāyāṃśayorbhavet ।
īśākhyā samudāye syādīśarūpeṣvivoditā ।।
ato dehādyupādhīnāmapāye samatā bhavet ।
īśarūpairathābhāsā mukhyataḥ sūryakādivat ।।
yadā tadopādhyāyattarūpāṇāṃ nāśitā bhavet ।
ityāśaṅkānivṛttyarthamāha vedādhipaḥ prabhuḥ ।
ata evopametyeva cānyābhāsaviśeṣitām ।।
yaduktaṃ tadadhīnatvaṃ sarvāvasthāsvaśeṣataḥ ।
jīvasya sadṛśatvaṃ ca cittvamātraṃ nacāparam ।।
tāvanmātreṇa cābhāso rūpameṣāṃ cidātmanām ।
nopādhyadhīnatādyaiśca nātisāmyaṃ nidarśane ।।
kiñcitsukhādisādṛśyamapīśenesurānṛte ।
tata ābhāsate nityaṃ tadvadābhāsate api ca ।।
bhānamastitvamapicaivāsamantād yatastataḥ ।
jīva ābhāsa uddiṣṭaḥ sadaiva paramātmanaḥ ।।
na jalāyattasūryādipratibimbopamatvataḥ ।
tadadhīnatvameveti kiñcit sādṛśyameva ca ।
samprakāśayataḥ sūtragatāvakhilamānataḥ ।।
jīveśabhedadṛṣṭayaiva samudāyaikatā kutaḥ ।
aśeṣadoṣarāhityaṃ sarvaśaktitvato hareḥ ।।
sarvopeteti kathitamata aikyaṃ kva doṣiṇā ।
aśeṣaśaktiyuktaścet svātantryād doṣavān katham ।।
anusandhānarahitamaikyaṃ cedekatā na tat ।
cetanaikye anusandhānaṃ pramāṇaṃ naiva cāparam ।।
anusandhānarahitasamudāyaikyameva cet ।
cetaneṣvastu tannāmamātrameva yatastataḥ ।।
muktau syādanusandhānaṃ cenmithyājñānitā bhavet ।
sarvajña ekatāṃ nānusandhatte naiva sā yataḥ ।।
paścāt syādanusandhānaṃ cenmithyājñānitā bhavet ।
vidyamānānusandhānaṃ na cedajñatvamāpatet ।।
asadaikyaṃ bhavet paścād yadi syāt saptamo rasaḥ ।
samudāyaikyametasmād dūrato apākṛtaṃ sadā ।।
ato aśeṣaguṇonnaddhaṃ nirdoṣaṃ yāvadeva hi ।
tāvadeveśvaro nāma tatra bhedo api na kvacit ।।
neha nānāsti kimapi harayo ayamayaṃ hi saḥ ।
ityādiśrutimānena jīvāṃśāḥ sarva eva ca ।।
niyamenānusandhānavanto yadyekatā svataḥ ।
aṃśino aśeṣasandhānamatyalpasyāpi vidyate ।।
bhuvi jātena cāṃśena sukhaduḥkhādi tadgatam ।
anubhūyate viśeṣastu kaścidīśakṛto bhavet ।।
īśasyācintyaśaktitvānnāśakyaṃ kvāpi vidyate ।
seśatānupapannaiva yadi jīvaikatāsya hi ।
anīśasyeśatetyeva viruddhaṃ sarvamānataḥ ।।
īśatvenaiva vijñātamanīśatvena cecchrutiḥ ।
anīśatvena vijñātamīśatvenāthavā diśet ।।
upajīvyavirodhena naiva mānatvameṣyati ।
ata eveśatāsiddherna kiñcicchakyamasya ca ।।
īśatve anīśabhedena śrutyā samyak prakāśite ।
ayuktamapi cānyatra yuktaṃ bhavati tadbalāt ।।
ato anyatrāpi yad dṛṣṭaṃ tadīśenaiva kalpyate ।
śrutyābhāsāptamapi nahīśatvaparipanthi yat ।।
īśo anīśo jaganmithyā duḥkhī mukto bhidā na hi ।
iti pratijñāvyāghātaḥ sarvadoṣādhikādhikaḥ ।।
iti hi brahmatarkoktiratiheyamato akhilaiḥ ।
bubhūṣubhirmatamidaṃ jīveśābhedavādinaḥ ।।
nāyuktamīśituḥ kiñcidīśatvasyāvirodhi yat ।
yadīśitvavirodhi syāt tadevāyuktamañjasā ।।
īśitvasyāvirodhena yojayitvākhilāḥ pramāḥ ।
siddheśitvena cāyuktamapi hīśe na yojayet ।।
mānataḥ prāptamakhilaṃ nāmānaṃ yojayet kvacit ।
iti hi brahmatarkoktirato yuktamihoditam ।।
sa cāprākṛtarūpatvādarūpaḥ svaguṇaśatmakam ।
rūpamasya śiraḥpāṇipādādyātmakamiṣyate ।।
ato nānityatā naiva śrutidvayavirodhitā ।
yathā hi taijasasyaiva prakāśasyojkhitāvapi ।
ātmaiva jyotirityāha jīvasyeśaṃ śrutistathā ।।
tadbhaktitāratamyena tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam ।
brahmādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāmānandāderyathākramam ।।
pratibimbavadapyeṣāmānando anyaguṇā yathā ।
nārāyaṇaguṇādhīnaścātyalpastadapekṣayā ।।
tasmād bhinnaśca satatamanyajjñānaṃ parasya ca ।
anyajjñānaṃ tu jīvānāmanya ānanda īśatā ।।
mukhyeśatā pareśasya gauṇī jīvasya sā yataḥ ।
iti śruteḥ sṛṣṭināśau tadadhīnāvitīrite ।
svabhāvatvāt sthiternaitadapekṣeti na yujyate ।।
yataḥ svabhāvo akhila īśāyatto akhilasya ca ।
avyakto api svaktayaiva bhaktānāṃ dṛśyate hariḥ ।।
tadabhinnā guṇā nityamapi sarve viśeṣataḥ ।
guṇatvena guṇitvena bhoktṛbhogyatayā sthitāḥ ।।
viśeṣātmatayā teṣāṃ nityaśaktayātmanā tathā ।
nityasthiterna dharmāṇāṃ kriyādīnāmanityatā ।।
na viśeṣātmatā ceyamanityā śaktirūpatā ।
saiva yat saviśeṣā syād viśeṣo anyo nacāpyayam ।।
svanirvāhakatāhetostathāpi syād viśeṣataḥ ।
viśeṣatvena vijñāteḥ pramāṇairakhilairapi ।।
sasarja sañjahāreti viśeṣo hyavagamyate ।
śrutyaiva sa sa eveti tadabhedaśca gamyate ।।
bhedo yadi viśeṣasya sa bhedo bhedinā katham ।
bhinnaścedanavasthā syādabhinnaścet purā na kim ।।
viśeṣo abhinna eveti tena nābhyupagamyate ।
abhinno nivirśeṣaśced bhedastadbhedatā kutaḥ ।।
anenānena bhinno ayamiti yat sa viśeṣataḥ ।
bheda evaiṣa bahudhā dṛśyate tat kimuttaram ।।
abhedabhedayoścaiva svarūpatvaṃ hi bhedinā ।
tayorapyaviśeṣatve paryāyatvaṃ hi śabdayoḥ ।।
abhedabhedaśabdau ca paryāyāviti ko vadet ।
bhedo anyonyamabhedaśca bhedinā ced viśeṣatā ।।
nirviśeṣe kathaṃ bhedo bhedinaikastathābhidā ।
punastayorvibhedaśca bhedimātratvato bhavet ।।
bhedinaścaiva bhedasya viśeṣo yadi gamyate ।
abhedābhedinoścaiva kiṃ bhedo abhedabhedayoḥ ।।
viśeṣeṇaiva sarvatra yadi vyavahṛtirbhavet ।
kalpanāgauravāyaiva kiṃ bhedaḥ kalpyate tadā ।।
aikyapratītyabhāvena bheda eva gavaśvayoḥ ।
sa eveti pratītau hi viśeṣo nāma bhaṇyate ।।
saccidāderaparyāyasiddhayarthaṃ māyināpi hi ।
aṅgīkāryo viśeṣo ayaṃ yadyasatyaviśeṣaṇam ।
pṛthak pṛthag vārayituṃ śabdāntaramitīṣyate ।।
māyāviśeṣarāhityaviśeṣeṇa viśeṣitā ।
satyasyāpi bhavet sā ca tathā cedanavasthitiḥ ।।
yadi satye viśeṣo na na taduktirbhavet tadā ।
lakṣyate cet tena lakṣyamityapi syād viśeṣitā ।।
punaḥpunarlakṣaṇāyāmapi syādanavasthitiḥ ।
yadyabhāvaviśeṣitvaṃ syādaṅgīkṛtameva te ।।
asārvajñyādirāhityamapyevaṃ te bhaviṣyati ।
tadā sārvajñyameva syād bhāvārthatvānnañordvayoḥ ।।
yadi naitādṛśaṃ grāhyamasukhatvānivartanāt ।
asattvajñānatādeśca syādasattvādikaṃ tadā ।।
anṛtādivirodhitvaṃ yadyasyābhyupagamyate ।
anaiśvaryavirodhitvamapyevaṃ kiṃ nivāryate ।।
akhaṇḍakhaṇḍanādevaṃ viśeṣo'khaṇḍavādinā ।
khaṇḍitenāpi manasā svīkāryo'nanyathāgateḥ ।।
akhaṇḍakhaṇḍavādibhyāṃ khaṇḍākhaṇḍena caiva tat ।
mahādareṇa śirasi viśeṣo dhārya eva hi ।।
nidarśanatrayeṇāto bhagavānatyabhinnatām ।
guṇānāmādareṇāha tacca nābhihitānvayaḥ ।।
yadāśeṣaviśeṣāṇamuktiḥ sāmānyato bhavet ।
padaikenāpyuttareṇa viśeṣāvagatirbhavet ।।
yato aśeṣaviśeṣāṇāṃ vastunāstyeva caikatā ।
ataḥ sāmānyato jñātaḥ padāntarabalāt punaḥ ।
bhaved viśeṣato jñānastena syādanvitoktitā ।।
svārtha evānvito yasmāt kenacit tadviśeṣataḥ ।
aneneti taduktayaiva jñāyate anubhavena hi ।।
yadyananvitamevaitat padaṃ svārthaṃ vadediha ।
tathānyānyapi sarvāṇi kaḥ kuryādanvayaṃ punaḥ ।।
vyāpāro na hi śabdasya paraḥ svārthaprakāśanāt ।
pumānapyekavāroktayā kṛtakṛtyo yadā bhavet ।।
anvayasya kathaṃ jñānaṃ śabdārthatvaṃ yadāsya na ।
yadaivānanvitārthasya vacanaṃ taiḥ padaibharvet ।।
ananvitaḥ syācchabdārtho na tadartho hi so anvayaḥ ।
nirākāṅkṣapadānyeva vākyamityucyate budhaiḥ ।।
tattadarthābhidhānena syānnirākāṅkṣatā ca sā ।।
apūrtestāvadarthānāmākāṅkṣā pūrvamiṣyate ।
karmakartṛkriyāṇāṃ tu pūrtau ko anyo anvayo bhavet ।।
apūrtiścet padairuktaiḥ kiṃ nṛśṛṅgeṇa pūryate ।
vyāpāraścet punasteṣāmanuktāvapi kiṃ na saḥ ।।
ukte buddhisthatāhetoryadi vyāpāra iṣyate ।
buddhisthatvāya yatnaṃ na kathaṃ kuryuḥ puraiva ca ।
puruṣādhīnatā teṣāṃ yadi paścācca sā samā ।।
pumānevānvayāyaiṣāṃ paścād yadi viceṣyate ।
ananvitābhidhānānāṃ sa evārthāntaroktiṣu ।
yatatāṃ śabdaśaktiścet tatra naivānvaye katham ।।
tatkalpanāgurutvādidoṣeto abhihitānvayaḥ ।
anubhūtiviruddhaśca tyājya eva manīṣibhiḥ ।।
kartṛśabde hyabhihite dharmasāmānyavedanāt ।
viśeṣadharmamanvicchan kimityeva hi pṛcchati ।।
guṇakriyādidharmāṇāṃ viśeṣe kathite punaḥ ।
nirākāṅkṣo bhaved yasmācchabdā anvitavācakāḥ ।।
ato anantaguṇātmaiko bhagavāneka eva tu ।
ucyate sarvavedaiśca te cākhilavilakṣaṇāḥ ।।
sarve sarvaguṇātmānaḥ sarvakartāra eva ca ।
tathāpi saviśeṣāśca vidvadyvutpattito apica ।।
taistaiḥ śabdaiśca bhaṇyante yujyate copadeśataḥ ।
anyānandādisādṛśyamānukūlyādinā param ।।
pūrṇatvādi mahat teṣāṃ vailakṣaṇyaṃ śrutau śrutam ।
pūrṇe aśeṣaniyantā ca sukhādutama ekakalaḥ ।।
guṇorusamudāyo ayaṃ vāsudevaḥ sa niṣkaḷaḥ ।
vāsudevaśrutiḥ saiṣā guṇān vakti hareḥ parān ।।
sa evāśeṣajīvasthanissaṅkhayānādikālikān ।
dharmādharmān sadā paśyan svecchayā bodhayatyajaḥ ।।
kāṃścit teṣāṃ phalaṃ caiva dadāti svayamacyutaḥ ।
na te viśeṣaṃ kamapi preraṇādikamucyate ।
kuryuḥ kadāpi tenāyaṃ svatantro anupacārataḥ ।।
karmāṇi tāni ca pṛthak cetanānyeva sarvaśaḥ ।
acetanaśarīrāṇi svakarmaphalabhāñci ca ।।
pratyekaṃ teṣu cānantakarmāṇyevaṃvidhāni ca ।
tāni caivamitīśasya nissīmā śaktiruttamā ।।
ekaiva brahmahatyā hi varāhahariṇoditā ।
brahmapārastavenaiva niṣkrāntā rājadehataḥ ।।
stotrasya tasya māhātmyād vyādhatvaṃ gamitā punaḥ ।
prāpya jñānaṃ paraṃ cāpa tathānyānyapi sarvadā ।।
anantānyuditānyevaṃ prabhuṇā kapilena hi ।
saṃsāre pacyamānāni karmāṇyapi pṛthak pṛthak ।।
tasmādanantamāhātmyaguṇapūgo janārdanaḥ ।
bhaktyā paramayā'rādhya iti pādārtha īryate ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

vairāgyato bhaktidārḍhyaṃ tenopāsā yadā bhavet ।
āparokṣyaṃ bhaved viṣṇoriti pādakramo bhavet ।।
yuktito jñātavedārtho nirasya samayān parān ।
parasparavirodhaṃ ca praṇudyāśeṣavākyagam ।।
adhyātmapraṇavo bhūtvā tasya sannihitatvataḥ ।
bahuyuktivirodhānāṃ bhānāt tatsahitaśruteḥ ।।
virodhaṃ ca nirākṛtya śrutīnāṃ prāṇatastvagān ।
parihṛtya virodhāṃśca tatprasādānurañjitaḥ ।।
dehakartṛtvamīśasya jñātvā tatpitṛtāsmṛteḥ ।
viśeṣasnehamāpādya sarvakartṛtvato adhikam ।।
niṣpādya bahumānaṃ ca tadanyatrātiduḥkhataḥ ।
utpādyādhikavairāgyaṃ tadguṇādhikyavedanāt ।।
sarvasya tadvaśatvācca dārḍhyaṃ bhakteravāpya ca ।
yatetopāsanāyaiva viśiṣṭācāryasampadā ।।
kartavyā brahmajijñāsetyukte kimiti saṃśaye ।
ata ityudite apyasya viśeṣānuktitaḥ punaḥ ।।
sṛṣṭibandhanamokṣādikartṛtvasya śrutatvataḥ ।
yato mokṣādidātāsāvato jijñāsya eva vaḥ ।
ityāha tat paraṃ brahma vyāsākhyaṃ jñānaraśmimat ।।
yenaiva bandhamokṣaḥ syāt sa ca jijñāsayā gataḥ ।
suprasanno bhavedīśo jijñāsāto asya muktidā ।।
mokṣādidatvamīśasya kathamevāvagamyate ।
iti cecchāstrayonitvācchāstragamyo hi mokṣadaḥ ।।
pratyakṣāvasitebhyaḥ syād yadi mokṣaḥ kathañcana ।
kimityanādisaṃsāramagnāḥ sarvā imāḥ prajāḥ ।।
yasmānniyamato duḥkhahāniḥ pratyakṣato bhavet ।
dhāvantyeva tamuddiśya rājādyamakhilāḥ prajāḥ ।।
anumānagamyato mokṣo yadi tasyānumaiva hi ।
dṛṣṭapūruṣavanmokṣadātṛtāṃ vinivārayet ।।
tacchāstragamya evaiko mokṣado bhavati dhruvam ।
śāstragamyaśca nānyo asti mokṣadatvena keśavāt ।।
mokṣado hi svatantraḥ syāt paratantraḥ svayaṃ sṛtau ।
vartamānaḥ kathaṃ śaktaḥ paramokṣāya kevalam ।।
anyāśrayeṇa yadyeṣa dadyānmokṣaṃ sa eva hi ।
tenānanusṛto mokṣaṃ na dadyādanyavākyataḥ ।
atastadarthamapi sa jñeyo viṣṇurmumukṣibhiḥ ।।
yamevaiṣa iti śrutyā tameveti ca sādaram ।
śāstrayonitvamasyaiva jñāyate vedavādibhiḥ ।।
ya enaṃ viduramṛtā ityuktastu samudragaḥ ।
tadeva brahma paramamiti śrutyāvadhāritaḥ ।।
yataḥ prasūteti tataḥ sṛṣṭimāha tato hariḥ ।
śāstrayonirnacānyo asti mukhyatastviti gamyate ।।
śāstrayonitvametasya jñāyate hi samanvayāt ।
samiti hyupasargeṇa paramukhyāthartocyate ।।
evaṃ paramamukhyārtho nārāyaṇa iti śruteḥ ।
nirdhāraṇāya nāśabdamiti vedapatirjagau ।।
kathaṃ samanvayo jñeyaḥ svalpaśākhāvidāṃ nṛṇām ।
vedā hyanantā iti hi śrutirāhāpyanantatām ।।
anantavedanirṇītirmahāpraḷayavāridheḥ ।
uttāraṇopametyasmānna jñeyo atra samanvayaḥ ।।
iti śaṅkāpanodārthaṃ sa āha karuṇākaraḥ ।
aśakyottaraṇatve api hyāgamāpāravāridheḥ ।
nirṇīyate mayaivāyaṃ romakūpalayodinā ।।
yadyapyaśeṣavedārtho durgamo akhilamānavaiḥ ।
majjñānāvyākṛtākāśe prāpnoti paramāṇutām ।।
iti prakāśayan viśvapatirāha prameyatām ।
nikhilasyāpi vedasya gatisāmānyamañjasā ।।
ko nāma gatisāmānyamanantāgamasampadaḥ ।
jñānasūryamṛte brūyāt tamekaṃ bādarāyaṇam ।।
anyo apyalpamatiḥ śākhācatuṣpañcagataṃ vasu ।
jānannānumitatvena brūyāt tasya prasādataḥ ।।
iti mukhyatayāśeṣagatisāmānyavit prabhuḥ ।
pratijajñe dṛḍhaṃ yasmād devānāmapi pūryate ।।
ato nikhilavedānāṃ siddha evaṃ samanvayaḥ ।
iti sujñāpitārtho api pṛthak cāha samanvayam ।।
tatra prathamato anyatra prasiddhānāṃ samanvayaḥ ।
śabdānāṃ vācya evātra mahāmalleśabhaṅgavat ।।
ito atyabhyadhikatve api turyapādoditasya tu ।
mahāsamanvaye tasmin nādhikāro akhilasya hi ।।
brahmaivādhikṛtastatra mukhyato anye yathākramam ।
durgamatvācca naivātra prāthamyenodito añjasā ।।
ato anyatra prasiddhānāṃ śabdānāṃ nirṇayāya tu ।
pravṛttaḥ prathamaṃ devastatrānandādayo guṇāḥ ।
īśasyaiveti nirṇītāḥ śrutiyuktisamāśrayāt ।।
devatāntaragāḥ sarve śabdavṛttinimittataḥ ।
viṣṇumeva vadantyaddhā tatsaṅgādupacārataḥ ।।
anyadevān vadantīha viśeṣaguṇavaktṛtaḥ ।
viṣṇumeva paraṃ brūyurevamanye apyaśeṣataḥ ।।
ityanyatraprasiddhoruśabdarāśeraśeṣataḥ ।
jñāte samanvaye viṣṇau liṅgairhyeṣa samanvayaḥ ।।
teṣāmanyagatatve tu na syāt samyak samanvayaḥ ।
ityevāśeṣaliṅgānāṃ brahmaṇyeva samanvayam ।।
āhobhayagatatvaṃ ca syādato liṅgaśabdayoḥ ।
iti saṃśayanuttyarthamubhayatra pratītitaḥ ।।
śabdānāṃ vartamānānāṃ saliṅgānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
samanvayo harāveva yannaivānyatra mukhyataḥ ।।
śabdā liṅgāni ca yato naivānyatra svatantratā ।
asvatantreṣu śabdasya vṛttiheturna mukhyataḥ ।।
yato ato yadadhīnāste śabdārthatvamupāgatāḥ ।
atyalpenaiva śabdasya vṛttihetuguṇena tu ।।
ayo yathā dāhakatvaṃ sa eveśaḥ svatantrataḥ ।
mukhyaśabdārtha iti hi svīkartavyo manīṣibhiḥ ।।
ityāhaivañca śabdānāṃ nārāyaṇasamanvaye ।
siddhe apyaśeṣaśabdānāṃ na kathañcana yujyate ।।
virodhāvavaratvāderapi prāptiryato bhavet ।
iti cedavaratvādi dvividhaṃ hyupalabhyate ।।
parasyāvaratāheturyaḥ svayaṃ para eva san ।
so api hyavaraśabdārtho yathā rājā jayī bhavet ।।
anyo avaratvānubhavī tayoḥ pūrvo asti keśave ।
dvitīyo jīva evāsti svātantrānnaca dūṣaṇam ।।
harerevamaśeṣeṇa sarvaśabdasamanvaye ।
ukte virodhahīnasya syāt samanvayatā yataḥ ।
ato aśeṣavirodhānāṃ kṛteśena nirākṛtiḥ ।।
samanvayāvirodhābhyāṃ sañjāte vastunirṇaye ।
kiṃ mayā kāryamityeva syād buddhiradhikāriṇaḥ ।।
tatra bhaktividhānārthamabhaktānarthasantatau ।
uktāyāṃ bhaktidārḍhyāya prokte aśeṣaguṇoccaye ।
vaktavyopāsanā nityaṃ kartavyetyādareṇa hi ।।
sopāsanā ca dvividhā śāstrābhyāsasvarūpiṇī ।
dhyānarūpā parā caiva tadaṅgaṃ dhāraṇādikam ।।
tathobhayātmakaṃ caiva pāde asmin bādarāyaṇaḥ ।
āhopāsanamaddhava vistarācchrutipūrvakam ।।
pṛthagdṛṣṭiraśakyatvamanirṇītiḥ samuccayaḥ ।
viśeṣadarśanaṃ kāryalopo nānoktirāśutā ।।
vibhramo apākṛtirliṅgamanavasthāviśeṣitā ।
aprayojanatā cātiprasaṅgo adūrasaṃśrayaḥ ।।
viśiṣṭakāraṇaṃ ceṣyā dṛṣṭavairūpyamunnatiḥ ।
anuktiraprayatnatvaṃ dṛḍhabandhaparābhavau ।।
puṃsāmyaṃ prāptasantyāgaḥ kāraṇānirṇayo bhramaḥ ।
viśeṣadarśitā'lāpo guṇasāmyaṃ pṛthagdṛśiḥ ।।
agamyavartma sandhānamiṣṭaṃ phalamakalpanā ।
śuddhavairūpyamaṅgatvamaviśeṣadṛśiḥ kriyā ।।
yuktayaḥ pūrvapakṣasthāḥ sujñeyatvaṃ vidhikriyā ।
māhātmyamalpaśaktitvaṃ yathāyogyaphalaṃ bhavaḥ ।।
phalasāmyaṃ viśeṣaśca guṇādhikyaṃ pradhānatā ।
yathāśaktikriyā sandhiḥ pramāṇabalamānatiḥ ।।
kāraṇaṃ kāryavaiśeṣyaṃ svabhāvo vastudūṣaṇam ।
pratikriyāvirodhaśca pratisandhiranūnatā ।।
saṃskārapāṭavaṃ svecchāniyatirvastuvaibhavam ।
viśeṣoktiramānatvaṃ prādhānyaṃ prītirāgamaḥ ।।
susthiratvaṃ kṛtaprāptiranādiguṇavistaraḥ ।
sādhanottamatā nānādṛṣṭiḥ śiṣṭiranūnatā ।।
avighnatvavirodhau ca guṇavaiśeṣyamāgamaḥ ।
siddhāntanirṇaye hyetā yuktayo avyāhatāḥ sadā ।।
yathāśaktayakhilān vedān vijñāyopāsanaṃ bhavet ।
tatrākhilasya vijñaptiḥ samyag brahmaṇa eva hi ।।
tadanyeṣāṃ yathāyogyamakhilajñaptiriṣyate ।
tāvatopāsane yogyo bhavedevākhilaḥ pumān ।।
mahattvasya paraṃ pāraṃ viditvaiva janārdanaḥ ।
stoṣyatāmeti tuṣṭatvamiti nāstyeva nārada ।।
kintu niścalayā bhaktayā hyātmajñānānurūpataḥ ।
yaḥ stoṣyati sadā bhaktastuṣyastasya sadā hariḥ ।।
ityādivākyasandarbhād yathāyogyākhilajñatā ।
ātmajñānānurūpatvaṃ yathāśakti vicāraṇāt ।।
vedaḥ kṛtsno adhigantavyaḥ svādhyāyādhyayanaṃ bhavet ।
ityādivākyavaiyarthyamanyathā na nivāryate ।।
adyāpi tena devādyāḥ śṛṇvate manvate sadā ।
dhyāyanti ca yathāyogaṃ tathāpyā vastunirṇayāt ।
śravaṇaṃ mananaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ sarvathaiva hi ।।
matiśrutidhyānakālaviśeṣaṃ gururuttamaḥ ।
vetti tasyoktimārgeṇa kurvataḥ syāddhi darśanam ।।
śravaṇaṃ dṛṣṭatattvasya mananaṃ dhyānameva ca ।
viśeṣānandasamprāptyā anyasyaitāni dṛṣṭaye ।।
yadi tādṛg gururnāsti nirṇītaśravaṇādikam ।
tatsiddhāntānusāreṇa nirṇayajñāt samācaret ।।
śravaṇādi vinā naiva kṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭhedapi kvacit ।
atyaśakye tu nidrādau punareva samārabhet ।।
abhāve nirṇayajñasya sacchāstrāṇyeva sarvadā ।
śṛṇuyād yadi sajjñānaprācuryamupalabhyate ।।
mahadbhayo viṣṇubhaktebhyo yathāśakti ca saṃśayān ।
chindyāt svato adhikābhāve svayameva samabhyaset ।।
aśeṣaguṇapūrṇatvaṃ sarvadoṣasamujkhitiḥ ।
viṣṇoranyacca tattantramiti samyag vinirṇayaḥ ।।
svatantratvaṃ sadā tasya tasya bhedaśca sarvataḥ ।
adoṣatvasya siddhayarthaṃ yadabhede tadanvayaḥ ।।
tattantratvaṃ ca muktānāmapi tadguṇapūrtaye ।
muktānāmapi bhedaśca na hi bhinnamabhinnatām ।
gacchad dṛṣṭaṃ kvacit tasyāpyabhāvo anubhavopagaḥ ।।
pūrvābhede doṣavattvamīśasyetyatibhinnatā ।
nārāyaṇena muktānāmapi samyagiti sthitiḥ ।।
bhedābhede apyabhedena doṣāṇāmapi sambhavaḥ ।
nirdoṣatvaṃ ramāyāśca tadanantaratā tathā ।।
brahmā sarasvatī vīndraśeṣarudrāśca tatsriyaḥ ।
śakrakāmau tadanye ca kramānmuktāvapīti ca ।।
satsiddhānta iti jñeyo nirṇīto hariṇā svayam ।
etadvirodhi yat sarvaṃ tamase andhāya kevalam ।।
andhaṃ tamo viśantīti prāha śrutiratisphuṭam ।
ityeva śrutayo aśeṣāḥ pañcarātramathākhilam ।।
mūlarāmāyaṇaṃ caiva bhārataṃ smṛtayo akhilāḥ ।
vaiṣṇavāni purāṇāni sāṅkhayayogau parāvapi ।।
brahmatarkaśca mīmāṃsetyanantaḥ śabdasāgaraḥ ।
anantara yuktayaścaiva pratyakṣāgamamūlakāḥ ।।
pratyakṣamaiśvaraṃ caiva ramādīnāmaśeṣataḥ ।
muktānāmapyamuktānāmetamevārthamuttamam ।।
anyāvakāśarahitaṃ prakāśayati sādaram ।
etadeva ca sacchāstraṃ duḥśāstraṃ tu tataḥ param ।।
sacchāstramabhyasennityaṃ duḥśāstraṃ ca parityajet ।
asaṃśayena tattvasya nirṇaye brahmadarśanam ।।
samyagviṣamavijñānatāratamyānusārataḥ ।
phalaṃ bhavet tāratamyāt sukhaduḥkhātmakaṃ nṛṇām ।।
samyak cādhikavijñānāt sukhādhikyaṃ bhavennṛṇām ।
ato yathātmaśaktayaiva śravaṇaṃ mananaṃ tathā ।।
viṣayeṣu ca saṃsargācchāśvatasya ca saṃśayāt ।
manasā cānyadākāṅkṣāt paraṃ na pratipādyate ।।
iti bhāratavākyaṃ hi tenaitaddoṣavarjitaḥ ।
sadopāsanayā yukto vāsudevaṃ prapaśyati ।।
doṣā anādisambaddhāste muktiparipanthinaḥ ।
santyeva prāyaśaḥ puṃsu tena mokṣo na jāyate ।।
sarve ta ete jīveṣu dṛśyante tāratamyataḥ ।
ṛjūnāmeka evāsti paramotsāhavarjanam ।
sa guṇālpatvamātratvānnarjatvena viruddhayate ।।
ato viṣṇau parā bhaktistadbhakteṣu ramādiṣu ।
tāratamyena kartavyā puruṣārthamabhīpsitā ।।
svādaraḥ sarvajantūnāṃ saṃsiddho hi svabhāvataḥ ।
tato adhikaḥ svottameṣu tadādhikyānusārataḥ ।।
kartavyo vāsudevāntaṃ sarvathā śubhamicchatā ।
na kadācit tyajet taṃ ca krameṇainaṃ vivardhayet ।।
sameṣu svātmavat snehaḥ satsvanyatra tato dayā ।
kāryaivamāparokṣyeṇa dṛśyate kṣipramīśvaraḥ ।।
tat tamo andhaṃ vrajed viṣṇusamatvaṃ yo anupaśyati ।
ramābrahmaśivādīnāmapi muktau kathañcana ।।
kimutādhikyadṛṣṭestad guṇābhāvamaterapi ।
doṣavetturabhedasya draṣṭurdraṣṭustathobhayoḥ ।।
ityāha sacchrutistena samproktaguṇasaṃyutam ।
upāsīta hariṃ dṛṣṭvā muktistenaiva jāyate ।।
dveṣād yanmuktikathanaṃ śrutivākyavirodhi yat ।
ripavo ye tu rāmasya vimukhatvānnirāmiṇaḥ ।
abhidrohapade nityamandhe tamasi te sthitāḥ ।।
haridviṣastamo yānti ye caiva tadabhedinaḥ ।
tannirguṇatvavettārastasya doṣavido api ca ।।
ityādiśrutisandarbhād dveṣiṇastama īyate ।
hiraṇyakaśipuścāpi bhagavannindayā tamaḥ ।
vidhikṣuratyagāt sūno prahlādasyānubhāvataḥ ।।
yadanindat pitā mahyaṃ tvadbhakte mayi cāghavān ।
tasmāt pitā me pūyeta durantād dustarādaghāt ।।
nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śṛṇvaṃstatparasya janasya vā ।
tato nāpaiti yaḥ so api yātyaghaḥ sukṛtāccyutaḥ ।।
avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanumāśritam ।
paraṃ bhāvamajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvaram ।।
moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ ।
rākṣasīmāsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohanīṃ śritāḥ ।।
māmātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto abhyasūyakāḥ ।
tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān ।
kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu ।।
āsurīṃ yonimāpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani ।
māmaprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yāntyadhamāṃ gatim ।।
yo dviṣṭād vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।
kathaṃ sa na bhaved dveṣya ālokāntasya kasyacit ।।
yo dviṣṭād vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।
majjanti pitarastasya narake śāśvatīḥ samāḥ ।
ityādivākyasandohād dveṣiṇastama eva tu ।।
naiva mokṣa iti prāhurlokāyatamate sthitāḥ ।
bhogaḥ śarīraparyantaṃ bhasmībhāvastato bhavet ।।
iti tat kena mānena dṛṣṭaṃ pratyakṣavādinā ।
na hi pratyakṣamānena mokṣābhāvo avasīyate ।।
ghaṭate muktidṛṣṭistu puruṣeṇa mahīyasā ।
neti vakturmahattvaṃ tu kathañcana na vidyate ।।
sādhayan sarvasāmānyaṃ kathameva viśeṣavān ।
dṛśyante puruṣā loke parāvaravido apica ।।
aparokṣadṛśo yoganiṣṭhāścāmalacakṣuṣaḥ ।
pratyakṣaṃ devatāṃ dṛṣṭvā tatprasādāptabhūtayaḥ ।।
jñānavijñānapārajñā niṣiddhayante kathaṃ nṛbhiḥ ।
dṛśyate cātimāhātmyaṃ teṣāmatimahaujasām ।।
yadi te api niṣiddhayante kiṃ noktiste niṣiddhayate ।
yaduktavākyaprāmāṇyaṃ pratyakṣeṇopalabhyate ।।
varādayo api taddattāḥ sadā satyā bhavanti hi ।
aprāmāṇyaṃ tadukteśca vṛthāvācāvasīyate ।।
na hi prayojanaṃ kiñcit paralokanivāraṇāt ।
vṛthāvācaṃ vṛthā hanyād yadi tasya kimuttaram ।
svajīvanavirodhāya vadan kiṃ nāma buddhimān ।।
prāmāṇye saṃśayaḥ kiṃ syāt tayoḥ puruṣayorapi ।
svajīvanaviruddhoktirajño dṛṣṭasya cāpi saḥ ।।
yaścātīndriyadevoktiśrotā dṛṣṭaparāvaraḥ ।
atītānāgataṃ sarvaṃ lokānubhavamāpayan ।
ataḥ pratyakṣagamyatvād vedamātvasya ca sphuṭam ।।
yadyāgamasya no mātvamakṣajasya tathā bhavet ।
yadyakṣajasya mātvaṃ syādāgamasya kathaṃ na tat ।
lokavākyād viśeṣaścāvyabhicāreṇa siddhayati ।।
asti mokṣo api dharmeṇa yathārthajñānato api ca ।
prāmāṇyamanumāyāśca jinasyāptatvasādhane ।।
tadvākyād dharmasajjñānavijñaptirbhavatīti ca ।
dharmo ahiṃsāparo nānyo jñānaṃ pudgaladarśanam ।।
iti jaināḥ kathaṃ tat syāt pramāṇamanumānataḥ ।
viṣayān prati sthitaṃ hyakṣaṃ pratyakṣamiti gīyate ।
pratyakṣaśabdānusārādanumeti prakītirtā ।।
ā samantād gamayati dharmādharmau paraṃ padam ।
yaccāpyatīndriyaṃ tvanyat tenāsāvāgamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
etena kāreṇenaiva tattanmānatvamiṣyate ।
svarūpaṃ hi tadeteṣāmanyathāsiddhimānataḥ ।।
ato anumā kathaṃ dharmaṃ pudgalaṃ cāpi darśayet ।
svarūpaṃ pudgalasyoktā doṣā ānandameva ca ।
na manyate pudgalaṃ sa duḥkhābhāvaḥ sukhaṃ tviti ।।
mātrābhogātirekeṇa sukhādhikyasya darśanāt ।
sukhasyābhāvatā kena na ca syāt kiṃ viparyayaḥ ।।
yadi bhāvo api kaścit syāt tasyaivābhāvatā kutaḥ ।
yadi sarve apyabhāvāḥ syuranyonyamiti bhāvatā ।।
abhāvābhāvatā yat syāt kiṃ naśchinnaṃ tadā bhavet ।
bhāvatvaṃ vidhirūpatvaṃ niṣedhatvamabhāvatā ।।
niṣedhasya niṣedho api bhāva eva balād bhavet ।
prathamapratipattistu bhāvabhāvaniyāmikā ।।
na ca pudgalavijñānaṃ mokṣadaṃ bhavati kvacit ।
asvātantryāt pudgalasya jñāto api sukhado na hi ।।
na hi duḥkhiparijñānād duḥkhitvaṃ vinivartate ।
yadi pudgalavijñānādaduḥkhī syāt kathañcana ।
dehavānapi nāduḥkhī kiṃ jñānāduttaraṃ sadā ।।
īśakḷptyanusāreṇa syāt kālādīśavādinaḥ ।
karmahetutvamapi tu niścaitanyānnahi kvacit ।।
aśeṣaduḥkhavilaye nedānīṃ kāraṇaṃ yathā ।
tathottaraṃ ca naiva syād dṛṣṭipūrvānumā yataḥ ।।
śaktasyānyasya vijñānaṃ tatprītijanakaṃ yadi ।
tayaiva bandhahāniḥ syāditi kiṃ nāma dūṣaṇam ।।
svajñānād bandhahānistu dṛśyate kasya kutracit ।
ahiṃsāyāśca dharmatvaṃ kena mānena gamyate ।
hiṃsāyā eva dharmatvamityukte syāt kimuttaram ।।
dharmasya sukhahetutvamapi kenāvagamyate ।
hatyayā mokṣahetutvaṃ kuto mānānnivāryate ।।
na ca śūnyaparijñānācchūnyabhāvanayāpi ca ।
mokṣaḥ kathañcana bhaved yadīdānīṃ kathaṃ na saḥ ।।
paraprasādanecchostu viḷambo nāma yujyate ।
pumicchādhīnatā no ced viḷambaḥ kiṅkṛto bhavet ।।
anyatrāpi viḷambāstu syurīśecchānimittataḥ ।
anyathā kāraṇaṃ cet syāt kiṃ kāryaṃ nopajāyate ।
kāraṇe sati kāryasya bhāvaḥ suniyato asya hi ।।
vijñānavādinaścaiva vijñānādvaitavedanāt ।
vijñānabhāvanāccaiva mokṣo na ghaṭate kvacit ।।
antarjñānasya bāhye ca kṣaṇikatvasya vedanāt ।
bhāvanāccoktamārgeṇa mānābhāvānna mucyate ।।
prakṛteḥ puruṣasyāpi viveko muktisādhanam ।
iti śaṅkayā na caitasmin mānamīśāprasādataḥ ।।
śrutayaḥ smṛtayaścaiva yadīśasya prasādataḥ ।
vadanti niyamānmuktiṃ tamṛte ataḥ kuto bhavet ।।
kaṇādayogākṣapādā apīśasya prasādataḥ ।
muktiṃ bruvāṇā apyāhurbhogādeva ca karmaṇām ।
kṣayaṃ prāhuḥ kutaścaitat prasanne jagadīśvare ।।
bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayāḥ ।
kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare ।।
bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayāḥ ।
kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi dṛṣṭa evātmanīśvare ।
iti śrutipurāṇādivacanebhyo anyathāgateḥ ।।
na ca pāśupatādyuktaśivādīnāmanugrahāt ।
nānyaḥ panthā iti hyuktaṃ puruṣajñānataḥ śrutau ।।
sarve nimeṣā jajñire vidyutaḥ puruṣādataḥ ।
evaṃ puruṣaśabdaśca prayukto abdhiśaye harau ।।
na tasyeśe kaścana tasya nāma mahad yaśaḥ ।
iti cādhipatistasya pratiṣiddhaḥ svayaṃ śrutau ।।
viśvataḥ paramāṃ nityaṃ viśvaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim ।
iti sarvādhikatvoktayā samo api vinivāritaḥ ।
samādhikasya rāhityānnopacārapumānasau ।।
puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yacca bhavyam ।
utāmṛtatvasyeśāno yadannenātirohati ।।
muktāmuktapareśatvamiti tasyāha sā śrutiḥ ।
amṛteśānavacanāt sarvasyeśānatoditā ।।
yadi sarvatvamuditamuteśa iti tad vṛthā ।
utaśabdo vadedeṣa hīśatvasya samuccayam ।।
puruṣeṇedaṃ vyāptamiti brāhmaṇaṃ cāha taṃ prati ।
etāvānasya mahimeti mahimno vaco hi tat ।।
so amṛtasyābhayasyeśo martyamannaṃ yadatyagāt ।
ityamuktādhipatyaṃ tu pūrvārdhoktamanūdya ca ।।
utāmṛtasyeśa iti vidhatte muktigeśatām ।
ato viṣṇuparijñānādeva muktirnacānyataḥ ।
tad yatheti śruteścaiva tataḥ karmakṣayo bhavet ।।
yathaidhāṃsi samiddho agnirbhasmasāt kurute arjuna ।
jñānāgniḥ sarvakarmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā ।।
sarvadharmān parityajya māmekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।
ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ ।
ityādibhagavadvākyairuktārthaścāvasīyate ।।
nityanaimittikaṃ karma kurvannanyat parityajan ।
mucyate saṃsṛteścaitadapyetena nirākṛtam ।
vidyaivetīmamevārthaṃ svayamevāha vedarāṭ ।।
vinā karma na mokṣaḥ syājjñānenetyapi sā śrutiḥ ।
nānyaḥ panthā iti hyeva nivārayati sādaram ।।
anyathopāsanamapi tamevamitivādinī ।
nivārayatyādareṇa na pratīka iti prabhuḥ ।।
andhaṃ tamaḥ praviśanti ye avidyāmupāsate ।
iti śrutivirodhācca nānyathopāsanaṃ bhavet ।।
na cāpyekatvavijñānāduktanyāyena mucyate ।
iti sarvaṃ pravijñāya sarvaistarkasadāgamaiḥ ।
upāsīta hariṃ nityaṃ guṇaireva svayogataḥ ।।
brahmā sarvaiguṇaiścaiva kriyāsāmānyataśca gīḥ ।
guṇasāmānyato rudro dravyasāmānyataḥ pare ।।
adhikāraviśeṣeṇa bhaktijñānasukhādibhiḥ ।
viśeṣo devatādīnāṃ mokṣe caiva viśeṣataḥ ।।
na tāvatā virodho asti nirdoṣatvāt samastaśaḥ ।
ābhāsatvāt pareṣāṃ tadavarāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
yato avarāṇāṃ sarve api guṇāḥ sarvāḥ kriyā api ।
niyamenaiva pūrveṣāṃ suprasādanibandhanāḥ ।
ataḥ sacchiṣyavat teṣāṃ naiverṣyādiḥ kathañcana ।।
na ca saṃsāridevānāṃ kāleyattāpare ime ।
sūtre hyārabdhamātrasya bhogenaiva kṣayo dhruvaḥ ।।
anārabdhakārye bhogena tvitare iti coditaḥ ।
paunaruktayena tenaite uktārthe iti niścayaḥ ।।
uṣāḥ svāhā ca parjanyo mitro agnirvaruṇo vidhuḥ ।
pravaho aniruddha indrome rudro vāṇī ca mārutaḥ ।
uttarottaratastvete guṇaiḥ sarvaiśca muktigāḥ ।।
sūryadharmau yathā somo manurdakṣo bṛhaspatiḥ ।
śacī ratiścāniruddhasamāstārā ca mitravat ।।
somavacchatarūpā tu prasūtirvahnivad virāṭ ।
parjanyavad vāruṇī ca tathā sañjñā ca rohiṇī ।।
dharmī ca mitravattvena prāvahī parikīrtitā ।
mitrapajarnyamadhyasthāvaśvinau vighnavittapau ।।
bhṛguragnisamo mitratanmadhye brahmaputrakāḥ ।
varuṇāgnyantarā tatra nāradaḥ prāya indravat ।।
kāmaḥ suparṇī comāvad vīndro rudravadīritaḥ ।
niṛtirmitrasadṛśo viśvāmitraḥ kasūnuvat ।।
vaivasvato manuścāśvipaścādanye tato avarāḥ ।
cyavanocathyavainyāśca śaśabinduśca haihayaḥ ।
tadvacca viprarājanyaviśeṣo atrāpi kaścana ।।
tadvat priyavrataścāpi tadanyāḥ śatadevatāḥ ।
pajarnyamitrāntarāḷe tadanye tu tato avarāḥ ।।
etebhyo abhyadhikā śrīrastu sadā muktā viśeṣataḥ ।
tatsamo nāsti paramo harireva nacāparaḥ ।।
saṃhitāyāṃ bṛhatyāṃ tu svayaṃ bhagavatoditam ।
tadetadakhilaṃ prāṇa āhaṅkārika eva ca ।
indrādanantaro dṛṣṭirapi yogyānusārataḥ ।।
samyag guruprasādaśca mukhyato dṛṣṭikāraṇam ।
śravaṇādi ca kartavyaṃ nānyathā darśanaṃ kvacit ।।
guṇādhikaṃ guruṃ prāpya taddhīnaṃ nāpnuyāt kvacit ।
viparyayastu kartavyaḥ sarvathā muktimicchatā ।।
same vikalpa eva syāt pūrvānujñā ca sarvathā ।
taduttamaguruprāptyai pūrvānujñā na mṛgyate ।।
gurubarrahmākhilānāṃ ca vidyā caiva sarasvatī ।
devatā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarveṣāmaviśeṣataḥ ।।
tatprasādena muktiḥ syānnānyathā tu kathañcana ।
svottamāstu krameṇaiva sarveṣāṃ guravaḥ śrutāḥ ।
upadeśo brahmaṇastu sarveṣāmeva muktaye ।।
sādhanebhyo adhikā bhaktirnaivānyat tādṛśaṃ kvacit ।
bhaktiścaiva harāveva mukhyānyatra yathākramam ।।
svādhikā tveva sarvatra svottameṣu krameṇa ca ।
anuvartate ca sā bhaktirmuktāvānandarūpiṇī ।
tatpūrvakopāsanaivaṃ kartavyā muktaye guṇaiḥ ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

evamutpannanirdoṣabhagavaddarśanāt sadā ।
apekṣitaphalaprāptirārabdhasyānatikramāt ।।
devarṣimānuṣādīnāṃ tattajjātyanusārataḥ ।
jaiminyuktaṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ tadviśeṣāśca kecana ।।
sāmānyaṃ bhagavatproktaṃ devādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
balavadvirodhisadbhāve jaiminyādyuktiriṣyate ।।
vikarmalepo naivāsti samyagdṛṣṭimatāṃ kvacit ।
guṇahāniśca naivāsti brahmaṇastvavikarmataḥ ।।
devānāmapi na prāyaḥ kḷptasya tu kathañcana ।
prāptahrāso bhavet kvāpi mahatā tu vikarmaṇā ।
tathāpi tat kḷptameva tasmānna niyamojkhitiḥ ।।
candrasugrīvayoścaiva svoccadāraparigrahāt ।
prāptahānirabhūnnaiva kḷptahāniḥ yathañcana ।।
hrāso api mānuṣādīnāmānandasya vikarmaṇā ।
bhavenmuktau viśeṣeṇa svoccānāmaparādhataḥ ।।
jñānottarasya pāpasya caturthe alepa ucyate ।
aśucitvādikaṃ tasya na bhavediti tatphalam ।
atra jñānaphalasyaiva mukterniyatatocyate ।।
prārabdhakarmajasyaiva viṣabhakṣānmṛteriva ।
prāptasyāpyanivartyasya kiñcid bhuktasya saṃvidā ।
upamarda iha prokto devādīnāṃ yathākramam ।।
sarvātmanā tvabhogo hi prārabdhasyaiva karmaṇaḥ ।
na brahmadarśino api syāt phalahrāsastu vidyate ।।
sarvātmanā phalahrāso yadi nārabdhakarmaṇaḥ ।
syāt kāmyavidhivaiyarthyamityuktaniyamo bhavet ।
evamadyāpi samproktaṃ tantrabhāgavate sphuṭam ।।
tāratamyaṃ phale no ced brahmādīnāṃ kathaṃ śrutiḥ ।
avṛjino akāmahata iti muktiṃ nigadya ca ।
ānandatāratamyaṃ ca teṣāṃ brūyāt pṛthak pṛthak ।।
saṃsāra eva cedetat tāratamyaṃ na mukhyataḥ ।
akāmahataśabdārtho avṛjinatvaṃ ca no bhavet ।।
kāmasya yatrāptāḥ kāmāstatra māmamṛtaṃ kṛdhi ।
iti yallakṣaṇaṃ mukteḥ śrutirāha balīyasī ।।
kāmāhatiḥ kuto anyatra prāptakāmasya sā bhavet ।
aprayatnena kāmānāmavāptiḥ sā yadā bhavet ।
tadaivākāmahatatā kuta evānyathā bhavet ।।
cetanasya tvasuptasya kutra dṛṣṭā hyakāmatā ।
avyaktireva kāmānāṃ na nāśo mohasuptayoḥ ।।
yatkāmaḥ svāpamāpnoti tadevotthāpitaḥ kutaḥ ।
avaśo api vyāharati kutaḥ suptāvakāmatā ।।
sarvakāmānavāpnoti brahmaṇā saha muktigaḥ ।
paryeti tatra jakṣaṃśca krīḍan ratimavāpnuvan ।।
kāmānnī kāmarūpī sannimān lokāṃśca sañcaran ।
āste gāyan sāma mukta ityādiśrutisadbalāt ।।
akāmaḥ syāt kathaṃ muktaḥ kāmā ye asya hṛdi śritāḥ ।
ityantaḥkaraṇasthānāṃ kāmānāṃ mokṣameva hi ।
āha śrutirhṛdītyeva na ced vyarthaṃ viśeṣaṇam ।।
hṛdyeṣa teṣāṃ śrayaṇamiti pakṣo na bhāsate ।
muktānāṃ kāmitāmāha pṛthakchākhāsu yacchrutiḥ ।।
ato akāmahatatvaṃ tu muktānāmeva mukhyataḥ ।
mukhyārthasya vṛthā tyāgo māyināmeva bhūṣaṇam ।।
apāpatvamaduḥkhatvaṃ cāvṛjinatvamihoditam ।
apriyaṃ vṛjinaṃ duḥkhamakaṃ toda itīyarte ।।
tatkāraṇatvāt pāpaṃ vā vṛjinaṃ nāma kathyate ।
ityuktaḥ svayamīśena nāmārthaḥ śabdanirṇaye ।।
apāpatvaṃ ca naivāsti yāvatsaṃsāramasya hi ।
ārabdhapāpamastyeva duḥkhaṃ ca jñānino api hi ।।
tasmāt tasmādakāmatvamiti cāśrutakalpanā ।
akāmahata ityukteḥ śrutahānirapi sphuṭā ।।
kutracit kāminaḥ puṃsaḥ kāmābhāvāt kvacit kvacit ।
indrādisukhabhogo astītyanubhūtirhi kupyati ।।
tasmādamuktasukhagaṃ tāratamyaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।
uktvā yaśceti muktānāṃ tāratamyaṃ sukhe śrutiḥ ।
āheti peśalaṃ tacca caśabdādeva gamyate ।।
rāddhaḥ saṃsiddha ityeva mukta evāvagamyate ।
sādhunā viṣṇunā yukto muktaḥ sādhuyuvā mataḥ ।।
yauvanaṃ nityametasya muktasyeti yuvā sa ca ।
phalamadhyayanasyāptaṃ tenādhyāyaka īritaḥ ।।
nirhrāsānandasamprāptyā cāśiṣṭa iti gīyate ।
sthitasyānanyathā prāpterdṛḍhiṣṭha iti coditaḥ ।।
baliṣṭhaśca svabhāvena mukto bhavati kevalam ।
tasyeyaṃ pṛthivītyādi pūrvabhāvavyapekṣayā ।।
sa eka iti saṃsāragatamuktavā sukhaṃ punaḥ ।
śrotriyasyeti vadati muktācchataguṇātmatām ।।
saṃsāragācca saṃsāragatasyaiva śatādhikam ।
muktānmuktasya yuktaṃ syācchrutyuktamabhivīkṣitaḥ ।।
yuktaṃ ca sādhanādhikyāt sādhyādhikyaṃ surādiṣu ।
nādhikyaṃ yadi sādhye syāt prayatnaḥ sādhane kutaḥ ।।
yatnaśca dṛśyate teṣāṃ mahāneva mahātmanām ।
yatra sādhanabāhulyaṃ sādhyabāhulyamatra ca ।
dṛṣṭaṃ niyamato no cenna yatnaṃ kuryarañjasā ।।
kṛcchreṇa sādhanādeva na muktavadudīryate ।
daśakalpaṃ tapaścīrṇaṃ rudreṇa lavaṇārṇave ।
tyaktavā sukhāni sarvāṇi kliṣṭena lavaṇāmbhasā ।।
śakreṇa varṣakoṭiśca dhūmaḥ pīto atiduḥkhataḥ ।
varṣāyutaṃ ca sūryeṇa tapo avākchirasā kṛtam ।।
suduḥkhena sukhaṃ tyaktavā dharmeṇākāśaśāyinā ।
pītā mayīcayo varṣasāhasramatisādaram ।।
atikṛcchreṇa kurvanti yatnaṃ brahmavido api hi ।
ityetadakhilaṃ mokṣaviśeṣābhāvataḥ katham ।।
daivī sampad vimokṣāya nibandhāyāsurī matā ।
iti mokṣaviśeṣaśca svayaṃ bhagavatoditaḥ ।।
tameva yūyaṃ bhajatātmavṛttibhirmanovacaḥkāyaguṇaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।
amāyinaḥ kāmadughāṅghripaṅkajaṃ yathādhikārāvasitārthasiddhaye ।।
akṣaṇvantaḥ karṇavantaḥ sakhāyo manojaveṣvasamā babhūvuḥ ।
ādaghnāsa upakakṣāsa u tve hradā iva snātvā u tve dadṛśre ।।
ityādīni ca vākyāni tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam ।
vyaktaṃ vadanti tat kena sāmyaṃ mukteṣu gamyate ।।
duḥkhādyabhāvasāmyaṃ ca sāmyavākyārtha īyate ।
bhaktayādiguṇasadbhāve hyatulyatvaṃ ca bhārate ।
uktaṃ sādhanavaiśeṣyamapi sarvatra kathyate ।।
durjñeyaṃ ghorarūpasya trailokyadhvaṃsinaḥ prabhoḥ ।
daivatairmunibhiḥ siddhairmahāyogibhireva ca ।।
nityayuktairmahābhāgairvimuktakleśasādhvasaiḥ ।
mahotsāhairmahādhairyaiḥ sattvasthairvyavasāyibhiḥ ।।
atītānāgatajñānaprabhavāpyayavedibhiḥ ।
śaucasvādhyāyasantoṣatapassatyadayānvitaiḥ ।।
kimu martyairbhayabhrāntidhvaṃsamoharujānvitaiḥ ।
alpāyurvīryadhīsattvavyavasāyaśrutivrataiḥ ।।
kastaṃ madāmadaṃ devaṃ madanyo jñātumarhati ।
brahmaiva kiñcijjānāti na tadanyo hi kaścana ।।
muktānāmapi siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ।
sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣvapi mahāmate ।।
iyaṃ visṛṣṭiryata ā babhūva yadi vā dadhe yadi vā na ।
yo asyādhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman tso aṅga veda yadi vā na veda ।।
yaḥ svātmamāyāvibhavaṃ svayaṃ gato nāhaṃ nabhasvāṃstamathāpare kutaḥ ।
brahmāpi yaṃ vetti naiveha samyaganye kuto devamunīndramartyāḥ ।।
namaste amitatattvāya dharmādīnāṃ ca sūtaye ।
nirguṇāya ca satkāṣṭhāṃ nāhaṃ vedāpare kutaḥ ।।
nāhaṃ parāyur ṛṣayo na marīcimukhyā jānanti yadviracitaṃ khalu sattvasaṅgāḥ ।
yanmāyayā muṣitacetasa īśadaityamartyādayaḥ kimuta śaśvadabhadravṛttāḥ ।।
ahaṃ mahendro nirṛtiḥ pracetāḥ somo agnirīśaḥ pavano arko viriñcaḥ ।
ādityaviśve vasavo atha sādhyā marudgaṇā rudragaṇāḥ sasiddhāḥ ।।
anye ca ye viśvasṛjo amareśā bhṛgvādayo aspṛṣṭarajastamaskāḥ ।
yasyehitaṃ na viduḥ spṛṣṭṛmāyāḥ sattvapradhānā api kiṃ tato anye ।।
savarsyādau smṛto brahmā tasmād devādanantaraḥ ।
jānāti devapravaraṃ bhūyaścāto adhikaṃ nṛpa ।।
na tvāmatiśayiṣyanti muktāvapi kathañcana ।
madbhaktiyogājjñānācca sarvānatiśayiṣyasi ।।
yathā bhaktiviśeṣo atra dṛśyate puruṣottame ।
tathā muktiviśeṣo api jñānināṃ liṅgabhedane ।।
sāyujyaṃ samanuprāptā api devādayo akhilāḥ ।
tāratamyāddhi tiṣṭhanti tāratamyaṃ hi sādhane ।।
manuṣyāṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaścid yatati siddhaye ।
yatatāmapi siddhānāṃ kaścinmāṃ vetti tattvataḥ ।।
ya imaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ madbhakteṣvabhidhāsyati ।
bhaktiṃ mayi parāṃ kṛtvā māmevaiṣyatyasaṃśayaḥ ।।
na ca tasmānmanuṣyeṣu kaścinme priyakṛttamaḥ ।
bhavitā na ca me tasmādanyaḥ priyataro bhuvi ।।
adhyeṣyate ca ya imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṃvādamāvayoḥ ।
jñānayajñena tenāhamiṣṭaḥ syāmiti me matiḥ ।।
śraddhāvānanasūyuśca śṛṇuyādapi yo naraḥ ।
so api muktaḥ śubhān lokān prāpnuyāt puṇyakarmaṇām ।।
dhyānenātmani paśyanti kecidātmānamātmanā ।
anye sāṅkhayena yogena karmayogena cāpare ।।
anye tvevamajānantaḥ śrutvānyebhya upāsate ।
te api cātitarantyeva mṛtyuṃ śrutiparāyaṇāḥ ।।
susūkṣmairapyaśeṣaiśca viśeṣaiḥ saha paśyati ।
svātmānaṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvarūpo api sarvadā ।।
savartra cānyadapyevaṃ tenādṛṣṭaṃ na hi kvacit ।
sarvatra sarvadaiveśaṃ paśyatyeva ramāpi tu ।।
natu sarvairviśeṣaistaṃ paśyantyapyanyato adhikam ।
svātmānamanyaccāśeṣaṃ paśyatyeva hi sarvadā ।।
brahmā tu sarvagaṃ paśyed guṇānapyato adhikam ।
natu sarveṣu kāleṣu tathā paśyatyamuktigaḥ ।।
muktastu sarvadā paśyet sarvagatvena cāpi tu ।
na ramāvad viśeṣāṇāṃ darśanaṃ śaknuyāt kvacit ।।
svātmānamanyacca sadā viśeṣairakhilairapi ।
paśyantyañjastathā vāṇī viśoṣāṃstāvato natu ।
traiguṇyāt parataḥ paśyed vyāptaṃ śataguṇaṃ harim ।।
giriśo garuḍaścaiva tamomātragataṃ harim ।
paśyed viśeṣānapi hi vāṇīdṛṣṭān na paśyati ।।
umā suparṇī ca mahattattvaṃ yāvat prapaśyati ।
rudradṛṣṭān viśeṣāṃśca naiva paśyet kadācana ।।
svarūpamanyarūpaṃ ca muktā devāḥ samastaśaḥ ।
jānantīndraśca kāmaśca brahma yāvadahaṅkṛtiḥ ।।
paśyanto manudakṣādyā buddhitattvasthitaṃ harim ।
paśyanti somasūryau tu manasthaṃ parameśvaram ।।
anye bhūtasthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ devāḥ paśyanti sarvadā ।
bahusāhasravarṣeṇa mahattattve kvacit kvacit ।।
anye caiva yathāyogyamaṇḍāntarvartinaṃ harim ।
śvetadvīpapatiṃ caiva hṛdyevānye tu kecana ।
kadācideva tatrāpi kecit paśyanti keśavam ।।
umā yāvadanantāṃśān pūrvadṛṣṭebhya eva tu ।
viśeṣān vāsudevasya paścāduktā vicakṣate ।।
śakrakāmādayaścaiva viśeṣān brahmaṇi sthitān ।
umādibhiḥ prabuddhebhyaḥ śatāṃśāneva cakṣate ।।
ityādivedasmṛtigavacanebhyo yathārthataḥ ।
tāratamyaṃ vimuktānāṃ sādhanānāṃ ca dṛśyate ।।
sādhyasādhanavairūpyamadṛṣṭaṃ kena kalpyate ।
vaiṣamyaṃ nirghṛṇatvaṃ ca tena syātāṃ parasya ca ।
sāpekṣatvāditi ca tau vidyādhīśena vāritau ।।
tāratamyāt sādhanānāṃ sādhyatādṛktavamīśataḥ ।
avaiṣamyādihetuḥ syāt sadaiva parameśvare ।।
svātantrye vidyamāne api sādhanādau pareśituḥ ।
apekṣyānādivaicitṛyaṃ na doṣa iti tadvacaḥ ।
nānāditvāditi hyuktamupapadyata ityapi ।।
apekṣyopāyavaiṣamyamupeyasya tathā sthitiḥ ।
mayā kayā viruddhā syād rājādāvapi dṛśyate ।।
tyāgo dṛṣṭasya cādṛṣṭakalpaneti suduṣkarau ।
māyibhyo anyena kenāpi tat kimanyaiśca vādibhiḥ ।।
māyino atrānugamyante śrutahānyaśrutagrahau ।
apyatra māyināṃ liṅge tat ke doṣāstato adhikāḥ ।।
niśśeṣagatadoṣāṇāṃ bahubhirjanmabhiḥ punaḥ ।
syādāparokṣyaṃ hi harerdveṣerṣyādistataḥ kutaḥ ।।
bhaveyuryadi cerṣyādyāḥ sameṣvapi kuto na te ।
tapyamānāḥ samān dṛṣṭvā dveṣerṣyādiyutā api ।
dṛśyante bahavo loke doṣā evātra kāraṇam ।।
yadi nirdoṣatā tatra kimādhikyena dūṣyate ।
yadyanyadarśanābhāvādīrṣyādirvinivāryate ।
adarśanādaratyādiḥ kathaṃ tena nivāryate ।।
brahmaṇo apyaratirdṛṣṭvā pūrvamekākinaḥ śrutau ।
naiva reme sa caikākī tasamānna ramate kvacit ।
dvitīyamaicchat tenāsāviti śrutaya ūdire ।।
yadīcchā tatra naivāstītyeva tat kalpyate mṛṣā ।
śrutyuktanirdoṣataiva kiṃ nāṅgīkriyate svayam ।।
tāratamyaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca śrutamevātihāya tu ।
aśrutā samatā kena kalpyate yuktimāninā ।।
kiṃ tanmānaṃ samatve te muktānāmupalabhyate ।
vṛthāyamāgrahaḥ kena śrutahānyaśrutagrahe ।।
mokṣe api tāratamyetaścetanatvāt purā yathā ।
ityukta uttaraṃ kiṃ te kalpanāmātravādinaḥ ।।
na ca duḥkhādikaṃ kalpyaṃ nirduḥkhatvaśruterbalāt ।
śokaṃ taratyātmavettā tīrṇaḥ sarvānaduḥkhabhāk ।।
yenānandyeva bhavati na śocati kadācana ।
kilbiṣaspṛt pituṣaṇiraraṃ hita iheśvaraḥ ।।
yaṃ yamantamabhiprepsuḥ sa saṅkalpād bhavediha ।
ityādiśrutayo mānaṃ nirduḥkhatvādisampadi ।।
ato duḥkhādyanumayā nāvakāśo atra labhyate ।
tāratamyānumā tena bhavennātiprasaṅginī ।।
śrutiyuktibalādevaṃ tāratamyaṃ vibhāvyate ।
muktāvapi tataḥ ke atra virodhaṃ kartumīśate ।।
anādiyogyatāṃ caiva kalivāṇīśvarāvadhim ।
ko nivārayituṃ śakto yuktayāgamabaloddhatām ।।
brahmaṇo anyatra ādhikyayuktaḥ kālo vivādavān ।
kālo hyayaṃ yathetyādi mānumāmānino bhavet ।।
anyaśabdo hariśrīsvasamebhyo anyavivakṣayā ।
prayukto naiva doṣāya rudrādiṣu ca yuktitaḥ ।।
uttamatvaṃ tu muktānāmapi na brahmaṇo bhavet ।
vyaktiḥ sukhasya tu bhavennatvādhikyaṃ sukhasya ca ।।
balajñānādhikatvaṃ ca tebhyo hi brahmaṇaḥ sadā ।
ādhikyasya tvanityatve na kiñcinmānamīyate ।।
śṛṇve vīra ugramugraṃ damāyannanyamanyamatinenīyamānaḥ ।
edhamānadviḷubhayasya rājā coṣkūyate viśa indro manuṣyān ।।
parā pūrveṣāṃ sakhyā vṛṇakti vitarturāṇo aparebhireti ।
anānubhūtīravadhūnvānaḥ pūrvītindraḥ śaradastartarīti ।।
divedive sadṛśīranyamardhaṃ kṛṣṇā asedhadapa sadmano jāḥ ।
ahan dāsā vṛṣabho vasnayantodavraje varcinaṃ śambaraṃ ca ।।
taṃ bhūtiriti devā upāsāñcakrire te babhūvustasmāddhāpyetarhi supto bhūbhrūrityeva praśvasityabhūtirityasurāste ha parābabhūvuḥ ।।
tad yathā peśaskarī peśaso mātrāmapādāyānyannavataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ tanuta evamevāyamātmedaṃ śarīraṃ nihatyāvidyāṃ gamayitavānyannavataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ kurute pitṛyaṃ pitṛyaṃ vā gāndharvaṃ vā daivaṃ vā prājāpatyaṃ vā brāhmaṃ vānyeṣāṃ vā bhūtānām ।।
prayānti paramāṃ siddhimaihikāmuṣmikīṃ drutam ।
yā na prāpyāsuraiḥ sarvairakṣayā kleśavarjitā ।
na tāṃ gatiṃ prapadyante vinā bhāgavatān narān ।।
avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanumāśritam ।
paraṃ bhāvamajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvaram ।।
moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ ।
rākṣasīmāsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohanīṃ śritāḥ ।।
mahātmānastu māṃ pārtha daivīṃ prakṛtimāśritāḥ ।
bhajantyananyamanaso jñātvā bhūtādimavyayam ।।
abhayaṃ sattvasaṃśuddhirjñānayogavyavasthitiḥ ।
dānaṃ damaśca yajñaśca svādhyāyastapa ārjavam ।।
ahiṃsā satyamakrodhastyāgaḥ śāntirapaiśunam ।
dayā bhūteṣvalolutvaṃ mārdavaṃ hrīracāpalam ।।
tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucamadroho nātimānitā ।
bhavanti sampadaṃ daivīmabhijātasya bhārata ।।
ḍambho darpo atimāśca krodhaḥ pāruṣyameva ca ।
ajñānaṃ cābhijātasya pārtha sampadamāsurīm ।।
māmātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto abhyasūyakāḥ ।
tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān ।
kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu ।।
āsurīṃ yonimāpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani ।
māmaprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yāntyadhamāṃ gatim ।।
dvividho bhūtasargo atra daiva āsura eva ca ।
viṣṇubhaktiparo daivo viparītastathā'suraḥ ।।
devānāṃ paramo dharmaḥ sadā yajñādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।
svādhyāyastattvaveditvaṃ viṣṇupūjāratiḥ smṛtiḥ ।।
daityānāṃ bāhuṣāḷitvaṃ mātsaryaṃ yuddhasatkriyā ।
nītiśāstrapraveditvaṃ śivapūjāratiḥ smṛtiḥ ।।
varṇāśramācāravattvaṃ svādhyāyo bhaktiracyute ।
śive sūrye tathā devyāṃ svabhāvo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
anādivaiṣṇavā eva devatāstu svabhāvataḥ ।
viparītāstato daityāḥ sadaivānādikālataḥ ।।
mānuṣā miśramatayo vimiśragatayo api ca ।
ityādivākyasandarbhe jñāyate anādiyogyatā ।।
yadyanādirviśeṣo na sāmprataṃ kathameva saḥ ।
adṛṣṭādeva cādṛṣṭaṃ svīkṛtaṃ savarvādibhiḥ ।।
ākasmiko viśeṣaścedadṛṣṭe kvacidiṣyate ।
sarvatrākasmikatvaṃ syānnādṛṣṭāpekṣatā bhavet ।
adṛṣṭāśced viśeṣo ayamanāditvaṃ kuto na tat ।।
nacānyabhedavad viṣṇau bhedastaddarśināmapi ।
dṛśyate pratyabhijñaiva bahurūpeṣu dṛśyate ।।
bahutvaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa na bhedena kathañcana ।
pratyabhijñā ca yeṣāṃ na te api tanmuṣyadṛṣṭayaḥ ।।
bhedaṃ naiva prapaśyanti bhedamanyebhya eva ca ।
paśyantyevaṃ haristeṣāṃ sandarśayati nānyathā ।।
evaṃ bṛhatsaṃhitāyāṃ vacanaṃ na purāṇagam ।
lokadarśanavādyeva vedarodhāya śaknuyāt ।।
aparīkṣitadṛṣṭiśca parīkṣāpūrvadarśanam ।
niṣeddhuṃ śaknuvādyeva vedarodhāya śaknuyāt ।।
na ca niścitabhedasya darśane asti purāṇagam ।
vākyaṃ kvaciddhi sammugdhadarśanaṃ tatra gamyate ।।
aparīkṣitamevātra vedhādikamadhīśituḥ ।
parīkṣādarśane naiva dṛśyate kenacit kvacit ।।
nirdoṣameva taṃ brahmā dadarśāśeṣarūpiṇam ।
nirdoṣameva rudro adrāṅ nirdoṣaṃ taṃ purandaraḥ ।।
nirdoṣāṇyasya rūpāṇi dṛṣṭānyevaṃ surottamaiḥ ।
anye sadoṣāḥ sarve api nirdoṣo harirekalaḥ ।
iti barkuśruteścaiva sadoṣaṃ nāsya darśanam ।।
aviddho viddhavad viṣṇurajāto jātavanmṛṣā ।
abaddho baddhavaccaiva darśayatyamitadyutiḥ ।
iti paiṅgiśrutiścaiva prāha nirdoṣatāṃ hareḥ ।।
aparīkṣitadṛṣṭayaiva sadoṣo dṛśyate hariḥ ।
parīkṣādarśane naiva dṛśyo doṣo hareḥ kvacit ।
iti paiṅgiśrutiścāha pramāṇaṃ hi parīkṣitam ।।
na parīkṣānavasthā syāt sākṣisiddhe tvasaṃśayāt ।
mānase darśane doṣāḥ syurnavai sākṣidarśane ।
sudṛḍho nirṇayo yatra jñeyaṃ tat sākṣidarśanam ।।
icchā jñānaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhabhayābhayakṛpādayaḥ ।
sākṣisiddhā na kaściddhi tatra saṃśayavān kvacit ।
yat kvacid vyabhicārī syād darśanaṃ mānasaṃ hi tat ।।
manaścakṣurdarśanāderapi yatraiva sākṣiṇā ।
prāmāṇyaṃ sugṛhītaṃ syāt tat parīkṣitadarśanam ।।
na jñānadṛṣṭimātreṇa prāmāṇyaṃ tasya dṛśyate ।
niyamena sukhādyeṣu prāmāṇyaṃ sākṣigocaram ।।
svaprāmāṇyaṃ sadā sākṣī paśyatyeva suniścayāt ।
jñānasya grāhakeṇaiva sākṣiṇā mānatāmiteḥ ।।
doṣābhāve pramāṇatvaṃ doṣābhāvasya sākṣiṇā ।
niścitatvaṃ kvaciccaiva svataḥ prāmāṇyamiṣyate ।।
ato na sarvamānānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ niścitaṃ bhavet ।
sākṣiṇā niścitaṃ yatra tat prāmāṇyasvalakṣaṇam ।।
na hi kaścit sukhādyeṣu saṃśayaṃ kurute janaḥ ।
nacaivākhilamānāni niścinotyakhilo janaḥ ।।
tasmādanubhavārūḍhaṃ kimarthamupalapyate ।
doṣābhāvādikaṃ caiva sākṣī samyak prapaśyati ।।
tat parīkṣitamānena na doṣo viṣṇavi kvacit ।
aparīkṣitadṛṣṭistu kasminnarthe na vidyate ।।
tat pratyakṣaviruddhārthe nāgamasyāpi mānatā ।
upajīvyamakṣajaṃ yatra tadanyatra viparyayaḥ ।।
laukike vyavahāre atra pratyakṣasyopajīvyatā ।
avatārādidaṣṭau syādāgamasyopajīvyatā ।।
āgamena hi viṣṇutvaṃ jñātvā doṣo atra kalpyate ।
na cet syāt doṣavānanyaḥ śāstrasiddhaṃ hi lakṣaṇam ।।
kasyacid doṣavattvaṃ syāditimātre akṣajaṃ bhavet ।
na viṣṇordeṣavattve hi pratyakṣaṃ vartate svataḥ ।।
kecit paśyanti doṣānityatrāpi syānnacākṣajam ।
paurāṇaṃ vākyamevātra tacchrutyaiva viruddhayate ।।
purāṇasyopajīvyaśca veda eva nacāparaḥ ।
tadvirodhe kathaṃ mānaṃ tat tatra ca bhaviṣyati ।।
aparīkṣitadṛṣṭiśca kathamevākṣajaṃ bhavet ।
yadyevaṃ devadattādibhramaḥ kiṃ nākṣajaṃ bhavet ।।
yāvacchakti parīkṣāyāmupajīvyasya bādhane ।
doṣo nāśodhite doṣa upajīvyatvamasvalam ।।
bhrame apyabhramabhāgo asti tanmātramupajīvya hi ।
bādhakajñānavṛttiḥ syānnacaivaṃ suparīkṣite ।
sarvaṃ tadupajīvyaiva pramāṇaṃ vartate yataḥ ।।
kathaṃ brahmeti tajjñeyaṃ sarvajñatvādilakṣaṇam ।
vihāya yasmātkasmāccit svarūpasyaiva ced yadi ।।
upajīvyatvametasmād vyāvṛttaṃ yāvatā bhavet ।
tāvataivopajīvyatvaṃ svarapasyaiva na kvacit ।।
sarvalakṣaṇayuktaṃ tu svarūpaṃ yadi bhaṇyate ।
astu no naiva hāniḥ syāt svapakṣaścāyamañjasā ।।
yasmādanvita evārthaḥ śabdānāmapi sarvaśaḥ ।
viśeṣasāmanyatayā svarūpamakhilaṃ bhavet ।।
purovartitvapūrvāṇi devadattādikabhrame ।
vyāvartayanti tadrūpaṃ caitramātrad vinaiva hi ।।
brahmaṇo nirviśeṣatvād vyāvartayati kiṃ punaḥ ।
yasmātkasmāccidapyarthāt tāvaccet siddhasādhanam ।।
cinmātratvaṃ ca naiveṣyamaviśeṣatvavādinaḥ ।
tāvanmātraṃ yadīṣyaṃ syāt sarvajñatvaṃ kuto na tat ।।
cinmātrābhedasādhye api siddhaṃ tat prativādinaḥ ।
svābhedāṅgīkṛtereva cittvaṃ svasyāpi yanmatam ।।
sarvāpekṣatayā sarvajñatvamityeva tannahi ।
iti ceccetanatvaṃ ca jñatvaṃ na jñeyavarjitam ।।
svajñeyatvaṃ ca naivāsau manyate saviśeṣataḥ ।
svaśabdo api parāpekṣastasmād vyāvṛttireva hi ।
svaśabdārtha iti proktaḥ svarūpaṃ nāma kiṃ na cet ।।
rūpaśabdena pūrṇatvāt tacca sāmānyatāvacaḥ ।
na svarūpābhidhāyi syād vaiyarthyaṃ svaravasya yat ।।
cetanasya svabhāvo hi caitanyamiti gīyate ।
tasmād viśeṣabāhulyaṃ caitanyasya viśeṣataḥ ।।
na jñeyajñātṛhīnaṃ hi jñānaṃ nāma kvacid bhavet ।
jñeyajñānavihīnaśca jña ityatra ca na pramā ।।
jñātṛjñeyavihīnaṃ ca jñānaṃ ced bhoktṛbhojyataḥ ।
hīnaṃ bhojanameva syāt tāḍanaṃ kartṛtāḍyataḥ ।।
nityatvāt tādṛśaṃ ca syāditi cennityavāgapi ।
vācyavaktṛvihīnā syānnahi sā caiva tādṛśī ।।
draṣṭāro vedavāco hi santi vācyāni cāñjasā ।
nityo draṣṭā ca vācyaśca bhagavāneva ca svayam ।।
na hi vaktṛvihīnā ca vācyahīnāpi vāk kvacit ।
jñātṛjñeyavihīnaṃ ca jñānamevaṃ na tad bhavet ।।
na hi nityo api vaktāsti vākyavācyavivarjitaḥ ।
jñānajñeyavihīnaśca jño apyevaṃ naiva vidyate ।।
kiñca sarvavilopaśca kena mānena gamyate ।
sarveṇa saha tad vākyāmarthaśca yadi gṛhyate ।
tadabhāvena sarvasya nāpalāpo bhavet tadā ।।
na gṛhyate ced tannyāyādapalāpo na hi kvacit ।
upapattivihīnasya vākyasyārtho na gamyate ।।
upakramādiliṅgānāṃ balīyo hyuttarottaram ।
śrutyādau pūrvapūrvaṃ ca brahmatarkavinirṇayāt ।।
pratyakṣamupapattiśca bahavaścāgamā yadā ।
viruddhayante nacārtho asti yatra liṅgavirodhitā ।।
sa evārthaḥ kathaṃ grāhya upapanne avirodhinī ।
mukhyārthe vidyamāne tu kva sāvarjñyaṃ niṣiddhayate ।।
ataḥ sarvaguṇairyuktaṃ brahmāṅgīkāyarmeva hi ।
apalāpo api sarvasya na kathañcana yujyate ।।
anādiyogyatā coktā tena grāhyaiva sarvathā ।
muktānāṃ tāratamyaṃ ca mānairuktairna cālyate ।।
jñānino api yato nityaṃ kurvanti śubhameva hi ।
tāratamyaṃ tu muktau ca tenaivādhyavasīyate ।।
tāratamyaṃ na cenmuktau kutaḥ kuryuḥ śubhaṃ punaḥ ।
kṛcchreṇāpi tapo jñānaṃ karmāpyete caranti hi ।।
bibhyati smāśubhānnityaṃ sakāmāśca śubhe sadā ।
na ca svabhāva evāyaṃ bhayapūrvapravṛttitaḥ ।
kṛcchreṇācaraṇāccaiva śubhasyaiva punaḥ punaḥ ।।
tādṛśo api svabhāvaścedajñasyāpi bhavet tathā ।
phalavattve pramāṇaṃ cet tatra jñasya samaṃ hi tat ।।
niṣkāmaṃ jñānapūrvaṃ ca nivṛttamiha cocyate ।
nivṛttaṃ sevamānastu brahmābhyeti sanātanam ।।
śubhenānandavṛddhi syādghrāsaścaivāśubhena hi ।
jñānino api yatastena kartavyaṃ śubhameva taiḥ ।।
upāste sa ya ātmānaṃ kṣīyate nāsya karma ha ।
asmāddhayevātmano yadyat kāmayet sṛjate ca tat ।।
avidvān bahukarmāpi hyantavat phalamāpnuyāt ।
yadeva vidyayā kuryāt tadeva hyativīryavat ।
ityādivākyasāmarthyāt tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam ।।
nacātropāsakasyaiva phalamakṣayamucyate ।
na hi jñānaṃ vinā kvāpi phalasyākṣayatā bhavet ।
jñānadvāreṇa cet tasya nāsmatpakṣapratīpatā ।।
jñānottarasyaivamapi hyakṣayatvaṃ nacānyathā ।
pūrvabhāviśubhānāṃ hi jñānenaiva kṛtārthatā ।।
prārabdhānāṃ tu bhogena tajjñānottarakarmaṇām ।
muktāvanupraveśaḥ syādanyathā tatkṛtirnahi ।।
jñānāt pūrvāṇi sarvāṇi śubhāni jñānasiddhaye ।
akāmyāni niṣiddhāni jñānarodhāya bhuktaye ।।
yogyatāyā balād yacca śubhabāhulyamāditaḥ ।
jñānabāhulyamevaitat kuryānnānyasya kāraṇam ।।
jñānasya bhaktibhāgatvād bhaktirjñānamitīryate ।
jñānasyaiva viśeṣo yad bhaktirityabhidhīyate ।।
parokṣatvāparokṣatve viśeṣau jñānagau yathā ।
snehayogo api tadvat syād viśeṣo jñānagocaraḥ ।।
ityābhiprāyataḥ prāyo jñānameva vimuktaye ।
vadanti śrutayaḥ so ayaṃ viśeṣo api hyudīryate ।।
bhaktirjñānamiti kvāpi na hi dveṣayutā dṛśiḥ ।
puruṣārthāya bhavati sarvaśrutivirodhataḥ ।।
cetanasya dvayaṃ bhogyaṃ saṃsāro muktireva ca ।
saṃsārastrividhastatra svargo madhyamadhastathā ।।
muktiśca dvividhā tatra sukhaṃ nityaṃ tathāparam ।
nityaduḥkhamiti jñeyaṃ sādhanaṃ saṃsṛtāvapi ।
kāmyaṃ karma niṣiddhaṃ ca sājñānamiti niścayaḥ ।।
dveṣo bhaktiśca muktau tu muktidvayavidhāyakam ।
iti paiṅgiśruterdveṣo naiva sanmuktikāraṇam ।।
asanmukteḥ kāraṇaṃ ca muktāvityatra keśavaḥ ।
muktiśabdodito mokṣaṃ svabhaktānāṃ karoti yat ।।
dveṣato api vimuktiścenmahātātparyarodhanam ।
bhaktayā prasannato devānmuktirityeva tadguṇān ।
vadanti śrutayaḥ sarvāḥ purāṇānyāgamā api ।।
yadi dveṣeṇa muktiḥ syād vaktavyo doṣasañcayaḥ ।
smartavyo bhagavān nityamityarthenaiva hi kvacit ।
dveṣādiva guṇānāha purāṇe kruddhavākyavat ।।
yathā kruddhaḥ pitā putraṃ maretyākṣepapūrvakam ।
proktasyānyasya kṛtyarthaṃ vadatyevaṃ purāṇagam ।।
vākyaṃ śrutivirodhena svavirodhena cāñjasā ।
bahvāgamavirodhācca na dveṣānmuktivācakam ।।
tamo dveṣeṇa saṃyānti bhaktayā muktiṃ tathaiva ca ।
viṣṇau viṣṇuprasādena vilomatvena cāñjasā ।
iti ṣāḍguṇyavacanamapyuktārthaniyāmakam ।।
mahātātparyarodhe ca kathaṃ vākyaṃ pramāṇatām ।
yāti sarvārtharūpaṃ hi mahātātparyamiṣyate ।।
vācakatvaṃ hi tātparyaṃ yadarthā akhilā ravāḥ ।
so arthaḥ kathaṃ parityājya ekaśabdasya saṃśaye ।
ato vijñānabhaktibhyāṃ puruṣārthaḥ paro bhavet ।।
yasya deve parā bhaktiryathā deve tathā gurau ।
tasyaite kathitā hyarthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ ।।
bhaktyā jñānaṃ tato bhaktistato dṛṣṭistataśca sā ।
tato muktistato bhaktiḥ saiva syāt sukharūpiṇī ।।
bhaktayā prasanno bhagavān dadyājjñānamanākulam ।
tayaiva darśanaṃ yātaḥ pradadyānmuktimetayā ।।
nāhaṃ vedairna tapasā na dānena nacejyayā ।
śakya evaṃvidho draṣṭuṃ pradadyānmuktimetayā ।।
bhaktayā tvananyayā śakya ahamevaṃvidho arjuna ।
jñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca tattvena praveṣyuṃ ca parantapa ।।
ityādivākyataścaiva so ayamuktārtha īyate ।
na ca prasādamāpnoti dveṣād bhaktyā tamāpnuyāt ।
iti dṛṣṭānusāritvamapyasminnartha īyate ।।
ye pṛthag vihitā viṣṇorguṇā vedena sādaram ।
ta eva dṛṣṭavailomyādaṅgīkāryā nacāparam ।।
anyad dṛṣṭānusāreṇa vāsudeve api gṛhyate ।
doṣābhāvāśca ye vedairuditā avihāya tān ।।
anuktā apica grāhyā mahātātparyaśaktitaḥ ।
evaṃ bṛhatsaṃhitāvāk siddhānto hi tadīritaḥ ।।
tāratamyena tadbhakteṣvapi bhaktirviniścayāt ।
kartavyaiṣāpi tadbhaktirlokavedānusārataḥ ।।
yo hi bhaktaḥ pradhāne syāt tadīyeṣvapi bhaktimān ।
dṛśyate asau niyamato viparīto viparyaye ।।
vyabhicāro yadi kvāpi bhaktihrāso atra kalpyate ।
bhaktidoṣo hyasau yanna tadbhakteṣvapi bhaktimān ।।
tāratamyena teṣvaddhā bhaktirdṛṣṭānusārataḥ ।
viṣṇuprasādānusārāt kāryā doṣastadanyathā ।।
svaprītyanusṛtau prītirloke apyaddhaiva dṛśyate ।
tāratamyaparijñānamapyetenaiva sādhanam ।।
lakṣmīviriñcavāṇīśagirijendrāṅgirassutāḥ ।
sūryādayaśca kramaśo bhagavatprītigocarāḥ ।।
teṣu bhaktiḥ krameṇaiva kāryā nityaṃ mumukṣubhiḥ ।
sarve api guravaścaite puruṣasya sadaiva hi ।।
tasmāt pūjyāśca namyāśca dhyeyāśca parito harim ।
iti ṣāḍguṇyavacanādapyeṣo artho avasīyate ।।
haribhaktiḥ krameṇaiva tadīyeṣu harismṛtiḥ ।
haristutistatsmṛtiśca tatstutirharipūjanam ।।
tatpūjāvihitatyāga iti mukteḥ krameṇa hi ।
niyamāt sādhanānyeva nityasādhyāni cākhilaiḥ ।।
iti pravṛttavacanaṃ sādhanasya vinirṇaye ।
pravṛtte pañcarātre hi sādhanasyātiniścayaḥ ।।
haridveṣo na śubhada ;saddveṣatvād yathā guroḥ ।
kramād bhaktirhariprītikāraṇaṃ tatpriyaupagā ।
bhaktiryato yathā svasminnityādyā yuktiratra ca ।।
prādhānyatāratamyānusāriṇī bhaktiruttamā ।
prītidaiva hareryasmād bhaktiḥ sā svopagā yathā ।।
iti vā jñānakarmādiphalaṃ caiṣu kramopagam ।
svātantryatāratamyena phalaṃ hi phalināṃ bhavet ।।
aśubhaṃ tvaśubhe apyeṣāṃ svātantryāt prītito hareḥ ।
ājñayā cānyagaṃ naiva bhogāya bhavati kvacit ।।
puṇyamevāmumāpānoti na devān pāpamāpnuyāt ।
ityādiśrutayo mānamukte arthe yuktayo aparāḥ ।।
upāsanādharmaphalaṃ yato dehāntare sthitiḥ ।
vāsudevājñayā caiva pūrvakarmānusārataḥ ।।
prerayanti hi te jīvān puṇyapāpeṣu nityaśaḥ ।
arāgadveṣataścaiva kathaṃ doṣānavāpnuyuḥ ।।
haryājñākaraṇādeva puṇyamebhiravāpyate ।
haripūjeti coddeśāt kathaṃ na śubhamāpnuyuḥ ।।
ato yathākramaṃ dharmajñānayoḥ phalamañjasā ।
sarvaprāṇigataṃ devāḥ prāpnuvantyā viriñcataḥ ।।
devā eva hi devānāṃ viśiṣṭā viniyāmakāḥ ।
brahmā tvakhiladevānāṃ narāṇāṃ ca niyāmakaḥ ।
ataḥ sarvaguṇāneṣa prāpanotyadhikamanyataḥ ।।
dravyasvātantryavijñānaprayatnairadhikaṃ phalam ।
devānāmanyagaṃ cāpi teṣu yad brahmaṇo hi tat ।।
bṛhattantroditaṃ vākyaṃ hariṇā phalanirṇaye ।
loke apyetādṛśaguṇaiḥ phalādhikyaṃ hi dṛśyate ।।
evañca kalipūrvāṇāmasurāṇāṃ mahat phalam ।
aśubheṣu sadaiva syānmithyājñānādikeṣu hi ।।
śubhāśubhaphalaṃ devā asurāśca samāpnuyuḥ ।
krameṇaiva yathāśakti yathā ye ye prayojakāḥ ।।
prerakā api pāpānāṃ na devāḥ pāpamāpnuyuḥ ।
iti prakāśikāyāṃ hi provāca harirañjasā ।।
yadyapyevaṃ surāṇāṃ ca daityānāṃ ca mahat phalam ।
śubhāśubhebhya evañca kartuśca syād yathoditam ।।
tasmānnirayamānuṣyasvargamuktyupabhoginaḥ ।
mānuṣottamamārabhya devāstu nirayaṃ vinā ।।
asurāstu vinā muktiṃ tamo andhamapi cāpnuyuḥ ।
iti tattvavivekoktaṃ svayaṃ bhagavatā vacaḥ ।।
jñānadā apicācāryā viśeṣāt phalamāpnuyuḥ ।
muktāvaṣṭaguṇaṃ śiṣyād gururāpanoti śobhanam ।।
tadgururdviguṇaṃ tasmāt sārdhaṃ tāvat tato apare ।
devāḥ sahasraguṇitaṃ kramāt tasmād yathottaram ।।
brahmā mahaughaguṇitamevaṃ phalavinirṇayaḥ ।
ityāha bhagavāñchāstre guruvṛttābhidhe svayam ।
yuktaṃ ca tanna godātā gomātraphalamāpnuyāt ।।
ya imaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ madbhakteṣvabhidhāsyati ।
bhaktiṃ mayi parāṃ kṛtvā māmevaiṣyatyasaṃśayaḥ ।।
na ca tasmānmanuṣyeṣu kaścinme priyakṛttamaḥ ।
bhavitā na ca me tasmādanyaḥ priyataro bhuvi ।
ityāha bhagavānevamapi pātramapekṣyate ।।
evamevāvirodhena prārabdhasyaiva karmaṇaḥ ।
jñānaṃ dṛṣṭaphalaṃ proktaṃ muktiścehaiva labhyate ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ ।।

samanvayāvirodhābhyāṃ siddhe vastuni sādhane ।
vicāriteṣvaśeṣeṣu sādhaneṣu viśeṣataḥ ।।
nityaśaḥ kāryamatyantamavaśyaṃ bhāvi sādhanam ।
cintyate prathamaṃ tatra śravaṇādisakṛtkriyā ।।
āvṛttirveti sandehe kartavyā'vṛttireva hi ।
upadeśo atat tvamasītyādirhyasakṛdeva yat ।।
liṅgāllātavyataḥ pūrvamṛjobarrahmatvataḥ śatāt ।
śuśrāvogratapā nāma yogyo rudrapadasya yaḥ ।।
sārddhaṃ parārddhaṃ viṣṇostu guṇān bhaktayā sadodyataḥ ।
tattribhāgamupāsāṃ ca cakre sambhṛtamānasaḥ ।।
daśamanvantaraṃ śakrapadayogyo garutmataḥ ।
padayogyāt sumanasaḥ sunando nāma cāśṛṇot ।
upāsāṃ cakra udyukto manvantaracatuṣyayam ।।
sūryācandramasoścaiva padayogyau sutejasau ।
surūpaḥ śāntarūpaśca manvantaracatuṣyayam ।
aśṛṇvatāṃ sumanaso manvantaramupāsatām ।।
tataḥ proktāstu te sarve bhaktayogratapaādayaḥ ।
apaśyan paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ tatprasādedhitāḥ sadā ।
ityuktaṃ viṣṇunā sākṣād granthe sattatvasañjñite ।।
ātmeti nāma kathitaṃ sākṣānnārāyaṇasya hi ।
ātmā brahma mahāṃstāraḥ parameśaḥ śuciśravāḥ ।।
viṣṇurnārāyaṇo ananta iti śrīpatirīryate ।
