iti piṅgaśrutiścaiva tathaiva paramaśrutiḥ ।।
omātmā bhagavān viṣṇurātmānando akṣaraḥ svarāṭ ।
viśvatrātā nṛsiṃho ajo nārāyaṇa urukramaḥ ।।
anasūyā tathaivātrerjajñe putrānakalmaṣān ।
dattaṃ durvāsasaṃ somamātmeśabrahmasambhavān ।।
iti bhāgavate caiva tasmādātmā janārdanaḥ ।
tasmādupāsyo viṣṇuriti jñātavyaḥ sajjanaiḥ sadā ।।
tathaivopāsate santastathaivopadiśanti ca ।
ādānārthatvataścāyamātmaśabdaḥ patiṃ vadet ।
svāmī me viṣṇurityeva nityadopāsyamañjasā ।।
svāmī viṣṇuriti dhyānaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyataḥ ।
kartavyaṃ sarvathaivaitanna kathañcana vismaret ।।
iti sattattvavacanaṃ ṣāḍguṇyavacanaṃ param ।
mama svāmī harirnityaṃ sarvasya patireva ca ।
iti dhyeyaḥ sarvadaiva bhagavān viṣṇuravyayaḥ ।।
pratīkaviṣayatvena na kāryā viṣṇubhāvanā ।
pratīkaṃ naiva viṣṇuryanmithyopāsā hyanathardā ।।
yo anyathā santamātmeśamanyathā pratipadyate ।
kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇātmāpahāriṇā ।।
yo anyathā santamātmānamanyathā pratipadyate ।
kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇeśāpahāriṇā ।।
yo anyathaiva sthitaṃ viṣṇumanyathā pratipadyate ।
kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇa brahmacāriṇā ।।
svātmānaṃ pratimāṃ vāpi devatāntarameva vā ।
cetanācetanaṃ vānyad dhyāyed yaḥ keśavastviti ।
kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ cāreṇeśāpahāriṇā ।।
yo anyad viṣṇuriti dhyāyejjānīyād vā hariṃ tathā ।
andhe tamasi majjet sa yatra naivotthitiḥ kvacit ।।
yo anyad viṣṇuriti dhyāyed viṣṇuranyaditi sma vā ।
anyathā dhyānadoṣeṇa mahātamasi majjati ।।
yo anyad viṣṇuriti dhyāyed viṣṇuranyaditi sma vā ।
mahātamasi magnasya tasya naivotthitiḥ kvacit ।।
yatkiñcidanyathā saṃsthamanyathā dhyātamañjasā ।
dhyāturmahādoṣakaraṃ kimu sarveśvaro hariḥ ।।
yatkiñcidanyathā saṃsthamanyathā jñātamañjasā ।
mahādoṣakaraṃ viṣṇuḥ kimu sarveśvareśvaraḥ ।।
yatkiñcidanyathā saṃsthamanyathā jñātamañjasā ।
anarthakāraṇaṃ loke kimu sarveśvareśvaraḥ ।।
na kiñcidanyathā jñeyaṃ dhyeyaṃ vā tena kutracit ।
kimu sarvottamo viṣṇurjñeyo nīcatayā kvacit ।।
tasmād vastu yathārūpaṃ jñeyaṃ dhyeyaṃ ca sarvadā ।
kāraṇaṃ puruṣārthasya nānyathā bhavati kvacit ।।
iti śrutipurāṇoktibalato na pratīkatā ।
dhyeyā viṣṇoḥ kvacid yasmānmithyājñānamanarthadam ।।
ityabhipretya na hi sa ityāha bhagavān prabhuḥ ।
pratīkasaṃsthitatvena dhyeyo viṣṇurnacānyathā ।।
brahmeti ca sadā dhyeyo bhagavān viṣṇurañjasā ।
utkṛṣṭo brahmaśabdārthaḥ pūrṇatvaṃ brahmatā yataḥ ।।
ādhivyādhinimittena vikṣiptamanaso api tu ।
dhyeyaiva brahmatā nityaṃ viṣṇorbhaktayā nirantaram ।
iti prakāśikāyāṃ ca vacanaṃ viṣṇuneritam ।।
nātmeti sūtramīśasya jīvatvapratipādakam ।
ātmaśabdaṃ yato hetuṃ kṛtvā jīvaṃ nyavārayat ।
svaśabdāt prāṇabhṛccaiva nokta ityeva vedarāṭ ।।
yadyātmaśabdo jīve api kathaṃ sa vinivārayet ।
ātmaśabdoditastasmād viṣṇureva nacāparaḥ ।।
ātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāstamṛte viṣṇumavyayam ।
na vadanti yato nāptā kvāpi tairguṇapūrṇatā ।
nārāyaṇādhyātmagatamiti yad vaiṣṇavaṃ vacaḥ ।।
yadi jīveśayorvedapatiraikyaṃ ca manyate ।
ātmaśabdaṃ kathaṃ tasmānnivārayati yuktitaḥ ।।
bhedasya vyapadeśaṃ ca sthitiṃ cādanameva ca ।
bhedadārḍhye hetumāha satātparyaṃ jagatpatiḥ ।।
vyāvahārikabhedaścet kvāsāvavyāvahārikaḥ ।
vyāvahārikamityeva vacanaṃ vyāvahārikam ।।
uta neti vikalpe tu yadi syād vyāvahārikam ।
tasyāpi bādhyatā cet syād bhedaḥ syāt pāramārthikaḥ ।।
avyāvahārikatvaṃ ced bhedo ayaṃ satyatāṃ gataḥ ।
ekasyāsatyatāyāṃ hi dvayoreva viruddhayoḥ ।
anyasya satyataiva syāditi kena nivāryate ।।
asatyaṃ noktamityukte satyamuktamiti prajāḥ ।
jānantyuktaṃ tu no satyamityukte asatyatāmapi ।।
na svapne api dvayaṃ mithyā tatraikaṃ satyameva hi ।
bhāvābhāvāvubhau tatra kathaṃ mithyā bhaviṣyataḥ ।।
bhāvasya hi niṣedhe tu nābhāvasya niṣedhanam ।
svavāco asatyatā cet syāt tasmād bhedasya satyatā ।।
tasmājjīveśayorbheda uktanyāyena gamyate ।
etasmādātmaśabdo ayaṃ paramātmābhidhā bhavet ।।
pratīkaviṣayatvena viṣṇudṛṣṭirna tad bhavet ।
pratīke viṣṇurityeva tasmāt kāryā hyupāsanā ।।
na ca viṣṇuḥ pratīkaṃ yat tasmānnātmetyupāsanā ।
iti pakṣo yadā brahmadṛṣṭiścātra viruddhayate ।
sa neti yuktistatrāpi sametyuktaviruddhatā ।।
yadyapyutkarṣamātreṇa hyatadbhave apyupāsanā ।
utkarṣa ātmano api syāccetanatvādacetanāt ।
tasamādatattvaṃ nopāsyamiti vedavido matam ।।
utkarṣād brahmatādhyāne yadi syāt phalamañjasā ।
brahmaṇo nīcatādhyānādanarthaḥ kiṃ na jāyate ।।
acetanasya brahmatvadhyāne tuṣyirnahi kvacit ।
nīcasya svātmatādhyāne kupyati brahma lokavat ।।
caṇḍālo nṛpa ityukte nṛpaścaṇḍāla ityapi ।
ko viśeṣaḥ parijñāte nṛpeṇa syāt kathañcana ।।
purato naradevasya caṇḍālo yadi pūjyate ।
rājavat kiṃ na kopaḥ syād rājño loke hi paśyati ।।
rājñastu purataḥ prokte caṇḍālaṃ nṛpa ityapi ।
ātmānaṃ sa iti proktamitivaddhayeva kupyati ।।
abhede naitayordhyāne ko viśeṣo vacasyapi ।
ayaṃ rājā tvamityukte caṇḍāle atha nṛpe api ca ।
caṇḍāla iti tu prokte samameva hi dūṣaṇam ।।
dhyāte tvekasya tadbhāve tadbhāvo anyasya kiṃ na tat ।
nacaiva tadavijñātaṃ sarvajñabrahmaṇā kvacit ।।
tasmādapeśalaṃ sarvamanyasya brahmatāvacaḥ ।
tasmād yathoktamārgeṇa brahmopāsyaṃ mumukṣubhiḥ ।।
tathopāsyāñjasā dṛṣṭaṃ brahma pāpaṃ ca bhasmasāt ।
karoti nikhilaṃ pūrvaṃ pāścāttyasyāpyasaṅgatām ।
karoti taddviṣaścaivaṃ puṇyanāśo apyasaṅgatā ।।
yadeva vidyayetyatra pūrvoktāddhi viśiṣṭate ।
pūrvaṃ svargādilabdhyarthaṃ vīryavattvena coditam ।
karma vidyāyutaṃ paścānmokṣe vīryapradaṃ tviti ।।
tato bhogena puṇyaṃ ca kṣapayitvetarat tathā ।
brahmadviḍ brahmadarśī ca tamomokṣāvavāpnutaḥ ।।
brahmāṇaṃ śatakālāttu pūrvamārabdhasaṅkṣayaḥ ।
brahmaṇastveva tāvattvaṃ pañcāśad brahmaṇastathā ।
rudrasya viṃśadeva syādindrasyārkādike daśa ।।
anyeṣāṃ brahmamātrasya tvanta ārabdhasaṅkṣayaḥ ।
brahmaṇaiva sahātaśca paraṃ nārāyaṇaṃ vrajet ।
iti sattattvavacanaṃ svayaṃ bhagavatoditam ।।
।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne caturthādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।

devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāmetāvat samameva hi ।
utkrāntimārgau devānāṃ na prāyeṇa bhaviṣyataḥ ।।
karmakṣayasatathotkrāntirmārgo bhogaścatuṣyayam ।
phalaṃ mokṣa iti proktaḥ kramāt pādeṣu coditaḥ ।।
sraṣṭṛṣveva tu sṛjyānāṃ praveśo brahmaṇo laye ।
devānāṃ mārga uddiṣṭo nārcirādirnacotkramaḥ ।।
sraṣṭustu grāsabhūtasya dehastatra layaṃ vrajet ।
yataḥ sṛjyasya devasya naivotkrāntistato bhavet ।।
layāccaivārcirādīnāṃ lokānāmapi sarvaśaḥ ।
kathaṃ mārgo bhavet teṣāṃ viśatāmuttamaṃ svataḥ ।।
jātānāṃ mānuṣe loke devānāṃ ca kadācana ।
utkrāntimārgau bhavato na tadā muktiriṣyate ।।
anyeṣāmapi sākṣāttu muktiḥ prāpyāpi taṃ harim ।
sahaiva brahmaṇā bhūyāditi śāstrasya nirṇayaḥ ।।
kṣmāmbhonalānilaviyanmanaindriyārthabhūtādibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ pratisañjighṛkṣuḥ ।
avyākṛtaṃ viśati yarhi guṇatrayātmā kālaṃ paraṃ svamanubhūya paraḥ svayambhūḥ ।।
evaṃ paretya bhagavantamanupraviṣṭā ye yogino jitamarunmanaso virāgāḥ ।
tenaiva sākamamṛtaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ brahma pradhānamupayāntyagatābhimānāḥ ।।
bhagavantamanuprāptā api tu brahmaṇā saha ।
paramaṃ mokṣamāyānti liṅgabhaṅgena yoginaḥ ।।
prāptā api paraṃ devaṃ sahaiva brahmaṇā punaḥ ।
ānandavyaktiyāyānti pūrṇāṃ liṅgasya bhaṅgataḥ ।।
iti śrutipurāṇoktibalād vijñāyate ca tat ।
bhogastu sarvadevānāṃ narādīnāṃ ca vidyate ।।
tatra praveśo devānāmuttarottarataḥ kramāt ।
ucyate dehagānāṃ ca vṛttīnāmevameva tu ।।
tatra mokṣasvarūpaṃ tu vādinaḥ pratibhāśrayāt ।
nānā vadanti puṃsāṃ hi matayo guṇabhedataḥ ।
pṛthak pṛthak prajāyante tamasaivānyathāmatiḥ ।।
rajasā miśrabuddhitvaṃ sattvenaiva yathā matiḥ ।
guṇātītā vimuktānāṃ matiḥ śuddhacitiryataḥ ।।
sāmyagevātha nityā ca tattanmāhātmyayogataḥ ।
bahaḷā cātiviśadā spaṣṭā caiva śriyo matiḥ ।।
mahāśuddhacititvena tato apyatimahācitiḥ ।
aśeṣoruviśeṣāṇāmatispaṣṭatayā dṛśiḥ ।
nityamekaprakārā ca nārāyaṇamatiḥ parā ।।
sūryaprabhāvadakhilaṃ bhāsayanti nirantarā ।
nirlepā vītadoṣā ca nityamevāvikāriṇī ।।
viśeṣāṃsatadgatāṃstyaktavā prāyastallakṣaṇā śriyaḥ ।
tathaiva spaṣṭatābhāvāt tattantratvācca kevalam ।
na tādṛśī brahmaṇastu prāya eva śriyo yathā ।।
muktānāṃ tu tadanyeṣāṃ samudrataraḷopamā ।
agnijvālāvadeva syāt smṛtigānāṃ dṛśo bhavaḥ ।।
evaṃvidheṣu jñāneṣu tamasā muṣyadṛṣṭayaḥ ।
khadyotasadṛśātyalpajñānatvādanyathādṛśaḥ ।
vadanti vādino mokṣaṃ nānāmatasamāśrayāt ।।
āśritya pratibhāmāha jinastatrātitāmasīm ।
jñānāt karmakṣayānmokṣo bhaved dehākhyapañjarāt ।।
pañjaronmuktakhagavadalākākāśagocaraḥ ।
nityamūrdhvaṃ vrajatyeva pudgalo hastapādavān ।।
iti tat kena mānena mokṣarūpaṃ pradṛśyate ।
gatirūrdhvā ca duḥkhetā gatitvāllaukikī yathā ।
ityukte cānumānaikaśaraṇasya kimuttaram ।।
anūrdhvagatitā tatra yadyupādhiḥ khagasya ca ।
dūrordhvagamane duḥkhamiti sādhyānugo na saḥ ।।
pratisādhanarūpasya nānumānasya dūṣaṇam ।
upādhiḥ pratirūpaṃ hi sādhanaṃ tannacāparam ।।
athāpi saśarīratvaṃ cātropādhirna vai bhavet ।
gatitvaṃ yatra dehitvamiti yat sādhanānugam ।।
āgamānanusāritve prasaṅgo ayaṃ yatastataḥ ।
nāpasiddhāntatā doṣaḥ prasaṅge yadi sā bhavet ।
tadaivātiprasaṅgaḥ syānna pasaṅgaḥ kvacid bhavet ।।
lokākāśagatitvaṃ cedupādhiḥ sādhanānugaḥ ।
so apītyukte vadet kiṃ sa tasmād vedodito bhavet ।।
mokṣa evaṃ svayaṃ viṣṇuryadyapīśo hyaśeṣavit ।
cakāra saugatamataṃ mohāyaiva cakāra yat ।।
asurāṇāmayogyānāṃ vedamārge pravartatām ।
ato asurādhikāratvānna grāhyaṃ tanmataṃ kvacit ।।
catuṣprakāraṃ taccoktaṃ śūnyaṃ vijñānamekalam ।
anumeyabahistattvaṃ tathā pratyakṣabāhyagam ।।
iti tatra tu ye śūnyaṃ vadantyajñānamohitaḥ ।
te mokṣaṃ tādṛśaṃ brūyurniśśaṅkaṃ māyino yathā ।।
na kiñcinamuktayavasthāyāmātmātmīyamathāpi vā ।
ekasmin saṃsṛtermukte na kiñcidavaśiṣyate ।।
tatsaṃvṛtyaiva bhedo ayaṃ cetanācetanātmakaḥ ।
dṛśyate saṃvṛterdhvaṃse nirviśeṣaiva śūnyatā ।।
na sattvaṃ naiva cāsattvaṃ śūnyatattvasya vidyate ।
na sukhatvaṃ na duḥkhatvaṃ na viśeṣo api kaścana ।।
nirviśeṣaṃ syayambhātaṃ nirlepamajarāmaram ।
śūnyaṃ tattvamasambādhaṃ nānāsaṃvṛtivarjitam ।।
aśeṣadoṣarahitaṃ manovācāmagocaram ।
mokṣa ityucyate asadbhirnānāsaṃvṛtidūṣitam ।।
saṃsṛtyavasthaṃ vijñeyaṃ saṃvṛtyaiva viśeṣyate ।
sthitayā dhvastayā caiva saṃsṛtirmokṣa ityapi ।।
kecit teṣvanyathā prāhuḥ saṃvṛtyaiva tvanekadhā ।
avacchinnaṃ mahāśūnyaṃ nānānapudgalaśabditam ।।
yasya śūnyaikarasatā jñānāt sā tvapagacchati ।
sa pudgalatvanirmukto mahāśūnyatvameṣyati ।।
saṃvṛtyānyastvavacchinno duḥkhānyanubhavatyalam ।
ityevaṃ māyinaścāhurekajīvatvavādinaḥ ।।
bahujīvamatāśceti māyā teṣāṃ tu saṃvṛtiḥ ।
nirviśeṣatvavācaiva śūnyaṃ brahmaiva no bhidā ।।
saccitsukhādikaṃ caiva kiṃ kuto akhaṇḍavādinaḥ ।
vyāvartyamātrabhedastu vidyate śūnyavādinaḥ ।।
anṛtāderapohaṃ tu svayameva hi manyate ।
nirviśeṣatvato naiva viśeṣo brahmaśūnyayoḥ ।।
prāmāṇyādi ca vedasya phalataḥ samameva hi ।
atattvāvedakaṃ yasmāt pramāṇaṃ tena kathyate ।
atattvāvedakatvaṃ yadaprāmāṇyaṃ satāṃ matam ।।
dīrghabhrāntikarī cet syādatattvāvedakapramā ।
rajjusarpādivijñānādapyādhikyādamānatā ।
syādāgamasyānivartyamahāmohapradatvataḥ ।।
talanailyādivijñānamākāśe mānatāṃvrajet ।
chatrākāratvavijñānaṃcandraprādeśatāmatiḥ ।।
nirbhedatvaṃ tu śūnyasya tenāpyaṅgīkṛtaṃ sadā ।
sattvāsattvādidharmāṇāmabhāva ubhayormataḥ ।।
na hi satpratiyogitvaṃ śūnyatvaṃ tena ceṣyate ।
na ca duḥkhavirodhitvādanyā hyānandateṣyate ।।
māyinā śūnyapakṣe api jñānaṃ jāḍyavirodhi ca ।
dharmaste api na santyeva ko viśeṣastatastayoḥ ।।
etādṛśānāṃ pakṣāṇāṃ dūṣaṇaṃ prabhurā kṛtam ।
svapakṣasādanenaiva nābhāva iti coktitaḥ ।।
ātmābhāve pumarthaḥ ka iṣṭasyātmāvadhiryataḥ ।
yadi nātmāvadhirmokṣo mokṣaḥ syād ghaṭaśūnyatā ।
kalpitatvād viśeṣāṇāṃ māyino api samaṃ hi tat ।।
dṛśyamāne viśeṣe api yadi cedaviśeṣatā ।
ghaṭābhāvo aviśeṣaḥ syāt pāścātyaścedanāgataḥ ।।
na mokṣo vimato yasmādadeho ghaṭaśūnyatā ।
yathetyukte vadet kiṃ sa yo anumāmātramānakaḥ ।।
na ca māyī vadet tatra pūrvoktenaiva vartmanā ।
amānatvācchrutestasya nacādehatvavādinī ।।
śrutiḥ kācidadehatvamaprākṛtaśarīragā ।
mokṣe bhogaṃ yato brūte jakṣan krīḍanniti śrutiḥ ।।
nirduḥkhatvānna tanmokṣaḥ pratipannaṃ yatheti ca ।
anumādūṣaṇaṃ kiṃ syād vādinoḥ śūnyamāyinoḥ ।।
duḥkhaṃ duḥkhādabhinnatvānmokṣo api syādasaṃśayam ।
bhede sadvaitataiva syādityādyamitadoṣataḥ ।
heyaṃ māyāmatenaiva saha śūnyamataṃ budhaiḥ ।।
evaṃ vijñānavādo api jñānamātraviśeṣataḥ ।
tasyāpi bhaṅguratvādiviśeṣamapahāya hi ।
advaitatāmataṃ sākṣāduktadoṣastato bhavet ।।
kālo na kevalajñānī kālatvāt pratipannavat ।
etayānumayā rodhānna tādṛṅmokṣarūpatā ।।
yadi kālo api netyāha kadeti praśna uttaram ।
kiṃ vakṣyati yadāvasthāṃ vadet sā pakṣatāṃ vrajet ।।
avasthātvāditi hyeva hetuḥ sāpi kadeti ca ।
pṛṣṭe kālaśca vaktavyo nākālatvaṃ tato bhavet ।।
na kāla iti sāmānyaniṣedhe kālagapramā ।
niruṇaddhi vaktavyo nākālatvaṃ tato bhavet ।।
ekajīvatvapakṣe tu kālābhāvādiyaṃ pramā ।
kupitā kālamādāya dvaitamevopapādayet ।।
vimataḥ prapañcavān kālaḥ kālatvāt pratipannavat ।
iti cānyānumaikatvaṃ jīvasya vinivārayet ।।
kālaśabdeśvaraikatvamatānyapyevameva hi ।
nirākṛtāni teṣāṃ ca samatvāt pakṣadoṣayoḥ ।।
jñānaṃ svarasabhaṅgayeva nityasantāmiṣyate ।
bauddhābhyāmaparābhyāṃ tu tatrāpyuktānumā ripuḥ ।।
mokṣo na śuddhavijñānasantānī kālagatvataḥ ।
pratipanno yathetyetadanumānaṃ taduttaram ।।
anumānāni sarvāṇi pratisādhanayogataḥ ।
niṣiddhānyuktabhaṅgayaiva śrutayaścāsmaduktigāḥ ।।
sāṅkhayanaiyāyikādyāśca prāhurmokṣaṃ tu nissukham ।
icchādveṣaprayatnāderapi sarvātmanā layam ।।
tatrāhurnaitadapyatra śobhanaṃ śrutayo yataḥ ।
mahānandaṃ ca bhogaṃ ca niyamena vadanti hi ।।
prākṛtapriyahānistu priyāspṛṣṭiritīryate ।
apriyaṃ pratikūlaṃ tadaviśeṣeṇa śabditam ।।
nāsti hyaprākṛtaṃ duḥkhaṃ sato jīvasya kutracit ।
priyaṃ svarūpamevāsya balānandādivākyataḥ ।।
heyatvādapapriyasyaiva priyahāneraniṣṭhataḥ ।
na samastapriyābhāvo mokṣe prokte tu yujyate ।।
apriyasya svarūpatvamasureṣveva hi śrutam ।
asurā naivamevaṃ ca naivaṃ cākhilamānuṣāḥ ।
ityātmapriyahānāya ko yateta ca buddhimān ।।
sañjñā nāstītyapi hyasya nāmuktajñeyateti hi ।
dharmānucchittimevāsya yato vaktayuttaraśrutiḥ ।।
āśaṅkayāsya jñānahāniṃ maitreyyā mohamāha mām ।
bhavānityuktavatyā hi nāhaṃ mohaṃ vadāmi te ।
ityuktavā yājñavalkyo hi svarūpānāśamūcivān ।।
jñānarūpasya vijñānānāśastannāśa eva yat ।
iti śūnyamatocchittyai punarānandapūrvakān ।
dharmānāhāpyanucchinnāṃstārkikairvinivāritān ।
mātrāsaṃsargamapyāha tathā mādhyandinaśrutiḥ ।।
ācikṣepa mataṃ tacca yasmin na viṣayādanam ।
ghrāṇādibhogābhāvasya tvaniṣṭatvahṛdā śrutiḥ ।।
yenedamakhilaṃ veda vijñātāraṃ svameva ca ।
kena taṃ ca vijānīyādityaniṣṭaṃ hi sarvathā ।।
nākhilajñāpako viṣṇurajñeyo niyamena hi ।
tajjñānārthaṃ hi vedānāmakhilānāṃ pravartanam ।।
pratyakṣāgamātmavijñānāvirodhānubhavādapi ।
na svavijñānitāyāṃ ca virodhaḥ kaścaneyate ।।
kartṛkarmavirodhaśca nityānubhavavirodhataḥ ।
kathameva padaṃ gacched virodho dṛṣṭabādhanam ।।
so aśnute sarvakāmaṃśca kāmānnī kāmarūpyatha ।
ityādiśrutayaścoktamarthameva vadanti hi ।।
asvātantryādivetyuktaṃ na dvaitābhāvataḥ kvacit ।
ātmaivābhūditi hyasmādaviśeṣaprasaṅgataḥ ।।
asvātantryopamābhedabhedeṣviva udīritaḥ ।
śabdatattva iti proktaṃ maitreyyuktottaraṃ ca kim ।।
sukhādidharmahānau tu mukteḥ kiñca prayojanam ।
yadyartho duḥkhahāniḥ syādanarthaḥ sukhanāśanam ।।
tayośca duḥkhahānāddhi sukhanāśo adhiko bhavet ।
prāpyāpi duḥkhaṃ sumahat sukhaleśāptaye janaḥ ।
yatate sukhahānau hi ko mokṣāya yatet pumān ।।
alpācca sukhānāśāddhi bibhetyatitarāṃ janaḥ ।
mahacca duḥkhamāpnoti sukhanāśanivṛttaye ।।
na ca rāganimittaṃ tad vītarāgā api sphuṭam ।
nāradādyāḥ sukhārthāya sahante duḥkhamañjasā ।
yuddhādidarśanaṃ yasmāt suduḥkhenāpi kuvarte ।।
yadendravairocanayorbrahmāstrābhyāṃ sutāpitāḥ ।
api naivājahuryuddharasāt te nāradādayaḥ ।
iti skāndavacastasmāt sukhābhāvasya ko yatet ।।
vimato duḥkhayug yasmāccetanaḥ san sukhojkhitaḥ ।
pratipanno yathetyeva cānumā kena vāryate ।।
sarvaśrutipurāṇeṣu sukhabhāvoktitastathā ।
muktau na grāhyamevaitat sukhābhāvamataṃ budhaiḥ ।।
so anānandād vimuktaḥ sannānandī bhavati sphuṭam ।
nirguṇe brahmaṇi mayi dhārayan viśadaṃ manaḥ ।
paramānandamāpnoti yatra kāmo avasīyate ।।
na viṣṇusadṛśaṃ daivaṃ na mokṣasadṛśaṃ sukham ।
na vedasadṛśaṃ vākyaṃ na varṇo akārasammitaḥ ।।
yatrānandāśca modāśca mudaḥ pramuda āsate ।
kāmasya yatrāptāḥ kāmāstatra māmamṛtaṃ kṛdhi ।।
iti śrutipurāṇāni tatratatra vadanti hi ।
ato mokṣe sukhābhāva iti yatkiñcideva hi ।।
śiraḥkarādyabhāvaśca na muktasya bhavet kvacit ।
śrutayaśca purāṇāni mānamatra bahūni ca ।।
na vartate yatra rajastamastayoḥ sattvaṃ ca miśraṃ na ca kālavikramaḥ ।
na yatra māyā kimutāpare hareranuvratā yatra surāsurārcitāḥ ।।
śyāmāvadātāḥ śatapatralocanāḥ piśaṅgavastrāḥ surucaḥ supeśasaḥ ।
sarve caturbāhava unmiṣanmaṇipravekaniṣkābharaṇāḥ suvarcasaḥ ।।
pravāḷavaiḍūryamṛṇāḷavarcasāṃ parisphuratkuṇḍalamaulimālinām ।
bhrājiṣṇubhiryaḥ parito virājate lasadvimānāvalibhirmahātmanām ।।
vidyotamānapramadottamābhiḥ savidyudabhrāvalibhiryathā nabhaḥ ।
śrīryatra rūpiṇyurugāyapādayoḥ karoti mānaṃ bahudhā vibhūtibhiḥ ।।
ṛcāṃ tvaḥ poṣamāste pupuṣvān gāyatraṃ tvo gāyati śakvarīṣu ।
brahmā tvo vadati jātavidyāṃ yajñasya mātraṃ vimibhīta u tvaḥ ।।
kāmānnarūpī caratītipūrvaśrutyā purāṇoktibhirapyadoṣaḥ ।
dehaḥ svarūpātmaka eva teṣāṃ muktiṃ gatānāmapi ceyate hi ।।
śiraḥkarādyairapi muktibhājo yuktā yataste puruṣā idānīm ।
yathetipūrvā anumāśca jīvasvarūpamaṅgādiyugāpayanti ।।
na brahmarūpatvamamuṣya dehino muktāvapi syāt pramayā kathañcit ।
sa brahmaṇā sahito aśeṣabhogān bhuṅkte tathopetya sukhārṇavaṃ tam ।।
yattat paraṃ jyotirupetya jīvo nijasvarapūtvamavāpya kāmān ।
bhuṅkte sa daivaṃ puruṣottamo aja ātmeti cokto guṇapūrtihetoḥ ।।
setuḥ sa devo akhilamuktibhāgāmutāmṛtasyeṣya iheśitā yat ।
ityādivākyairbhagavadvaśaḥ san bhuṅkte'khilān muktigato api bhogān ।।
kālo apyasau naikyayutaḥ pareṇa jīvasya kālo yata eṣa yadvat ।
ityādikā apyanumāḥ pramāṇaṃ muktau ca jīvasya paratvarodhe ।।
kathaṃ ca yaḥ pūrvamasau na paścād bhavet sa evetyapi yuktimeti ।
yato na dṛṣṭaṃ yadabhūnna pūrvaṃ paścāt tadāseti kutaśca kiñcit ।।
nacaiva muktau tu hareḥ pṛthaktavamaikyaṃ tathā syāditi yuktimeti ।
yato na kutrāpi bhidābhidā ca dṛṣṭā citaścetanayā kutaścit ।।
itthaṃ matāni bhramajāni yasmānmokṣaṃ samuddeśyamapi bhrameṇa ।
vidurna samyag yadapīha laukikāḥ sukhaṃ mama syācca sadeti jānate ।।
audāryamuccāvacaśaktirātmasvarapūdārḍhyaṃ ca nijasvabhāvaḥ ।
svātantryamāpūrṇaviśeṣayogyatā virodhahāniśca caturthapāde ।।
vyavasthitistvaviśeṣaḥ sthitiśca niṣedhasāmānyavidhikriyāṇām ।
vibhaktatā cātvarayaiva siddhirvipakṣasamprāptiviruddhahetavaḥ ।।
suśakyatā śaśvadatiprasiddhivivekavinyāsavicārasañjñāḥ ।
nānāpravṛttiḥ kṛtakṛtyatā ca vipakṣatarkāḥ samatītapāde ।।
mahāphalatvaṃ praviviktatā ca sandhigrahaḥ sādhanamāptakṛtyam ।
viśeṣakāryaṃ kṛtisaṃsthitiśca suyuktayo nirṇayagāḥ svapakṣe ।।
vyāmiśratā kāryakaratvamarthakḷptiḥ sudārḍhyaṃ paratantratā ca ।
samānadharmaḥ kṛtaśeṣatā ca lokopamā pūrvamatānusārāḥ ।।
viśeṣasāmyaśrutirāḍhyatā ca samānalopo mahimā viśeṣaḥ ।
kṛtārthatā śaśvadanupravṛttiḥ siddhāntanirṇītiviśiṣṭahetavaḥ ।।
pradhānavāyustviha vāyunāmā bhūteṣvitiproktagato api yuktayā ।
yasmācchrutau pavate ceti bhūri prokto yato bhūtamānī ca so api ।
mahāmānī tvalpamānī ca yasmāt tacchabdenāpyucyate tena so api ।।
tasmin layaṃ yānti bhūtānyaśeṣakramāvirodhena sa eva viṣṇau ।
indrādīnāṃ tatra layaḥ kramaṃ tu proktaṃ viśeṣādanusṛtya nānyat ।।
tasmādaśeṣā girijāṃ praviśya tayaiva rudraṃ saha tena vāṇīm ।
tayā patiṃ prāpya sahaiva tena layaṃ harau yānti samastajīvāḥ ।।
somastu vārīśayuto aniruddhaṃ viśatyasau kāmamasau ca vāruṇīm ।
sā śeṣadevaṃ sa giraṃ ca saiva vāyuṃ viśatyañja itīha nirṇayaḥ ।।
umāgirīśāvapi bhāratīrāviti sma vāg vedagatā bravīti ।
ahīndrapatnīmahipaṃ viriñcapatnīṃ viriñcaṃ ca vimuktikāle ।।
ta eva yat tatpadamāpnuvanti tatkāla etān samupāsya jīvāḥ ।
brahmatvakāle praviśanti caitānīti sma vāk tādṛśatāmupaiti ।।
sūryo agniyukto gurumāpya tena śakraṃ sahainena suparṇapatnīm ।
tayā suparṇaṃ saha tena vāṇīṃ brahmāṇametadgata eva yāti ।।
indrapraveśastu yadocyate atra tadā hyumetyeva suparṇapatnī ।
uktā suparṇaśca girīśanāmnā tato virodhaśca na kaścanātra ।।
bhṛgvādayo dakṣamavāpya tena prāpyendrametena suparṇapatnīm ।
viśanti ye manavo rājamukhyā manuṃ praviśyātra gatā mahendram ।।
ākāśa urvī ca guruṃ praviśya tenaiva yātaḥ puruhūtadevam ।
sanādayo yatayaḥ kāmameva viśanti śiṣṭā api havyavāham ।।
varṇāśramācāraratā manuṣyā dharmaṃ manuṃ so api sameti kāle ।
tameva sarve pitaraḥ surānugāḥ sarve kuberaṃ sa ca somameva ।।
vimuktikāle praviśantyabhīkṣṇaṃ bhogāṃśca taddehagatāḥ prabhuñjate ।
ānandasuvyaktiramutra teṣāṃ bhavatyataśceṣyata eva nirgatāḥ ।
krīḍanti bhūyaśca samāviśanti tāneva sāyujyamidaṃ vadanti ।।
sāyujyahīnāśca laye tu sarve proktena mārgeṇa viśanti sṛṣṭau ।
bahiśca niryānti tato anyadāpi sāyujyabhājāṃ bhavati praveśaḥ ।।
uktaṃ samastaṃ paramaśrutau hi proktaṃ tu sargakramato viparyayaḥ ।
muktau laye yadvadatho layaśca viparyayeṇetyavadad girāṃ patiḥ ।।
layo yato muktiriyaṃ surāṇāṃ bhogo viśeṣeṇa ca yaṃ vadiṣyati ।
uktaśca bimbapratibimbabhāvaḥ piṅgaśrutāvuktalayānusārataḥ ।।
bimbe layo yanniyataśca muktau cidātmanāṃ tadvaśatā ca sarvadā ।
tejo abhidhāṃ tu śriyamāpya viṣṇumagre tataḥ putratayaiva vāyuḥ ।
āptaḥ prasūtaḥ punareva viṣṇuṃ praviśya muktaḥ praḷaye atra tiṣṭhati ।।
sarve api te muktagaṇā amandasāndraṃ nijānandamaśeṣato api ।
bhuñjanta evāsata īśadehe laye atha sarge bahireva yānti ।।
prayāti dharmaṃ nirṛtistu śakraṃ marudgaṇāḥ pārṣadāstathaiva ।
sarve aniruddhaṃ pṛtanādhipādyāsturaśrutirhītthamiyaṃ vimuktiḥ ।।

।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyane caturthādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

utkrāntamārgaśca vimuktagamyaṃ pādoditam sukramavikramau ca ।
sāntānikaṃ prāptirabhīṣyatā ca saukayarmityanyamatasya tarkāḥ ।।
viśeṣasamprāptirurutvamāptiḥ kramānurāgaḥ kathitānuvṛttiḥ ।
siddhāntanirṇītikarāḥ pratīkaṃ dehādikaṃ tadgatameva ye narāḥ ।।
upāsate te purataḥ samāpnuyurbrahmāṇamasmānmatimāpya viṣṇum ।
prāpsyantyato anye api tamāpya tasmāddhariṃ gatā muktibhājaḥ parānte ।।

।। śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyane caturthādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।

atikramoktiḥ kṛtirarthalābhaḥ parā gatiḥ pāragatistadokaḥ ।
samastakāryaṃ vaśitā ca viśvasambhāvanā yuktayastvanyapakṣe ।।
sāmānyarūpaṃ pratibhānamuktirāścaryatākṛtrimatāstadoṣaḥ ।
viśeṣakḷptiḥ kṛtaniḥśramaśca māhātmyamityeva sunirṇayārthāḥ ।।
ananyabhṛtyatvamihoditabhyastvanyasya bhṛtyatvanivāraṇāya ।
patiṃ yadeṣāmapi viṣṇumāha hyutāmṛtatvasya patitvavāgdhareḥ ।।
ete apicānyādhipatitvayuktā viṣṇvanyacittvena yathā pumāṃsaḥ ।
prasiddhibhājastviti cānumaiva hyabhīṣyasiddhayai bhavatīha niścayāt ।।
muktasvakīyāvarayantṛtāsti muktāvapi brahmapurassarāṇām ।
anena devena tathāmunā ca hīṣye parārvāktanalokināmiti ।।
phalaṃ śrutirjñānata āha muktāvetacca sarvāśubhanāśaliṅgāt ।
lokādhipatyaṃ ca vidhātureva sarvātmanetyāha turaśrutiśca ।
sarve baliṃ devagaṇā vahantītyetacca nānyasya hi yuktimeti ।।
lokā itīhāpi tu lokināṃ vaco lokā iti hyeva ravaḥ prajāsu ।
prayujyate sarvajanaiḥ sadaiva tanmānino lokapadena coktāḥ ।
tadgāstu muktā iha lokaśabdā anyonyanāthā iti paiṅgināṃ śrutiḥ ।।
alokaśabdena vimuktibhājo vācyāḥ padaṃ tādṛgapīha yuktam ।
lokābhidhāścāpi yato hi muktāḥ prakāśarūpāḥ satataṃ ca sarve ।
brahmaiva lokādhipatirvimukto bhavediti prāha turaśrutiśca ।।
naceha vijñānaphalaṃ samuktaṃ lokādhipatyaṃ ravibimbato harau ।
uktaṃ pṛthak tacca puraiva yasmād bhedo amunetyādi ca samyaguktaḥ ।।
tvapratyayaṃ cāpyatihāya naiva rūpeṇa teneti bhavedihārthaḥ ।
bhavatyasāvityaṇuśabdamatra vihāya vākyāni bahūni doṣaḥ ।।
ato jagadvayāpṛtimanta eva brahmādayaḥ pūrṇaguṇāḥ krameṇa ।
amandamānandamajasrameva bhuñjanta ātmīyamajāt samāsate ।।
namo namo aśeṣaviśeṣapūrṇaguṇaikadhāmne puruṣottamāya ।
bhaktānukampādatiśuddhasaṃviddātre anupādhipriyasadguṇātmane ।।
yasya trīṇyuditāni vedavacane rūpāṇi divyānalaṃ baṭ tad darśatamitthameva nihitaṃ devasya bhargo mahat ।
vāyo rāmavaconayaṃ prathamakaṃ pṛkṣo dvitīyaṃ vapurmadhvo yattu tṛtīyametadanumā granthaḥ kṛtaḥ keśave ।।
niḥśeṣadoṣarahitakalyāṇākhilasadguṇa ।
bhūtisvayambhuśarvādivandyaṃ tvāṃ naumi me priyam ।।

।। iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne caturtho adhyāyaḥ ।।
